# Overview

Lumina is a pnpm monorepo project designed as a creator tool to enhance daily consistency for English-speaking micro-creators (1K–50K followers). It streamlines the content creation loop from onboarding and style profiling to idea generation, templated content creation, side-by-side review, and export. The Phase 1 MVP focuses on a rule-based Style Profile, a cloud-based Ideator powered by Claude Haiku 4.5 for generating video ideas with strict constraints, templated content creation, and a side-by-side review process. Lumina supports micro-creators in the US, UK, CA, AU, IN, PH, and NG markets, aiming to validate this core loop.

# User Preferences

I prefer to develop iteratively and see changes frequently. Please ask before making any major architectural changes or introducing new dependencies. I value clear, concise explanations and prefer a functional programming style where appropriate. Do not make changes to files or folders marked as `ARCHIVED` or related to `MONETIZATION` or `POSTING` systems unless explicitly instructed and the associated feature flag is enabled.

# System Architecture

Lumina is a pnpm workspace monorepo built with TypeScript.

**UI/UX Decisions:**
- The mobile application is developed using Expo (React Native).
- The onboarding process is a 3-step flow: region selection, first video import, and two additional imports.
- The post-export review screen reads as a finish line: a single final-video preview, a 3-item confidence strip, an optional 2-action Quick Boost (Smoother flow / Faster hook with Fix → Done ✓ micro-interaction), a friction-free "Made with Lumina" watermark toggle, a primary "Save & Post" CTA, and low-emphasis "Make another version" / "Back to ideas" secondary actions. No before/after comparison, analysis blocks, or technical warnings.
- The post-export flow extends Save & Post into a complete posting loop: a "Just save" secondary path (quieter "Saved ✓ / Post it later" copy with no auto-handoff); a "Save & Post" success block ("Saved ✓ / Ready to post / Takes ~10 seconds") that auto-opens a bottom-sheet platform picker (TikTok / Instagram / Snapchat / Copy only); an inline platform handoff card ("Almost there!" + 2-step guide + caption box + Copy caption / Copy & open {Platform} buttons); real deep links via `expo-linking` with web fallbacks (TikTok `snssdk1233://`, Instagram `instagram://library`, Snapchat `snapchat://`); clipboard writes via `expo-clipboard` on every platform tap; and a return-loop "Posted? / How did it go?" card that surfaces via `AppState`/`useFocusEffect` once the user comes back from a platform deep-link, replacing the two text buttons with Make another version / Back to ideas / View saved videos.
- A 5-question screen biases format distribution, tone, effort, privacy, and hook style based on user input.
- One-tap export to the gallery with an optional "Made with Lumina" watermark.

**Technical Implementations:**
- **Monorepo Structure:** Managed with pnpm workspaces.
- **Node.js:** Version 24.
- **API Framework:** Express 5 interacts with PostgreSQL via Drizzle ORM.
- **Database Conventions:** Additive migrations, versioned registry, immutable primary-key types.
- **LLM Integration:** Claude Haiku 4.5 via Replit AI Integrations for idea generation.
- **Per-Creator Format Distribution:** Rule-based system derives a target mix of four canonical patterns.
- **Idea Core Axis (Phase 1) [FROZEN — do not modify]:** A 120-value `ideaCoreType` axis (12 IdeaCoreFamilies × 10 types) drives selection scoring, within-batch HARD guards (≤2 per family / ≤1 per type / failure_contradiction <40%), and cross-batch regen rescue (≥2 NEW families). The legacy `scriptType` axis remains resolved + persisted as inert telemetry only — it no longer influences scoring or guards.
- **Idea Core Axis (Phase 2 — catalog expansion) [FROZEN — do not modify]:** The scenario pool grew from 25 → 83 entries (additive only — Phase 1 wiring untouched) so the 120-value `ideaCoreType` axis has a family-balanced raw pool to draw from. Per-family default-type targets: 7 each for emotional_loop / failure_contradiction / decision_paralysis / social_friction / physical_betrayal / environmental_chaos / memory_glitch / time_distortion / ritual_disruption / identity_drift / information_asymmetry, 6 for anti_climax. 6 new `SceneObjectTag`s added (`restaurant_table`, `gift_box`, `nightstand`, `weighing_scale`, `umbrella`, `wifi_router`) with `ENV_CLUSTER_BY_TAG` mappings. All 5 side-tables (`VISUAL_ACTION_BY_FAMILY`, `TOPIC_LANE_BY_FAMILY`, `SCRIPT_TYPE_BY_FAMILY`, `IDEA_CORE_TYPE_BY_FAMILY`, `SCENE_OBJECT_TAG_BY_FAMILY`) wired for every new family — no fallback path fires for any new entry. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data). `IDEA_CORE_TYPE_OVERRIDES` intentionally NOT extended (sparse-override pattern preserved; defaults are sufficient). QA: 16-candidate pool now spans 8-10 distinct ideaCoreFamilies per batch (was 5-6 in Phase 1); 3 sequential batches produce 9 distinct families across the run with failure_contradiction staying under 40% in every batch.
- **Hook Template / Scroll-Stopping Upgrade (Phase 3, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 1 `ideaCoreType` axis + Phase 2 83-scenario pool to fix the "hooks read like AI rather than scroll-stopping mid-action thoughts" failure mode. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-HOOK-TEMPLATE-SYSTEM-SCROLL-STOPPING-UPGRADE-Goal-Fix-w_1777529547655.txt`. ZERO schema changes (pure TS data + a new derived score axis on the existing `IdeaScore`). **Catalog growth (76 → 102 entries across the same 12 `HookLanguageStyle`s):** the spec's 9 conceptual categories map onto the existing 12 styles (FRAGMENT → `anti_hook`, DEADPAN/BLUNT → `matter_of_fact`, EMOTIONAL_SPIKE → `confession`, SELF_AWARE/META → `observation`; rest 1:1 — no new style enum values added so the cross-batch novelty axis stays unchanged). 26 new entries are scenario-agnostic (`build: () => "..."`) so they read as raw mid-action thoughts (e.g. `"again. seriously."`, `"still nothing."`, `"9:14pm. still here."`, `"i opened it. then closed it."`) instead of frame-around-a-noun phrasings. `validateHook`'s word-count floor was lowered 3 → 2 specifically to admit these FRAGMENT-style hooks; the other rejection rails (banned prefix / generic filler / voice violation / dangling word / truncation marker / interpolation leak) all still apply, so a 2-word hook only ships if it's intentionally abrupt. **Per-template rigidity + sharpness:** `LanguagePhrasingEntry` extended with two OPTIONAL fields — `rigidityScore?: 1-5` (lower = less reusable across scenarios = better) and `sharpnessScore?: 1-5` (higher = more emotional impact). All 76 pre-existing entries backfilled with hand-audited values; the 26 new entries set both explicitly. `getEntryScores(entry)` helper resolves both fields with default 3/3 when absent — used by both the picker + the scorer so JSONB-cached entries written before Phase 3 still resolve cleanly. **scrollStopScore axis:** new `scrollStopScore: number` (0-10) field on `IdeaScore`, computed by `scoreScrollStop(hook, sourceEntry?)` from intrinsic hook properties (fragment shape, emotional charge, structure break, specificity) PLUS the source `LanguagePhrasingEntry`'s rigidity/sharpness when available. Composition: baseline 0, +3 fragment (≤4 words OR period mid-string), +2 emotional charge (token match OR entry sharpness ≥4), +2 unusual structure (no leading pronoun OR timestamp-leading), +2 not a full sentence, +1 highly specific (digit OR proper noun); −3 entry rigidity ≥4, −2 safe-phrasing prefix (`"i think"` / `"i feel like"` / `"you know when"` / `"kind of"`), −2 over-explained (>12 words), −3 pure abstraction; final `Math.max(0, Math.min(10, raw + 5))`. Folded into `IdeaScore.total` with low weight (`Math.round(scrollStopScore * 0.5)`) — nudges selection without overriding the pre-existing 6-axis scorer that shapes selection today. **PatternMeta wiring:** new optional `sourceLanguagePhrasing?: LanguagePhrasingEntry` field on `PatternMeta`, populated by `assembleCandidate` from the entry the picker returned alongside `index + hook`. RUNTIME-ONLY — the entry's `build` function does NOT survive JSON serialization to the JSONB cache, but `rigidityScore` / `sharpnessScore` / `voiceProfiles` (the JSON-safe subset) DO survive, so `getEntryScores` still resolves correctly on rehydrated entries; readers MUST stick to score-field lookups via `getEntryScores` and never call `.build()`. **Banned-prefix layer (PART 4):** the spec's hard-rejection requirement was already satisfied pre-Phase-3 by `BANNED_HOOK_PREFIXES` + the existing `validateHook` wiring (`the way i` / `why did i` / `why do i` / `i really thought` / `me saying` / `me, ` / `what i said vs what i did`); Phase 3 only verified the upgraded 102-entry pool produces zero banned-prefix hits in shipped batches. **QA (3-batch driver):** 102 entries total ✓ (need ≥100), zero banned-prefix hits across 48 shipped hooks ✓, scrollStopScore mean=9.25 across all candidates ✓ (need ≥5), mean=9.89 across top-3 picked ✓ (need ≥6), 12 distinct `HookLanguageStyle`s across 3 batches ✓ (need ≥4). Spec FRAGMENTs probe `"again. seriously."` / `"still nothing."` / `"immediately no."` / `"9:14pm. still here."` all score 9-10; `"I think this might be a problem someday"` correctly scores 5 (safe-prefix penalty fires).
- **HookIntent Refactor (Phase 4, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 3 102-entry catalog + per-template rigidity/sharpness wiring to introduce a `HookIntent` controller axis (`scroll_stop` / `compulsion` / `relatable`) that sits ABOVE `HookLanguageStyle` and drives both template selection and per-intent scoring. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-REFACTOR-HOOK-SYSTEM-INTRODUCE-HookIntent-Goal-Cleanly-_1777532632693.txt`. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data + new derived score axis on the existing `IdeaScore` + 1 new optional field on `PatternMeta`). **Catalog tagging:** all 102 Phase 3 entries hand-tagged with `hookIntent: HookIntent` (REQUIRED on `LanguagePhrasingEntry`); legacy 15-entry `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_STYLE` catalog (used only by `tryRewrite`) tagged with OPTIONAL `hookIntent?: HookIntent` defaulting to `scroll_stop` via `getEntryIntent` helper. Distribution across the 102-entry pool: scroll_stop=46, compulsion=23, relatable=33 — chosen so each language style supports ≥1 intent without forcing artificial balance. **Generation flow (slot rotation):** `generatePatternCandidates` Cartesian inner loop assigns `assignedIntent = HOOK_INTENTS[slotIndex % 3]` per slot; `assembleCandidate` accepts the assigned intent + threads it to `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing`, which runs an INTENT-FIRST 6-pass discipline (3 passes filtered to entries matching the assigned intent, then 3 fallback passes over ANY-intent entries when intent-matching pool is exhausted; sets `meta.intentFallback = true` on fallback). `meta.hookIntent` is derived from the entry the picker actually returned (NOT `assignedIntent`) so fallbacks surface the real shipped intent. **Per-intent scoring:** new `scoreCompulsion(hook, source?)` (mystery-end words / forward-implication / demonstrative+verb / anti-resolution; baseline +5) and `scoreRelatable(hook, source?)` (first-person opener / specific behavior verb / admission tokens / lowercase-conversational / anti-abstract; baseline +5) added alongside the existing `scoreScrollStop`; `scoreHookIntent(hook, intent, source?)` dispatches by intent. New `hookIntentScore: number` (0-10) field on `IdeaScore` computed via the dispatcher and folded into `total` at `Math.round(hookIntentScore * 0.5)` REPLACING the prior `scrollStopScore * 0.5` fold so scoring stays intent-correct without double-counting. The `scrollStopScore` field STAYS on `IdeaScore` for telemetry (always computed via `scoreScrollStop` regardless of intent) but no longer contributes to `total`. **Batch guards:** within `selectionPenalty` — `-3` per duplicated `hookIntent` in the in-progress pick set (sized between the language-style/voice -2 and archetype -4 levers, matching HookIntent's framing as the controller axis ABOVE language style); `+5` fresh-intent BONUS when batchSoFar.length>0 AND this candidate's intent is not yet in the batch (captures the spec's "Prefer 1 of each" SOFT preference and creates an 8pt swing that overcomes both the typical 2-3pt baseline gap between intent scorers AND the 2pt lower novelty bonus that compulsion candidates accrue from a narrower archetype/lang-style pool); `-100` HARD all-3-same-intent guard fires only when batchSoFar.length===2 AND both prior picks share THIS candidate's intent (overwhelms any plausible base total so the selector ALWAYS prefers a shippable other-intent candidate over a third clone). Intentless candidates (legacy cache reads / Llama / Claude wraps) silently skip both branches. **PatternMeta wiring:** new optional `hookIntent?: HookIntent` + `intentFallback?: boolean` fields on `PatternMeta`, populated by `assembleCandidate` from the entry the picker returned. JSON-safe — both fields survive JSONB cache round-trips. **QA (5-batch driver):** all 4 gates green — pool balanced (each intent in [3,9] per 16-candidate batch), shipped distribution 6/4/5 across 5 batches × 3 picks (all intents ≥3, target met), zero all-same-intent batches (HARD guard fires correctly), per-intent shipped `hookIntentScore` mean = 8.83 / 7.00 / 9.20 (all ≥6 floor). Telemetry: ~50% intent-fallback rate at the picker level reflects the catalog's uneven (style × intent) coverage — acceptable because pool composition still ends up balanced and downstream selection still ships all 3 intents. **Architect-review fixes (post-T005):** two correctness gaps surfaced by code review and patched: (1) the `-100` "hard" all-3-same intent penalty in `selectionPenalty` is a SOFT lever (it only blocks the greedy selector when an other-intent shippable EXISTS in the pool); a true hard guard was missing for the pool-starvation case where all candidates collapse to 1 effective intent. Added guard (h) to `batchGuardsPass` in `hybridIdeator.ts` — for batches of size ≥3, reject when ALL picks contributed an intent AND `new Set(intents).size === 1` (skips legacy/fallback wraps that don't carry `hookIntent` to avoid synthetic rejections). Defense-in-depth so the spec's "no batch of 3 ships with all 3 sharing the same intent" rule holds even under starvation. (2) `tryRewrite` in `ideaScorer.ts` rewrites a hook from a DIFFERENT legacy `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_STYLE` entry but did not update `meta.hookIntent` — rewritten candidates carried STALE intent metadata, causing `scoreHookIntent` to dispatch to the wrong per-intent scorer and the soft/hard intent batch guards to make decisions on a phantom intent. Patched: re-derive via `getEntryIntent(entry)` (defaults to `scroll_stop` for legacy entries without the field, matching first-pick discipline at `assembleCandidate` line 4948 of `patternIdeator.ts`); also clear `intentFallback` since rewrite is its own path and the original picker's fallback telemetry no longer applies. Both fixes preserve the typecheck baseline (8 pre-existing errors, zero new). Other architect findings surfaced as known trade-offs: style-first weave (HookLanguageStyle chosen before intent filter) is acceptable as additive Phase 4 compromise — full spec flow `ideaCoreType → HookIntent → compatible HookLanguageStyle` would require restructuring the Phase 1/2/3 weave (frozen this phase); +5/-3/-100 selector calibration is strong relative to other axis levers (archetype -4, scenarioFamily -3) but is now backed by a real hard guard rather than relied on as a pseudo-hard constraint; per-intent scorers (`scoreCompulsion`, `scoreRelatable`) are directionally coherent but permissive (no curly-apostrophe normalization for `should've`/`didn't`, generic first-person/lowercase admits over-score) — calibration tightening deferred to a follow-up so the structural overlay lands first.
- **Pattern Mapping Layer (Phase 5, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 4 `HookIntent` controller axis to introduce a typed `VideoPattern` axis (12 values: `silent_reaction` / `escalation` / `micro_story` / `before_after` / `pov_internal` / `loop_behavior` / `object_pov` / `delayed_reaction` / `montage_repeat` / `confidence_collapse` / `deadpan_statement` / `cut_before_end`) that sits ABOVE the legacy `idea.pattern: string` and the existing `idea.howToFilm: string` so every shipped idea has a structured filming approach derived from `IdeaCoreFamily × HookIntent`. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-PHASE-5-PATTERN-MAPPING-LAYER-Goal-Make-every-idea-feel_1777536080211.txt`. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data + 2 new optional fields on `PatternMeta` + 1 new optional field on `Idea` zod schema). The legacy `idea.pattern` / `idea.howToFilm` / `idea.structure` strings are UNTOUCHED — Phase 5 is a parallel typed axis that the renderer can adopt incrementally. **Catalog (`PATTERN_DEFS`):** `Record<VideoPattern, VideoPatternDef>` where `VideoPatternDef = { id, beats: string[], pacing: "fast"|"medium"|"slow", cameraStyle: string, typicalDuration: "short"|"medium" }`. All 12 patterns curated with 3-4 directorial beats matching spec examples (silent_reaction → trigger→flat-face→tell→hold; escalation → attempt→worse→worse→fail; before_after → before→cut→after→hold; etc.) so `filmingGuide` derivation is just a beats copy. **`PATTERN_BY_FAMILY`:** `Record<IdeaCoreFamily, readonly VideoPattern[]>` covering ALL 12 families (not just the spec's 8 keys). Spec keys mapped semantically — overthinking↔emotional_loop+decision_paralysis, avoidance↔ritual_disruption, failure_contradiction (exact), absurd_escalation↔environmental_chaos, micro_win↔anti_climax, social_behavior↔social_friction, identity_conflict↔identity_drift, time_distortion (exact). Three families missing from spec (physical_betrayal, information_asymmetry, memory_glitch) curated consistently with their semantics. Every family resolves to 2-3 patterns. **`PATTERN_X_INTENT_COMPAT`:** `Record<HookIntent, readonly VideoPattern[]>` — spec PART 5 verbatim for 10 of 12 patterns; the 2 patterns absent from the spec table (before_after, confidence_collapse) added: before_after → scroll_stop+relatable (visual contrast), confidence_collapse → compulsion+relatable (forward-implication + admission). **Selector (`pickVideoPattern`):** walks family-allowed ∩ intent-compat, ranks candidates by inverse recency (unused patterns boost, recent patterns penalize) with deterministic tie-break, returns `{ pattern, intentFallback }`. On empty intersection, falls back to family-only pool (intent ignored, `intentFallback=true` set on meta). The selector ALWAYS returns a pattern — every candidate ships with a structured filming approach. **Generation flow:** `assembleCandidate` resolves `videoPattern` AFTER `hookIntent` is known via the actual winning entry's intent (`getEntryIntent(sourceLanguagePhrasing)`, NOT `assignedIntent` — mirrors Phase 4 discipline so fallbacks surface the real intent), threads to `meta.videoPattern` + derives `idea.filmingGuide = [...PATTERN_DEFS[pattern].beats]` (shallow-copy so downstream mutations don't corrupt the catalog). `assembleCandidate` accepts an optional `recentVideoPatternsInPool: ReadonlySet<VideoPattern>` parameter; `generatePatternCandidates`'s Cartesian inner loop tracks a per-pool `recentVideoPatterns` Set and feeds it forward so within-pool diversity is partially enforced before selection sees the pool. **Batch guards:** within `selectionPenalty` (ideaScorer.ts) — `-3` per duplicated `videoPattern` in the in-progress pick set (parallel to the Phase 4 within-batch hookIntent dup -3 lever and the within-batch voiceProfile -2 lever, sized matching VideoPattern's framing as a controller axis); `-3` cross-batch when the candidate's videoPattern appeared in the immediate-prior batch (single-tier, no frequent-last-3 stack — within-pool recency in `pickVideoPattern` already gives natural spread, so the cross-batch lever just prevents yesterday's duplicates from re-shipping). New `recentVideoPatterns?: ReadonlySet<VideoPattern>` field added to `NoveltyContext`. Added guard `h2` to `batchGuardsPass` (hybridIdeator.ts) — max 2 picks share `videoPattern` per batch (parallel to the legacy `idea.pattern` guard at hybridIdeator.ts:374 but on the typed Phase-5 axis). Pattern-less candidates (legacy cache reads / Llama / Claude wraps where `meta.videoPattern` is absent) silently abstain from all three levers — the guard never fires against absences. **PatternMeta + Idea wiring:** new optional `videoPattern?: VideoPattern` + `videoPatternIntentFallback?: boolean` fields on `PatternMeta`; new optional `filmingGuide: z.array(z.string()).max(8).optional()` on the `Idea` zod schema (max-8 cap — spec patterns produce 3-4 beats so the cap is generous). Both fields are JSONB-safe and optional so pre-Phase-5 cached entries round-trip cleanly without re-validation failure. **QA (5-batch driver):** all 7 gates green — every picked candidate has non-null `videoPattern` + `filmingGuide` ✓; every pattern ∈ `PATTERN_BY_FAMILY[family]` ✓; every pattern ∈ `PATTERN_X_INTENT_COMPAT[intent]` OR `intentFallback=true` ✓; no batch ships 3-of-same pattern ✓; ≥2 distinct patterns per batch ✓; `filmingGuide` matches the chosen pattern's `PATTERN_DEFS[pattern].beats` exactly ✓; ≥6 distinct patterns across 5 batches × 3 picks (actual 6/12) ✓. Telemetry observation: `before_after` over-represented (5/15 picks) because `ritual_disruption` is a common scenario family in the default pool — calibration tightening (per-pattern fairness in selector recency) deferred as a known trade-off; spec gates pass. Typecheck baseline preserved (7 pre-existing errors, zero new).
- **Hook Template Tuning (Phase 3 follow-up, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 5 `VideoPattern` axis to fix the "hooks repeat the same skeleton with different nouns" failure mode (e.g. `"manage [X] now? hostage situation."` shipping in batches 2, 4, 6 with only the noun swapped). Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-PHASE-3-HOOK-TEMPLATE-TUNING-Cap-formulaic-skeleton-reuse_<phase3-tuning>.txt`. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data + 1 new optional field on `PatternMeta` + 1 new optional field on `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape — both round-trip safely through pre-Phase-3-tuning cache reads). The legacy `LanguagePhrasingEntry` / `assembleCandidate` / `selectionPenalty` shapes are UNTOUCHED structurally — the tuning is a parallel set of OPTIONAL signals layered onto the existing per-intent + selection-layer scorers. **Catalog tagging:** every formulaic `(s) =>` template (templates that take a scenario noun and reuse the same skeleton across many scenarios) hand-tagged with a stable `skeletonId: string` field on `LanguagePhrasingEntry` — 9 skeletons total: `todays_update`, `how_many_days_pretending`, `how_to_avoid_three_steps`, `todays_reminder_wait`, `prep_to_think`, `future_me_vs_current_me` (build fn also rewritten — the original was producing broken sentences), `just_observing_disaster`, `morning_plan_action`, `manage_now_hostage` (typo `its` → `it's` fixed). Truly-generic `() =>` templates (templates that abstract away from the scenario entirely — e.g. `"again. seriously."`, `"still nothing."`) tagged with `genericHook: true` — 7 entries flagged. Both fields OPTIONAL so the other 86 catalog entries (and rehydrated JSONB cache entries written before this phase) round-trip cleanly without re-validation failure. **PatternMeta wiring:** new optional `hookSkeletonId?: string` field on `PatternMeta`, populated by `assembleCandidate` from the entry the picker actually returned (NOT the assigned slot — mirrors Phase 4 `hookIntent` discipline so fallbacks surface the real shipped skeleton). JSON-safe — survives JSONB cache round-trips via the same path as `videoPattern`/`hookIntent`. **Per-intent generic penalty:** `scoreScrollStop` / `scoreCompulsion` / `scoreRelatable` each subtract `-4` from `raw` when `sourceEntry?.genericHook === true` (parallel to the existing `entryRigid` / `entrySharp` reads). Symmetric across all 3 intent scorers because `genericHook` candidates abstract away from the scenario noun, lowering the scroll-stop/compulsion/relatable shape value across the board regardless of which intent is being scored. Sized at -4 (vs the spec's draft -2) because the per-intent score saturates at the `Math.max(0, raw + 5)` clamp — -2 wasn't reliably moving the composite total. **Cross-batch hookSkeleton demotion (3 tiers):** `NoveltyContext` extended with three OPTIONAL `ReadonlySet<string>` fields — `recentHookSkeletons` (immediate-prior batch), `frequentHookSkeletonsLast3` (≥2 of last 3 batches), and `hookSkeletonsAtSessionCap` (≥2 across the FULL visible cache history, not just last-3). The third tier was added mid-tuning after QA showed the every-other-batch repeat pattern (`manage_now_hostage` shipping at batches 2, 4, 6) escapes both `recent` and `last-3-frequent`: at batch-6 selection, batch-5 didn't have it (so `recent` zeroed) and only batch-4 had it within the last-3 window (so `frequentLast3` zeroed too — needs ≥2 hits in 3 batches to fire). `selectionPenalty` cross-batch block applies `-3` for `recent`, `-2` stack for `frequentLast3`, `-8` for `hookSkeletonsAtSessionCap`. The session-cap was sized -8 (vs draft -4) because some formulaic skeletons (notably `manage_now_hostage`) outscore the next compulsion-intent alternative by ~5pt on the composite — -4 was too soft to displace them. **Within-batch hookSkeleton demotion:** within-batch block applies `-3` per duplicated `metaHookSkeletonId(c.meta)` already in `batchSoFar` (parallel to the Phase 5 `videoPattern` -3 lever and the Phase 4 `hookIntent` -3 lever). Skeleton-less candidates (legacy cache reads / Llama / Claude wraps where `meta.hookSkeletonId` is absent) silently abstain from all 4 levers — the lever never fires against absences. **Selection-layer generic demotion:** flat `-3` in `selectionPenalty` (post per-intent score-clamp, in the un-clamped selection-layer space) when `metaSourceLanguagePhrasing(c.meta)?.genericHook === true`. Closes the per-intent saturation ceiling so generic-template hooks reliably lose to scenario-specific phrasings even when their other axes (hookImpact / tension / personalFit) score equally — the per-intent -4 alone wasn't enough because once a generic's intrinsic intent signal goes below 0 the additional demotion has no effect on the composite total. **CachedBatchEntry persistence:** `hookSkeletonId?: string` added to `CachedBatchEntry` shape; `tryParseEntries` tolerantly parses (string-only, drop empty — same shape as `trendId` / `videoPattern`); written into the cache envelope at both write sites (success path + retry path). `buildNoveltyContext` derives all 3 cross-batch sets from the cached envelope: `recentHookSkeletons` from the immediate-prior batch's `hookSkeletonId` field, `frequentHookSkeletonsLast3` via the same compute pattern as `frequentIdeaCoreFamiliesLast3` (≥2 hits across last 3 batches), and `hookSkeletonsAtSessionCap` from a per-skeleton occurrence count over the FULL `priorBatches` array (≥2 hits triggers session-cap inclusion). `buildNoveltyContext` signature extended with new optional 3rd parameter `allBatchesForSessionCap` (defaults to `last3Batches` for backward-compat callers); the production caller passes the full `priorBatches` array so session-cap sees the full session, not just last-3. **QA (10-batch driver):** both gates green — G1 (no `hookSkeletonId` appears >2× across the session) PASS; G2 (generic-template hooks `genericHook=true` appear strictly less often than scenario-specific phrasings) PASS with generic=3 / scenario-specific=10 across 30 shipped hooks. Distribution: 17 skeleton-tagged formulaic + 3 generic + 10 scenario-specific, with no skeleton exceeding 2 occurrences. Typecheck baseline preserved (same 7 pre-existing errors, zero new).
- **Hook Catalog Cleanup + Hardening (Phase 3B, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 3-tuning skeleton-cap + generic-demotion to fix three specific bug classes surfaced by the post-Phase-3 review: (1) grammar-level template breakage (article collisions like `"the the promotion post"`, `"a the mirror"`, "talks about it's 3am"), (2) semantically-incompatible (template, scenario) fits where a fragile skeleton built on a noun whose grammatical type doesn't match (e.g. `noun_third_roommate` requires an object/abstract but received an event/action noun), and (3) verb-form mismatches between templates and `actionShort` (e.g. `"I lied about feel grateful for the birthday wishes"` — template needed gerund but `actionShort` is imperative). Spec source: in-session prompt `qa_phase3b_review.ts`. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data + 1 new required field on `Scenario` + 1 new optional field on `LanguagePhrasingEntry`). The legacy `assembleCandidate` / `selectionPenalty` / `validateHook` shapes are UNTOUCHED structurally. **`validateHook` rails (PART 1, 3 new):** `\b(the|a|an)\s+(the|a|an)\b` regex catches all 9 article-collision cases; repeated-adjacent-word rejector with allowlist `had`,`that` catches the doubled-word class without false-positives on legitimate constructions like `"had had"`; `BANNED_GRAMMAR_BIGRAMS` const list (`"talks about it's"`, `"thinking about it's"`, `"thinks about it's"`, `"about it's 3am"`, `"about it's 2am"`) catches the discovered grammar-bigram failure mode. All three rails apply BEFORE the existing dangling-word / truncation / interpolation-leak rejection rails so the new failures surface as natural picker-walk fallbacks rather than late-stage rejections. **`TopicNounType` axis (PART 2):** new union type `TopicNounType = "object"|"abstract"|"action"|"place"|"event"|"body_state"|"person"` REQUIRED on every `Scenario` (no default — forces hand-tagging via typecheck). All 83 SCENARIOS hand-tagged: object (laptop, water bottle, mirror, phone, etc.), place (gym, library, bedroom, etc.), event (sneeze, meeting, birthday, concert), abstract (compliment, post, group chat, mood), body_state (soreness, hunger, tiredness), action (typing, scrolling, brushing). New optional `allowedNounTypes?: ReadonlyArray<TopicNounType>` field on `LanguagePhrasingEntry`; undefined = "any noun type works" (preserves backward-compat for the 60+ permissive entries and rehydrated JSONB cache reads). All 39 formulaic-skeleton templates with `skeletonId` hand-tagged with deliberate allowlists: `noun_third_roommate` (object, abstract), `noun_villain_origin` (object, abstract, person), `noun_smug` (object, abstract), `at_what_point_admit` (object, abstract, body_state, event), `timestamp_negotiating` (object, abstract, event, body_state), `manage_now_hostage` (object, abstract, event, body_state), `how_many_days_pretending` (object, abstract, event, body_state), `manage_live_together` (object, abstract, body_state), `started_ended_worse` (event, place, action), `started_managing_now_live` (object, abstract, body_state), `how_to_avoid_three_steps` (object, place, person), `planner_vs_version_me` (object, abstract, place, body_state), `afternoon_louder` (object, abstract, body_state, event), etc. 3 templates whose `build` reads `realityShort`/`actionShort` (not `topicNoun`) intentionally left untagged since their phrasing is noun-type-agnostic (`todays_update`, `nothing_changed_reality`, `morning_plan_action`). The 3 instruction-shape templates that DO consume `topicNoun` (`how_to_avoid_three_steps`, `pro_tip_skip`, `tutorial_ignore`) are tagged with the conservative `["object","place","event","person"]` allowlist post-architect-review — they read awkwardly with `body_state`/`abstract`/`action` nouns (e.g. "skip the soreness today", "skip the typing dots today" don't parse as something a user can deliberately not-do). **Picker integration (PART 3):** `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk()` extended with one new gate inserted AFTER the existing `voicePred` filter and BEFORE `entry.build(scenario)`: `if (entry.allowedNounTypes !== undefined && !entry.allowedNounTypes.includes(scenario.topicNounType)) continue;`. Skip-before-build is critical — the prior pattern would have called `build()` then thrown the result away after `validateHook` rejection, wasting a slot in the seed-rotated walk. Backward-compat: undefined `allowedNounTypes` always passes through, so the dead-code legacy `pickValidatedPhrasing` path (only `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing` is wired) and all permissive entries are unaffected. **Specific template fixes (PART 4):** 5 double-article templates rewritten — `"everybody has a ${topicNoun}"` → `"everybody has ${topicNoun}"` (topicNoun already includes article), `"planner vs version me on a ${topicNoun}"` → `"planner me vs actual me on ${topicNoun}"`, `"the ${topicNoun} is smug about a ${X}"` → `"the ${topicNoun} is smug about today, frankly"`, `"3pm and the ${topicNoun}"` → `"3pm and ${topicNoun}"`, `"ate the afternoon a ${topicNoun}"` rewrites. Plus 1 verb-form fix surfaced by post-T006 QA: `"I lied about ${actionShort}"` → `"I claimed I'd ${actionShort}, frankly"` (actionShort is imperative form like `"feel grateful for the birthday wishes"`; "I claimed I'd" reads natural with imperative, "I lied about" needed gerund). **QA (10-batch driver):** all targets green — 0 grammar bugs (article-collision / repeated-word / banned-bigram regex sweep over all 30 shipped hooks returns empty), 0 composition suspects (fragile noun-template fit regex returns empty), 19 skeleton-tagged formulaic + 4 generic + 7 scenario-specific (no skeleton exceeds 2 occurrences across the session, matching Phase 3-tuning's session-cap), 26 distinct scenario families across 30 picks, intent distribution 11/10/9 across the 3 intents. Typecheck baseline preserved (same 8 pre-existing errors in `ideaGen.ts` / `trendCatalog.ts` / `ideator.ts` / `styleProfile.ts`, zero new). Phase 3 (commit c338c8d) and Phase 5 frozen — no scoring / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Hook Catalog Skeleton-Tag Completion (Phase 3C, additive overlay):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 3B `TopicNounType` axis + picker noun-type gate to fix the "tagged-but-uncapped" failure mode surfaced by post-Phase-3B QA: a 4-batch real-API curl sweep showed `"I am totally fine about X"` shipping 4×, `"introducing: X again, shockingly"` 2×, `"still avoiding X, posting instead"` 2×, `"X taking notes about my life again"` 2× — all formulaic skeletons that EXISTING Phase 3-tuning session-cap (max 2× per session) and tiered cross-batch penalty levers (`recentHookSkeletons` -3, `frequentHookSkeletonsLast3` -2, `hookSkeletonsAtSessionCap` -8) were architected to demote, but couldn't fire on because the underlying catalog entries had no `skeletonId` tag. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS catalog tagging + 1 new optional field on `HookPhrasingEntry` + 1 new noun-type gate inside `tryRewrite`). The legacy `assembleCandidate` / `selectionPenalty` / `validateHook` / `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing` shapes are UNTOUCHED structurally — Phase 3C is a parallel set of OPTIONAL signals layered onto the same scoring + cache axes Phase 3-tuning already wired. **Catalog audit:** all 29 untagged formulaic `(s) =>` topicNoun-consuming templates surfaced — 8 in legacy `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_STYLE` (only consumed by `tryRewrite` rewriter; the sibling `pickValidatedPhrasing` picker is dead code per `rg` audit), 21 in live `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_LANGUAGE_STYLE` (consumed by `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing`). Initial Python sweep caught 27 single-line `build:` arrow-fn entries; architect review surfaced 2 additional multi-line `build:` arrow-fn entries (`looked_did_nothing_scrolling`, `started_small_no_longer`) where the build expression spans a newline between `=>` and the backtick literal — those were tagged in a follow-up pass with the same skeleton + allowedNounTypes discipline. Final coverage: a multi-line-aware regex audit confirms 69 total topicNoun-consuming entries across both catalogs and 0 remaining untagged. **Bulk skeletonId tagging (PART 2):** every untagged formulaic template hand-assigned a stable `skeletonId` matching its phrasing skeleton — legacy 8: `way_i_avoid_sport`, `way_i_gaslight_about`, `refusing_to_deal`, `why_lie_about`, `why_expect_anything`, `totally_fine_about`, `planned_to_handle`, `lying_about_again`; live 21: `keep_pretending_doesnt_exist`, `avoiding_posting`, `whole_personality`, `always_one_never_deal`, `everybody_has_avoiding`, `same_loop_with`, `personality_trait_apparently`, `quietly_losing_to`, `is_it_really_still_about`, `open_stare_close`, `walks_past_nods`, `stood_near_ghost`, `life_notes_again`, `anyway_noun`, `not_great_with_today`, `so_noun`, `here_we_are_with`, `whole_post_noun`, `quiet_kind_of_nothing`, `introducing_again`, `looked_did_nothing_scrolling`, `started_small_no_longer`. Total formulaic skeletons in the cross-batch axis is now 39 (Phase 3-tuning) + 29 (Phase 3C) = 68 distinct ids the cap can demote against. **`HookPhrasingEntry.allowedNounTypes` field (PART 4 — symmetry with Phase 3B `LanguagePhrasingEntry.allowedNounTypes`):** new optional `allowedNounTypes?: ReadonlyArray<TopicNounType>` field on `HookPhrasingEntry` matching the Phase 3B field shape, with identical semantics: undefined = "any noun type works" (preserves backward-compat for permissive entries and rehydrated cache). Restrictive allowlists hand-assigned per template grammar — `totally_fine_about` + `lying_about_again` ["abstract","body_state","object","place"] (excludes event/action/person — "I am totally fine about the meeting/sneeze/concert" reads false-tone-deaf because the speaker can't denial-loop a discrete event the same way they denial-loop a chronic condition); `avoiding_posting` + `everybody_has_avoiding` + `quiet_kind_of_nothing` ["object","place","event","action","abstract"] (broad — only excludes body_state and person which don't combine with "avoiding/quiet kind of nothing"); `whole_personality` + `personality_trait_apparently` ["object","abstract","action"] (a person noun would create "the friend is my whole personality" which mis-frames; place/event read awkward); `quietly_losing_to` ["event","body_state","abstract","object"] (place/person/action don't fit the "losing to" framing); `way_i_avoid_sport` + `why_expect_anything` + `walks_past_nods` ["place","object","person"] / ["object","place","event","person"] / ["place","object","person"]; `open_stare_close` ["object"] (you can only stare-then-close objects); `stood_near_ghost` ["place","object"]; `life_notes_again` ["object","abstract","place"]; `gaslight_about` ["abstract","event","body_state","place"]. The 12 truly-permissive short anti-hook fragments (`anyway_noun`, `so_noun`, `here_we_are_with`, `whole_post_noun`, `not_great_with_today`, `introducing_again`, `refusing_to_deal`, `why_lie_about`, `planned_to_handle`, `keep_pretending_doesnt_exist`, `always_one_never_deal`, `same_loop_with`, `is_it_really_still_about`) intentionally left without an `allowedNounTypes` allowlist — their phrasings work across every noun type and the rigidity/sharpness scores already discipline their pick rate. **`tryRewrite` noun-type gate (PART 3, mirror of Phase 3B picker gate):** `tryRewrite` rewriter loop in `ideaScorer.ts` extended with one new gate inserted BEFORE `entry.build(scenario)` (mirroring the gate added to `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk()` in Phase 3B): `if (entry.allowedNounTypes !== undefined && !entry.allowedNounTypes.includes(scenario.topicNounType)) continue;`. Skip-before-build is critical — the prior pattern would have called `build()` then thrown the result away after `validateHook` rejection, wasting a slot in the seed-rotated walk. Backward-compat: undefined `allowedNounTypes` always passes through; `tryRewrite`'s existing `entry.skeletonId → nextMeta.hookSkeletonId` propagation (Phase 3-tuning) means tagging the legacy entries auto-activates the cap with no further wiring. **QA (10-batch real-API curl sweep against `POST /api/ideator/generate`):** noun-fit gate empirically firing — 0 grammar-bug regex hits across 30 shipped hooks (article-collision / repeated-word / banned-bigram), 0 noun-fit violations (zero `totally_fine_about` + event-noun pairs across the 12 ships of that template, confirming the `["abstract","body_state","object","place"]` allowlist is filtering at the rewriter), 0 typecheck regressions (same 8 pre-existing baseline errors in `ideaGen.ts` / `trendCatalog.ts` / `ideator.ts` / `styleProfile.ts`). The cross-batch session-cap was not visibly firing across the test sweep because each `regenerate: true` curl call is treated as an independent session in this isolated test setup — in real production sessions where the cache accumulates, the now-tagged 27 skeletons will participate in all three `selectionPenalty` tiers (-3 within-batch dup / -3 immediate-prior + -2 frequent-last-3 / -8 session-cap-≥2) identically to the 39 pre-existing Phase 3-tuning tags. Phase 3 (commit c338c8d), Phase 3B (commit 02dfd507), Phase 4, and Phase 5 frozen — no scoring / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Phase 3D Bug-Fix Pass (additive, narrow scope):** Layered on top of the now-frozen Phase 3C skeleton-tag completion to fix three production bugs surfaced by a real-session 8-batch QA run. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS runtime in 4 files: `ideaScorer.ts`, `hybridIdeator.ts`, `patternIdeator.ts`, `ideaGen.ts`). No scoring philosophy changes, no catalog expansion, no Phase 5 changes. **Bug A — `tryRewrite` skeleton cap bypass:** the rewriter walked the full legacy `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_STYLE` catalog and could re-pick a skeleton that the cross-batch session-cap was actively trying to demote (`totally_fine_about` shipping in every batch even though the scorer's -8 session-cap was firing — the bypass happened upstream at the candidate-pool generation step, before the scorer could see it). Fix: added optional `recentHookSkeletons?: ReadonlySet<string>` parameter to `tryRewrite`, with a two-pass entry walk — pass 1 SKIPS entries whose `entry.skeletonId` is in the hot-skeleton set; pass 2 falls back to the prior any-entry behavior when pass 1 starves (preserves the "always return something rewritten if a valid candidate exists" contract that downstream pool-merging relies on). Both call sites (~L1372, ~L1400 in `ideaScorer.ts`) thread `input.recentHookSkeletons` from the existing `FilterAndRescoreInput` field. Acceptance: across multiple 8-batch runs, `totally_fine_about` no longer ships in every batch (typically 2-3 of 8 vs 8 of 8 pre-fix). **Bug B — exact hook string dedup:** the legacy `9:14pm. still here.` static-timestamp template was shipping repeatedly because the entry had no `skeletonId`, so the existing skeleton cap couldn't engage; even after Phase 3C's tagging push there was still a "different code path emits the same exact string" failure mode where two pattern-variation candidates produced byte-identical hooks across batches. Fix in three parts: (1) tagged the `9:14pm. still here.` entry in `patternIdeator.ts` with `skeletonId: "static_timestamp_still_here"` so the cap can fire on it. (2) added `normalizeHookForDedup(hook)` exported helper in `ideaScorer.ts` (lowercase + trim + collapse whitespace + strip trailing `.,!?;:`) — deliberately preserves mid-string punctuation so emoji / dashes / intentional fragmentation (period mid-string) all survive normalization; the static-timestamp template's "two-clause status fragment" shape depends on the mid-string period for its visual identity. (3) added optional `recentHookStrings?: ReadonlySet<string>` field to `NoveltyContext` AND `FilterAndRescoreInput` in `ideaScorer.ts`; populated by `buildNoveltyContext` in `hybridIdeator.ts` (~L1581) from the FULL visible cache history (`allBatchesForSessionCap` parameter — production caller passes the full 5-batch envelope, not just last-3, so the dedup window matches the scorer-side cap window); applied as a HARD `-1000` demotion in `selectionPenalty` (~L2117 in `ideaScorer.ts`) when the candidate's normalized hook matches either the cross-batch set OR the within-batch `batchSoFar` set. The -1000 magnitude is sized to overwhelm any plausible composite total so the selector ALWAYS prefers a fresh-string candidate over a duplicate when one exists; the selector still picks the highest-scored member of a fully-poisoned pool (acceptable starvation behavior). Both `filterAndRescore` call sites in `hybridIdeator.ts` (~L2467 local pool, ~L2538 fallback merge) thread `recentHookSkeletons` + `recentHookStrings` from `noveltyContext`. Acceptance: across multiple 8-batch runs, zero exact-hook repeats. **Bug C — Claude fallback word-count crash guard:** when the Claude fallback returned 3 ideas where every hook exceeded the 10-word ceiling, `callJsonAgent`'s schema validation threw, `recoverPartialIdeas` returned 0 partial recoveries, and the entire `runHybridIdeator` request crashed instead of degrading to the local-only selection. Fix in three parts: (1) added `recoverIdeasWithHookFix(rawText, ...)` + `tryShortenHook(hook)` helpers in `ideaGen.ts` (~L1201) — the hook-fixer parses loose JSON, then for each idea where the hook exceeds 10 words runs a deterministic trim (split on comma/dash, keep the first clause if ≤10 words; otherwise drop that idea entirely). The survivors are `safeParse`'d through the existing `IdeaSchema` so any other validation issue still rejects normally. (2) wired the recovery into `generateIdeas` (~L1054 in `ideaGen.ts`) — when `callJsonAgent` throws AND `recoverPartialIdeas` returns 0, run `recoverIdeasWithHookFix` on the raw text as a last-chance pass before re-throwing. (3) tightened the fallback prompt's hook-length line (~L999 in `ideaGen.ts`) with a JSON-only + drop-long-hooks reminder. The orchestrator-level catch in `runHybridIdeator` (`hybridIdeator.ts`) was already swallowing `generateIdeas` errors and falling back to local-only selection — this change strengthens the per-call recovery so more candidates survive instead of needing the catch. Acceptance: across multiple 8-batch runs (with `usedFallback=true` firing on multiple batches), zero `runHybridIdeator` crashes. **QA verification:** an in-memory non-demo creator was created via a temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase3d` route that ran `runHybridIdeator` 8× with `regenerate=i>0`, computed metrics, and deleted the creator. Multi-run results: 0 exact-hook repeats (Bug B PASS), `totally_fine_about` not in every batch (Bug A PASS), 0 errors with Claude fallback firing (Bug C PASS). The temporary QA route file + both wires in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 (commit c338c8d), Phase 3B (commit 02dfd507), Phase 3C, Phase 4, and Phase 5 frozen — no scoring / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Big Premise + Comedy Compression Layer (Phase 6, additive overlay):** Layered ABOVE the existing Phase 3 hook-template catalog (per spec PART 7 — premises sit ON TOP of templates, not replacing them) to fix the "hooks read like accurate observations but never like jokes" failure mode. Spec source: in-session prompt — 5 comedic premise styles (`SELF_ROAST`, `ABSURD_METAPHOR`, `CONTRAST_DUALITY`, `OVER_DRAMATIZATION`, `IDENTITY_FRAMING`), each a scenario-AGNOSTIC complete-hook string ≤10 words, treated as a distinct candidate kind that flows through the existing seed-rotated picker but bypasses the legacy scenario-specific scoring rails it was never designed for. ZERO schema/migration changes (pure TS data — 2 new optional fields on `LanguagePhrasingEntry`, 2 new optional fields on `PatternMeta`, 1 new optional field on `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape, 1 new optional field on `NoveltyContext`; all round-trip safely through pre-Phase-6 cache reads). NO scoring philosophy changes (`scoreIdea` itself is untouched), NO `HookIntent`/Phase 5 changes, NO catalog reduction. Part 4 boost/penalty (premise-specific scoring lift) deferred per spec — the structural-only flow ships standalone. **Catalog growth (29 new entries):** `BigPremiseStyle = "self_roast"|"absurd_metaphor"|"contrast_duality"|"over_dramatization"|"identity_framing"` union + `BIG_PREMISE_STYLES` const array exported from `patternIdeator.ts`. ~6 entries per style (29 total) added to `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_LANGUAGE_STYLE` and distributed across `confession`/`observation`/`matter_of_fact`/`anti_hook` language-style buckets so the existing seed-rotated picker can reach them. Each premise entry: `build: () => "..."` (scenario-agnostic — never consumes `scenario.topicNoun`), `bigPremise: true`, `premiseStyle: <one of 5>`, hand-assigned `hookIntent`/`voiceProfiles`, `rigidityScore: 1` (lowest — premises are unique not reusable), `sharpnessScore: 5` (highest — premises punch). Intentionally NO `genericHook` flag (premises are sharp, not flat) and NO `skeletonId` (each premise IS its own joke, not a noun-swap skeleton — no within-skeleton reuse risk). All 29 entries pass `validateHook` (≤10 words, no banned prefixes, no doubled articles). **`assembleCandidate` metadata threading + cache persistence:** `meta.usedBigPremise: boolean` + `meta.bigPremiseStyle?: BigPremiseStyle` populated from the picker's actually-returned entry (NOT the assigned slot — mirrors Phase 4 `hookIntent` discipline so fallbacks surface the real shipped style). Both fields added to `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape; `tryParseEntries` tolerantly parses `bigPremiseStyle` (validates against `BIG_PREMISE_STYLES`, drops unknown values for forward-compat). Written into the cache envelope at both write sites (success path + retry path). **`validateBigPremise(hook)` (PART 2 + PART 3 + PART 4-penalty rules):** new validator gate enforcing ≤10 words, no filler list (`just`, `kind of`, `really`, `basically`, `literally`, `actually`, `pretty much`, `sort of`), no boring "i did X again" / "i (was )?thinking about" patterns, no naked observation openers (`i think`, `i feel like`, `you know when`). Wired into `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk()` AFTER the existing `validateHook` gate — when `entry.bigPremise === true`, the picker requires BOTH validators to pass before returning. Existing template entries skip this gate (the `entry.bigPremise === true` predicate is the trigger), so the legacy flow is untouched. **Cross-batch premise-style novelty:** new optional `recentBigPremiseStyles?: ReadonlySet<BigPremiseStyle>` field on `NoveltyContext` (additive, undefined = no signal). `buildNoveltyContext` derives the set from `last3Batches`'s `e.bigPremiseStyle`. `selectionPenalty` extended with two new levers — within-batch `-3` per duplicated `meta.bigPremiseStyle` already in `batchSoFar`, cross-batch `-2` when the candidate's style is in `recentBigPremiseStyles`. Both sized SMALLER than the skeleton tiers (-3/-8) because each premise entry is intrinsically unique (no template-noun-swap reuse risk), so the goal is style-distribution spread, not duplicate-suppression. Premise-less candidates (legacy template picks where `meta.bigPremiseStyle` is absent) silently abstain from both levers. **Structural plumbing fixes:** two structural changes in `ideaScorer.ts` to make premises survive the legacy filter pipeline that was designed for scenario-specific hooks: (1) `tryRewrite` early-returns `null` when `meta.usedBigPremise === true` — premises are scenario-AGNOSTIC complete jokes, so rewriting one to a scenario-bound legacy template would defeat the feature (premises are immune to the rewrite path entirely); (2) `tryRewrite` also clears `usedBigPremise`/`bigPremiseStyle` on the rewritten meta (mirrors the existing `sourceLanguagePhrasing`/`skeletonId`/`intentFallback` clears) so a legacy entry post-rewrite is correctly typed as non-premise; (3) `filterAndRescore` hard floor at the `score.hookImpact === 0` check now exempts premise candidates ONLY from that arm — the `tension`/`filmability` arms still apply. The exemption is required because `scoreHookImpact` requires TENSION_MARKERS or scenario-specific words (`3am`/`coffee`/`gym`/etc) which scenario-AGNOSTIC premises never contain by design; without the exemption, every premise scores `hookImpact = 0` legitimately and gets rejected. The deferred Part 4 boost would have lifted them implicitly — the exemption is the minimal structural plumbing needed until Part 4 ships. **QA verification (3-batch real-pipeline driver):** all gates green — 5 premises shipped across 3 batches (avg 1.67 per batch ≥1 spec target), max 7 words per premise (≤10 spec cap), 0 within-batch style duplicates, 0 cross-batch style repeats, 0 batches with 3-of-same-style, 0 crashes. Per-style distribution across the test sweep: `self_roast` 1, `absurd_metaphor` 1, `contrast_duality` 1, `over_dramatization` 1, `identity_framing` 1 (all 5 styles appeared). Cold-start batch 0 ships 0 premises because the seed-rotated picker hits offset 0 deterministically and the premises are placed past the legacy entries in the catalog ordering — acceptable per acceptance criterion (average ≥1, not minimum ≥1). The temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase6` route file + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 (commit c338c8d), Phase 3B (commit 02dfd507), Phase 3C, Phase 3D, Phase 4, and Phase 5 frozen — no scoring / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes, no DB schema changes.
- **PremiseStyle Engine (Phase 6 EXPANSION, additive layer on the 5-bucket BigPremiseStyle infra):** Layered ON TOP of the just-shipped Phase 6 BigPremiseStyle layer to expand the comedic vocabulary from 5 broad buckets to 50 fine-grained styles WITHOUT changing any of the upstream picker/cache/validator/scoring infra. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-PHASE-6-PREMISE-STYLE-ENGINE-...1777580367516.txt`. Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO scoring philosophy / Phase 5 / HookIntent changes; no template-catalog reductions. **Catalog (`patternIdeator.ts`):** new `PremiseStyleId` union of 50 ids (`cosmic_overreaction`, `gen_z_collapse`, `whiplash_wisdom`, `expectation_collapse`, `pattern_exposure`, `duality_clash`, `overdramatic_reframe`, `delusion_spiral`, `chaos_confession`, `pain_point_precision`, `everyday_armageddon`, `group_chat_guilt`, `main_character_meltdown`, `plant_parent_psychosis`, `self_destruction_speedrun`, … 35 more spanning identity / contrast / over-dramatization / absurd-metaphor / self-roast clusters), `PremiseStyleDef` type `{label, purpose, transformLogic[], worksBestWith[], hookShapes[], examples[], parentBucket: BigPremiseStyle}`, `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS: Record<PremiseStyleId, PremiseStyleDef>` literal with all 50 entries — each maps to ONE of the 5 existing parent buckets via `parentBucket` so all upstream `bigPremise: true` plumbing (validator gate, hard-floor exemption, tryRewrite skip, cross-batch novelty) is reused unchanged. `PREMISE_STYLE_LABELS: Record<PremiseStyleId, string>` for telemetry; `getPremiseStyleParent(id)` + tolerant `parsePremiseStyleId(unknown)` helpers exported. **Entry generation (`buildPremiseEntriesFromDefs`):** programmatic builder reads `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS[id].examples` and yields one `LanguagePhrasingEntry` per example with `bigPremise: true`, `premiseStyle: def.parentBucket`, `premiseStyleId: id`, `rigidityScore: 1`, `sharpnessScore: 5`. Spread-distributed across 4 hookLanguageStyle buckets (~99 total entries: confession 17 × relatable, observation 11 × compulsion, matter_of_fact 11 × scroll_stop, anti_hook 11 × scroll_stop) so the existing seed-rotated picker reaches them without any new picker logic. **Catalog quality:** every example pre-validated against `validateHook` + `validateBigPremise` — 7 initial broken examples (6 trailing-word "me"/"is" → DANGLING, 1 "main character energy" → VOICE_VIOLATION) reworded in catalog source so the QA driver reports 99/99 = 100% catalog pass-rate (zero silent picker rejections). **Metadata thread:** `premiseStyleId?: PremiseStyleId` + `premiseStyleLabel?: string` added to `PatternMeta` (additive, optional, undefined for legacy/Llama/Claude paths). `assembleCandidate` populates both via `PREMISE_STYLE_LABELS` lookup when the picked entry carries a `premiseStyleId`. `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape gains `premiseStyleId?: PremiseStyleId`; `tryParseEntries` tolerantly parses via `parsePremiseStyleId` (drops unknown values for forward-compat); written at BOTH cache write sites (success path + retry path). `tryRewrite`'s rewrite-clear path also clears `premiseStyleId`/`premiseStyleLabel` on rewritten meta so a legacy entry post-rewrite isn't mis-tagged. **Novelty levers (fine-grained, layered on top of bucket-level levers):** `recentPremiseStyleIds?: ReadonlySet<PremiseStyleId>` added to `NoveltyContext` (additive, undefined = no signal); `buildNoveltyContext` derives the set from `last3Batches` per-entry `e.premiseStyleId`. `selectionPenalty` extended with two new fine-grained levers — within-batch `-8` per duplicated `meta.premiseStyleId` already in `batchSoFar` (sized LARGER than the bucket-level `-3` because the spec hard rule "no same PremiseStyle twice in one batch" is at the FINE-GRAINED id level, not the bucket level), cross-batch `-2` when the candidate's id is in `recentPremiseStyleIds`. Both levers silently abstain when `meta.premiseStyleId` is absent (legacy template / Llama / Claude / pre-EXPANSION premise picks). **QA verification (10-batch real-pipeline driver, deleted post-pass):** every catalog example passes both validators (99/99 = 100%), 30 hooks shipped across 10 batches, 0 broken hooks (`validateHook` post-shipping), 0 within-batch fine-grained `premiseStyleId` duplicates (acceptance HARD rule), 0 within-batch dups under regenerate stress, average word count 7.23 (well within ≤10 cap). **Premise-share gap acknowledged + carried forward:** observed 30% premise-share vs spec aspirational target of 50%+. The 50% target is gated on the spec's deferred Part 4 ("PremiseStyle should influence hook generation BEFORE templates" — i.e. the picker should *prefer* premise entries over template entries when both exist), which is explicitly OUT OF SCOPE for this additive-only EXPANSION work (would require a scoring philosophy change, ruled out by the EXPANSION guardrail "5-bucket BigPremiseStyle infra reused unchanged"). The 30% number reflects the existing Phase 6 picker's organic premise share with no premise-favoring bias — Phase 6 EXPANSION's job was vocabulary expansion + fine-grained novelty, both shipped clean. Part 4 (premise-first selection bias) carried forward as deferred follow-up. **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase6expansion` route file + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; the temporary `export` keyword on `readBatchHistory` (used by the QA driver to read per-batch metadata not surfaced on the public `Idea` shape) was reverted to `function`; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 base all frozen — no scoring / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Premise-First Selection + Output Line Optimization (Phase 6C, additive overlay on Phase 6 EXPANSION):** Layered on Phase 6 EXPANSION to deliver Part 4 (premise-first selection bias) plus a comedy-compression / caption-like rejection rail so shipped hooks are short / simple / funny / instantly understandable, AND to constrain Llama to premise-preserving polish only. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-PHASE-6C-PREMISE-FIRST-SELECTION-OUTPUT-LINE-OPTIMIZATI_1777586447218.txt`. Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO scoring philosophy / Phase 5 / HookIntent changes; reuses the Phase 6 EXPANSION 99-entry premise catalog + 50-id PremiseStyleId axis untouched. **Premise-first picker walk (`pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** the seed-rotated single-pass walk became a TWO-PASS walk gated by a deterministic 100-bucket hash (`PREMISE_FIRST_BUCKET_PCT = 85`) — Pass 1 only considers entries with `bigPremise === true` (in same seed-rotated order; failures naturally drop to Pass 2); Pass 2 falls back to all entries (legacy templates) only when Pass 1 yielded nothing OR when the bucket lands in the 15% legacy-rhythm slice (mirrors the trend-cap selector's hash style for cache-replay determinism). The 15% legacy-rhythm slice exists explicitly per spec ("keep 10-20% legacy") so the engine never feels like one premise note on repeat. **Selector preference (`selectionPenalty`, `ideaScorer.ts`):** new `PREMISE_PREFERENCE_BONUS = +3` applied unconditionally when `meta.usedBigPremise === true` (positive lever, NOT a hard guard, so legacy still wins on superior quality); SYMMETRIC `+2 boost` (positive twin to the existing -2 cross-batch demote) when candidate's `premiseStyleId` is NOT in `recentPremiseStyleIds` AND `recentPremiseStyleIds.size > 0` (first-batch cold-start abstains so the boost never shapes a fresh creator's first run). **Output-line compression + caption-like / AI-feel rejection (`compressHook` + `validateOutputLine`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** new `compressHook(hook)` is a pure idempotent transform that strips leading filler words (`currently | kind of | sort of | pretty much | basically | literally | actually | really | just`), softeners (`a little bit | i think | i feel like | you know`), trailing redundancies (`today | again` when already implied), double articles + multi-clause caption-like splits — never returns empty + abstains when the compressed length would fall under the 3-word floor. New `validateOutputLine` rail (layered AFTER `validateHook` + `validateBigPremise`) rejects caption-like (3+ sentences OR sentence-starting-capitalized followed by period-then-capital), too-many-clauses (>2 commas OR >2 of `and|but|or|because`), over-clever (`paradox | conundrum | juxtaposition | irony | oxymoron`), AI-feel patterns (`it turns out that | as it happens | interestingly enough | the truth is | ultimately`). Wired into the picker walk as: `compressHook(candidate)` first, then the COMPRESSED string is `validateOutputLine`-checked; failure falls through to next entry (NOT a rewrite — picker walks). **Within-batch HARD premiseStyleId guard (`hybridIdeator.ts`):** in `selectWithNovelty` + `exhaustiveReselect`, a candidate whose `meta.premiseStyleId` is already shipped in the current batch is HARD-rejected (in addition to the existing -8 selection penalty which stays as defense-in-depth for greedy ordering). HARD-guarantee: 0 same fine-grained `premiseStyleId` ships twice in any batch; the bucket-level `parentBucket` is unaffected (still soft-guided by the -3 lever). **Llama premise-preserving polish constraint (`llamaHookMutator.ts`):** when input candidate has `meta.usedBigPremise === true`, the system prompt receives a POLISH-only addendum ("PRESERVE the premise/joke. Make it shorter and more natural. Allowed: drop filler, fix awkward phrasing, preserve slang/lowercase/fragments. Forbidden: change the joke, add new scenes/objects/people, professionalize, make it more clever.") AND a new `polish_changed_premise` validator rejects mutations whose Levenshtein distance from the original > 0.4 × original.length OR that introduce a new content noun not in the original (the existing `scene_drift` validator covers a subset; the polish gate is stricter). The pre-existing quality-first override stays unchanged (rewrite only ships if `hookImpact > original` OR `personalFit > original` OR `total ≥ original + 1`). Non-premise candidates (legacy templates) keep the existing Llama behavior unchanged. **QA verification (`POST /api/_qa/phase6c`, 10-batch real-pipeline driver, deleted post-validation):** sentinel non-demo creator (`authUserId="qa:phase6c"`), envelope reset per invocation, count=3, `regenerate=i>0`. Canonical run at spec'd `PREMISE_FIRST_BUCKET_PCT=85` shipped 30 hooks across 10 batches: **premiseShipped=18 / 30 = 60% (✓ doubled vs Phase 6 EXPANSION's 30% baseline; below the spec's 80-90% HARD gate)**, legacyShipped=12 / 30 = 40%, **avgWordCount=6.63 (✓ in the 6-10 HARD range)**, wordCountMin=4 / wordCountMax=9, **withinBatchPremiseStyleDups=0 (✓ HARD guard verified)**, **0 broken/dangling hooks across the 30 shipped lines (✓ HARD)**, no Llama mutations introduced new content nouns on premise hooks (HARD — Llama path inactive without OpenRouter key in QA env, polish validator unit-verified). **Premise-share gap acknowledged + carried forward:** the 60% lands in the same structural ceiling Phase 6 EXPANSION hit at 30% — at the spec's `count=3` ship size the candidate pool exposes ~2-3 unique `premiseStyleId`s per batch (Cartesian weave at `target=Math.max(12, Math.min(input.count ?? 16, 20))` → target=12 with count=3), so once slots 1-2 ship two distinct premise styles the HARD within-batch dup guard exhausts the fresh-style premise set and slot 3 falls through to the dominant legacy templates ("I am totally fine about ${topicNoun}" / "I really planned to handle ${topicNoun}") which carry no `genericHook=true` demotion. Bumping `PREMISE_FIRST_BUCKET_PCT` 85→95 only moved the share 60%→67% (gained 1 premise across 30 slots) — confirming the bottleneck is candidate-pool premise-style diversity, not the picker walk gate. Closing the final 20pp gap requires either bumping the candidate-pool target floor (touches core production performance, OUT OF SCOPE for Phase 6C per the spec guardrail "ZERO schema changes; reuses Phase 6 EXPANSION infra") OR expanding per-(scenario, hookLanguageStyle) premise-style coverage in the catalog — both deferred to a future phase (Phase 6D / Phase 7). The 60% measurement still represents a 2× lift over Phase 6 EXPANSION's organic 30% baseline; all other HARD gates pass; selection levers + output-line compression + Llama polish constraint are wired and verified working as designed. **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase6c` route file + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 / catalog-removal changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Premise Execution Expansion (Phase 6D, additive overlay on Phase 6C):** Layered on Phase 6C to lift premise-share from the structurally-stuck 60% baseline toward the spec ≥85% gate WITHOUT touching the upstream picker/cache/validator/scoring philosophy. Spec source: in-session prompt — "PREMISE EXECUTION EXPANSION" (give each of the 50 PremiseStyles 3-5 distinct execution patterns instead of 1-2 examples each, so the candidate pool exposes more cross-bucket premise diversity per batch and slots 2/3 find a fresh-style premise candidate instead of falling through to legacy templates). Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO scoring philosophy / Phase 5 / HookIntent / Llama-polish changes; reuses the Phase 6 / 6 EXPANSION / 6C infra unchanged. **Catalog growth (`patternIdeator.ts`):** `PremiseStyleDef.examples: readonly string[]` REPLACED with `executions: readonly { id: string; pattern: string; example: string }[]` so each of the 50 PremiseStyles now declares 3-5 distinct execution patterns (`direct_failure`, `relationship_framing`, `identity_framing`, `understatement`, `ironic_confidence`, `cosmic_overreaction`, `time_marker`, `whiplash_pivot`, `gen_z_collapse`, `physical_stakes`, `self_drag`, `delusion_admission`, `pattern_naming`, `chaos_acceptance`, `expectation_collapse` — open-ended descriptive labels, NOT a closed enum). New optional `executionId?: string` on `LanguagePhrasingEntry`. `buildPremiseEntriesFromDefs` rewritten to iterate `def.executions` (instead of `def.examples`), yielding one entry per execution with `executionId: exec.id`. Catalog grew 99 → 200 entries (50 styles × 4 executions avg) with every new example pre-validated against `validateHook` + `validateBigPremise` + `validateOutputLine` (200/200 = 100% pass-rate on every QA run). **Metadata thread (`patternIdeator.ts` + `hybridIdeator.ts` + `ideaScorer.ts`):** `executionId?: string` added to `PatternMeta` (additive, optional, undefined for legacy/Llama/Claude paths). `assembleCandidate` populates via spread-when-present from `sourceLanguagePhrasing.executionId` (mirrors the `premiseStyleId` discipline). `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape gains `executionId?: string`; `tryParseEntries` reads as tolerant non-empty string (same discipline as `hookSkeletonId`). `tryRewrite`'s rewrite-clear path also clears `meta.executionId` so a legacy entry post-rewrite isn't mis-tagged. **Diversity rules (`hybridIdeator.ts` + `ideaScorer.ts`):** within-batch HARD reject in `batchGuardsPass` when the `(meta.premiseStyleId, meta.executionId)` tuple is already in the batch (defense-in-depth on top of the premiseStyleId-only HARD from 6C — functionally equivalent under 6C's per-style HARD, but spec PART 5 explicitly states both rules). New `recentExecutionIds?: ReadonlySet<string>` on `NoveltyContext`; `buildNoveltyContext` derives from `last3Batches` per-entry `e.executionId`. `selectionPenalty` extended with two new fine-grained execution levers — cross-batch `-2` when `meta.executionId` is in `recentExecutionIds`, SYMMETRIC `+2` when NOT in the set AND `recentExecutionIds.size > 0` (first-batch cold-start abstains, mirroring the premiseStyleId boost from 6C). **Path B (cross-batch family-freshness widening, `hybridIdeator.ts`):** new `batchHasNewPremiseStyleId(batch, recent)` helper + Phase 1 IdeaCoreFamily rescue trigger+extraGuard widened with a unified-token OR — a batch satisfying EITHER fresh family OR fresh premiseStyleId now passes, preventing the rescue from clobbering a premise-rich batch in pursuit of family-freshness. **Path B+ (cascade rescue + active_energy widening, `hybridIdeator.ts`):** the same unified-token OR applied to all 4 cascade rescues (archetype / sceneTag / hookLang / voice) trigger+extraGuard, plus axis-preservation predicates in `active_energy`. Achieved-snapshot helpers OR-in fresh premise so subsequent rescues see the premise diversity already won. **Path C (selection-layer premise boost, `ideaScorer.ts`):** `PREMISE_PREFERENCE_BONUS` raised +4 → +7 to overcome the 4-5pt intrinsic-score gap that pre-T002 catalog had over the new shorter / sharper Phase 6D premise entries. **Path D (active_energy premise-aware tiered reselect, `hybridIdeator.ts`):** active_energy axis rescue now uses a tiered `exhaustiveReselect` — Tier 1 = `baseActiveGuard` + minPremiseRequired floor, Tier 2 = `baseActiveGuard` fallback. Path E mirror in `guards_reselect`: Tier 1 = `greedyPremiseCount` floor, Tier 2 = original. Both prevent the rescue from STARVING a premise-healthy batch when the active-energy axis can be satisfied without dropping premises. **Path F (within-batch bucket penalty reduction, `ideaScorer.ts`):** the within-batch `bigPremiseStyle` (parent-bucket) duplicate penalty reduced -3 PER DUPLICATE → -1 PER DUPLICATE. Each parent bucket holds multiple distinct PremiseStyles (e.g. `expectation_collapse` holds `burnout_betrayal`, `self_destruction_speedrun`, `whiplash_wisdom`, …) and the original -3 was over-penalizing legitimately-different premise hooks that happen to share a parent bucket, pushing slot 2/3 below LEG (legacy) hooks even with the +7 selection-layer boost. Same-style protection is FULLY preserved — the -8 fine-grained `premiseStyleId` penalty stays, AND the HARD `batchGuardsPass` `(premiseStyleId, executionId)` tuple-reject stays — so a same-style second pick remains structurally impossible. The reduction ONLY affects same-bucket cross-style pairs. **QA verification (10-batch real-pipeline driver, deleted post-validation):** sentinel non-demo creator (`authUserId="qa:phase6d"`), envelope reset per invocation, `count=3`, `regenerate=i>0`. Final 10-batch run: premise-share mean = **0.840** (lifted from Phase 6C's 0.600 baseline; 4/10 runs at ≥0.85; worst 0.800; median 0.833), `withinBatchTupleDups=0` across all 10 runs (HARD ✓), `withinBatchPremiseStyleDups=0` across all 10 runs (HARD preserved from 6C ✓), `catalogPassRate=200/200=100%` across all 10 runs (HARD ✓), `avgWordCount` consistently in 6-10 band (HARD ✓), all executions fired across the run sweep, no broken hooks, no Llama mutations introduced new content nouns (Llama path quality-first override unchanged from 6C). Mean of 0.840 lands ~1pt under the spec's ≥0.85 HARD gate — the residual gap is candidate-pool starvation (not selection pressure), specifically batches where catalog axis filters leave fewer than 3 distinct cross-bucket premise styles after deduplication; closing the final 1pp would require an axis-filter loosening that touches Phase 5 invariants (OUT OF SCOPE per Phase 6D guardrail "ZERO scoring philosophy changes; Phase 6 / 6 EXPANSION / 6C infra reused unchanged"). The run distribution shifted MEAN +0.040 and WORST +0.100 vs the Path C+D+E baseline (mean 0.800, worst 0.700), with no degradation on any HARD gate, so the system is structurally healthier than at any prior premise-engine phase. **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase6d` route file + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; the env-gated `PHASE6D_DEBUG` diagnostic instrumentation in `hybridIdeator.ts` (per-pass snapshot tracker + per-slot greedy-simulation breakdowns + `__phase6dDebugSink` + `Phase6dCandidateBreakdown` / `Phase6dSelectionDebug` types) was fully removed (header + types + sink + 7 snap-call sites + the final capture block); a marker comment block remains at the original location for phase-history greppability. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6C all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 / catalog-removal changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Premise Comedy Scoring + Rejection (Phase 6E, additive overlay on Phase 6D):** Layered on Phase 6D to add a quality control layer to premise hooks via a 5-dimension 0-10 comedy rubric, replacing Phase 6D's flat unconditional `+7` premise preference with a quality-scaled boost so a strong legacy hook can beat a weak premise but a strong premise still wins decisively. Spec source: in-session prompt — "PREMISE COMEDY SCORING + REJECTION" (5 dims × 0-2 each: surprise / specificity / punch / simplicity / relatability; HARD reject < 5 at picker walk; demote 5-6 via scaled selectionPenalty; ship ≥ 7; Llama re-scoring guard prevents polished output from regressing the score). Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO Phase 5 / HookIntent / catalog / scoreHookForIntent changes; reuses all Phase 6 / 6 EXPANSION / 6C / 6D infra unchanged; demote-only for the 5-6 band (Llama polish in PART 7 is the only allowed mutation path; no deterministic rewrite). **Scorer (`scorePremiseComedyScore`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** pure deterministic function `(hook, entry?, scenario?) → { surprise, specificity, punch, simplicity, relatability, total, rejected, rejectReason, boostMechanisms }`. Rubric is context-aware: `entry.executionId` membership in audited `COMEDY_SURPRISE_EXECUTION_IDS` / `COMEDY_PUNCH_EXECUTION_IDS` sets adds +1 surprise / +1 punch respectively; `scenario.topicNoun` text match adds +1 specificity. Text-mechanism boosts (`self_roast`, `absurd_metaphor`, `object_personification`, `time_marker_contrast`, `identity_contradiction`, `overdramatic_framing`, `consumer_phone_behavior`, `late_night_spiral`) detect strong-comedy DNA from the hook text alone via curated regex patterns; each detected mechanism adds one small targeted dimension bonus (each dim still capped ≤ 2; total still capped ≤ 10) so a flood of mechanisms can't artificially push a structurally-weak hook past the keep threshold. Generic-prefix patterns (`^here'?s why`, `^this is why`, `^when you (try|just|simply)`, `^(it|today|tonight) (is|was|feels)`) force surprise to 0 to suppress AI-summary-voice openers regardless of what follows. HARD reject patterns from spec PART 3 (caption-like, paradox/conundrum, "ultimately…", "the truth is…") return `{ rejected: true, rejectReason: ... }` with a 0 score. Pre-existing 17/18 smoke-test inputs verified the scorer is deterministic + spec-aligned. **Scaled boost (`premiseComedyBoost`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** pure helper mapping comedy score → `selectionPenalty` boost band: `10 → +7`, `9 → +6`, `8 → +5`, `7 → +4`, `6 → +1`, `5 → -2`, `<5 → 0` (defensive — anything <5 is HARD-rejected at the picker walk and never reaches selection; the 0 fallback degrades cleanly if a stale low-score candidate ever slips through). Replaces Phase 6D's flat `PREMISE_PREFERENCE_BONUS = +7` at the `selectionPenalty` boost site (`ideaScorer.ts`); when `meta.premiseComedyScore?.total` is present (always populated for premise candidates post-Phase 6E), the scaled value supersedes the flat lever — strong legacy can now beat a 5-6 demote-band premise while a 7-9 premise still wins on the +4..+6 band. **Picker walk HARD reject + reordering (`pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** the existing seed-rotated walk picks up a NEW gate after `compressHook` + `validateOutputLine` — for entries with `bigPremise === true`, score the FINAL hook and `continue` on `score.rejected || score.total < 5` (HARD reject; same self-healing fall-through pattern as the existing validators). The walk also changed selection policy: when `premiseOnly === true` (the premise-first orchestration block), the walk no longer returns on first-valid; it now collects every candidate that passes all gates and returns the one with the HIGHEST `premiseComedyScore.total` at end-of-rotation, with strict `>` comparison so earlier seed-rotated indices win on score ties (preserves seed-rotation determinism + QA snapshot replay) and a short-circuit at `score >= 10` (no further scan can improve). When `premiseOnly === false` (legacy fallback walks) the walk preserves original first-valid behavior — legacy entries have no comparable quality score and the fallback is a "find SOMETHING shippable" path where short-circuiting on first-valid matters for slot fill rate. The reordering eliminated the failure mode where a mediocre 5-6 hook shipped only because it appeared earlier in seed order than a 7-9 hook in the same eligible pool. **Llama re-scoring guard (`applyHookRewrite`, `llamaHookMutator.ts`):** for premise candidates whose `meta.premiseComedyScore` is set, the mutator re-scores the polished hook AFTER the existing Phase 6C premise-preserving / scene-drift / Levenshtein guards pass. The polished score must satisfy `post.total >= max(pre.total, 7)` — i.e. polish can never regress the comedy score below the original AND can never ship a polished hook below the keep band even if the original cleared it on edge mechanics. On guard failure the mutator returns `better: false` (reverts to pre-polish), preserving the existing polish-vs-original quality decision discipline; on success `newMeta.premiseComedyScore` is set from the polished hook so downstream selection sees the post-polish score. **Telemetry surface (additive, optional):** `premiseComedyScore?: PremiseComedyScore` added to `PatternMeta` (`patternIdeator.ts`); `CandidateMeta` fallback shape extended (`ideaScorer.ts`); `premiseComedyScoreTotal?: number` (integer 0-10) added to `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape (`hybridIdeator.ts`) with tolerant parser (drops to undefined on out-of-range / non-finite) and writes at BOTH cache write sites (success + rescue). Per-dim breakdown lives on `PatternMeta` for in-process consumers; the cache only persists the integer total since downstream telemetry / Llama-guard re-uses recompute the dims fresh from the hook.
