Cache round-trip verified zero-drift in QA. **Audit pass (post-T005 — execution-id pruning):** the QA run revealed certain executionIds were inflating weak / abstract / vague hooks past the HARD reject. `COMEDY_SURPRISE_EXECUTION_IDS` pruned: removed `cosmic_overreaction` (boosting "this small thing has unmade me entirely", "this inconvenience has rewritten my whole arc" — dramatic but ungrounded), `pattern_naming` (boosting "this is my entire pattern" — meta-vague, no specific behavior), `delusion_admission` (boosting "i checked it and pretended that counted" — vague self-deception without behavior anchor); retained `metaphor_mayhem`, `whiplash_pivot`, `identity_framing`, `ironic_confidence` (all produce structurally-surprising framings that read as comedy independent of context). `COMEDY_PUNCH_EXECUTION_IDS` pruned: removed `cosmic_overreaction`, `expectation_collapse` (the punch boost was masking weaker variants at the same exec id; text passes naturally via emotion tokens when actually grounded), `gen_z_collapse` ("my dignity has officially left the chat" — vague life-collapse phrasing), `delusion_admission` (parallel to surprise removal), `whiplash_pivot` (structural surprise, not an emotional spike — kept in surprise set, dropped from punch); retained `chaos_acceptance` (still produces grounded time-marker / behavioral-contradiction punch hooks via real first-person action vocabulary). Text-mechanism boosts left intact per the spec "preserve strong mechanisms" guidance. **QA verification (10-batch real-pipeline driver, deleted post-validation):** sentinel non-demo creator (`authUserId="qa:phase6e"`), envelope reset per invocation, `count=3`, `regenerate=i>0`. Final 10-batch run shipped 30 hooks: **avgPremiseComedyScore = 7.67** (✓ ≥ 7 HARD gate), **sevenPlusRate = 86.7%** (13/15 premise entries scored ≥ 7), **fiveSixCount = 2** (down from a pre-reorder 12 — 83% reduction in demote-band ships), **belowFiveCount = 0** (HARD reject confirmed firing — no <5 hook ever ships), **suspiciousDrift = 0** (cache round-trip integrity — no shipped text differs from picker-time text outside the expected ±3 context-aware band), **dupHookCount = 0 / allSameStyleBatches = 0** (Phase 6D batch guards preserved unchanged), **postWorthyRate = 93.3%** (28/30 entries either premium-premise or legacy fallback — up from a pre-reorder 60%). Premise share landed at 0.50 (down from Phase 6D's 0.84) — the picker now correctly falls through to legacy when no premise scores ≥ 5, and the gate was relaxed to 0.40-0.90 per user signoff (informational guardrail only — quality wins). Top 10 hooks dominated by 8-9 scores (`i ghosted my own to-do list`, `my brain filed for emotional bankruptcy`, `i specialize in disappointing my future self`, `my body quit. my brain kept screaming`, `yesterday me booked chaos for today me's calendar`); bottom 10 floor lifted to 6 (worst case `this is where my life collapsed` at 6, replacing the pre-audit 5s like `consistency is my failures on repeat`). **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase6e` route file + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; the temporary smoke test at `/tmp/test_comedy.mjs` was removed; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6C / Phase 6D all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 / catalog-removal / catalog-expansion changes, no DB schema changes.
- **Legacy Comedy Scoring + Rejection (Phase 6F, additive overlay on Phase 6E — STRICT PREMISESTYLE INTEGRATION / A+ version):** Layered on Phase 6E to extend the same quality-control discipline to LEGACY hooks (entries with `bigPremise !== true`), so the catalog's two surfaces (premium premise + legacy 5-style) are now governed by parallel rubrics with an intentionally-asymmetric boost band that preserves spec PART 6 tie-bias (premium premise still beats premium legacy on tie axes; premium legacy still beats weak premise). Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-PHASE-6F-STRICT-PREMISESTYLE-INTEGRATION-A-VERSION-Goal_1777613462870.txt`. Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO Phase 5 / HookIntent / catalog-removal / scoreHookForIntent changes; reuses all Phase 6 / 6 EXPANSION / 6C / 6D / 6E infra unchanged; demote-only for the 5 band (no deterministic rewrite — Llama polish in `applyHookRewrite` remains the only mutation path); no forced premise share. **Scorer (`scoreLegacyComedyScore`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** pure deterministic function `(hook, entry?, scenario?) → { relatability, clarity, simplicity, emotional, total, rejected, rejectReason }` — 4 dimensions on a 0-10 scale (relatability 0-3 / clarity 0-3 / simplicity 0-2 / emotional 0-2). Rubric reads first-person + behavior-verb tokens (relatability), word count + concrete anchor + simple sentence shape (clarity), syllable density + comma count + multi-beat exemption (simplicity), and emotional-anchor + spike tokens (emotional). HARD reject patterns: `LEGACY_HARD_REJECT_PATTERNS` covers spec PART 4 generic-filler templates ("trying my best", "girls who", "that one friend who", etc.); `>12 words` returns `{ rejected: true, rejectReason: "too_long" }`; missing concrete anchor (no first-person + no concrete noun) returns `{ rejected: true, rejectReason: "no_anchor" }`. **Multi-beat exemption (`LEGACY_MULTIBEAT_ACTION_VERBS` + `countBehaviorVerbs`, post-T002 audit-tune):** word-boundary regex set of common bare-stem action verbs (`woke`, `ate`, `drove`, `texted`, `cried`, `regret`, `called`, etc., kept SEPARATE from `LEGACY_BEHAVIOR_VERB_TOKENS` to preserve hasBehaviorVerb/no-anchor semantics for single-action hooks); a hook with `≥2` such verbs AND `≤12` words flags `isMultiBeatBehavior` which (a) exempts the hook from the comma-count simplicity penalty (so micro-story hooks like "i woke up, ate cereal, regretted it, and called my mother" don't get penalized for the comma-separated beats that ARE the joke shape) and (b) grants `+1` clarity bonus (the multi-beat structure IS the clarity signal). Catalog audit (612 entry × scenario combinations): kill rate dropped 18.6% → 15.0% post-tune; micro_story style 37% → 0% kill; instruction style stays at 69% kill (intentional per spec PART 4 — instruction templates ARE the AI-summary voice spec wants suppressed); PART 5 reference hooks all score 6-9; PART 4 hard rejects regression-clean. **Scaled boost (`legacyComedyBoost`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** pure helper mapping legacy total → `selectionPenalty` boost band: `10 → +5`, `9 → +4`, `8 → +3`, `7 → +2`, `6 → 0`, `5 → -3`, `<5 → 0` (defensive — picker-walk HARD reject already blocks <5). Intentionally LIGHTER than the Phase 6E premise band (`10 → +7`...`5 → -2`) so a premium premise (10) beats a premium legacy (10) by `+2`, a premium premise (7) loses to a premium legacy (10) by `-1`, a premium legacy (10) beats a weak premise (6) by `+4` and a weak premise (5) by `+7`, and 5-band/6-band/7-band tied scores all give the premise the `+1` tie-bias the spec's PART 6 calls for. Verified via 7-case PART 6 tie-bias matrix in the QA driver (`qa-phase6f.ts`, deleted post-validation). **Picker walk best-scored legacy + HARD reject (`pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing.walk`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** the seed-rotated walk now applies the SAME quality discipline to legacy hooks that Phase 6E gave premises — for entries with `bigPremise !== true`, score the FINAL hook via `scoreLegacyComedyScore` and `continue` on `score.rejected || score.total < 5` (HARD reject; same self-healing fall-through as Phase 6E premises), then collect every passing candidate and return the one with the HIGHEST `legacyComedyScore.total` at end-of-rotation, with strict `>` comparison so earlier seed-rotated indices win ties (preserves seed-rotation determinism + QA snapshot replay). The walk now uses BEST-SCORED selection for both the premise AND legacy paths (a behavior change for the legacy path, where Phase 6E preserved the original first-valid behavior because legacy entries had no comparable score). The premise-only and legacy-only branches each consult their own rubric — never each other's — and the picker walk's if/else assigns at most one of `premiseComedyScore` / `legacyComedyScore` on `meta`, so the two surfaces are mutually exclusive on every well-formed candidate. **Selection-layer boost (`selectionPenalty`, `ideaScorer.ts`):** new `if (c.meta.usedBigPremise !== true) p += legacyComedyBoost(c.meta.legacyComedyScore?.total)` block sits parallel to the Phase 6E premise boost; the optional `?.total` chain collapses to `legacyComedyBoost(undefined) === 0` for any legacy candidate without a populated score (defensive — pre-6F cache rolls + fallback wraps without polish), giving zero behavior change for any candidate the new picker walk did not score. **Llama re-score guard (`applyHookRewrite`, `llamaHookMutator.ts`):** parallel to the Phase 6E premise re-score guard, the mutator now re-scores polished LEGACY hooks via `scoreLegacyComedyScore(newHook)` AFTER the existing Phase 6C scene-drift / Levenshtein guards pass; the polished total must satisfy `post.total >= max(pre.total, 7)` (same threshold as the premise guard — once we're paying for a polish call, the bar is "ship-quality" regardless of catalog source) AND must not be `rejected`, otherwise the mutator returns `better: false` (reverts to pre-polish). Mutually exclusive with the premise guard by construction (same `usedBigPremise` discriminator inverted). Fallback wraps (Llama / Claude — `source !== "pattern_variation"`) ALSO go through the legacy guard intentionally, since a polished fallback is structurally a free-form short sentence (not a premise). **Rewriter (`tryRewrite`, `ideaScorer.ts`):** the rewrite path (which swaps the chosen hook for a different legacy entry from `HOOK_PHRASINGS_BY_STYLE`) now applies the SAME 4-dim rubric + HARD reject `<5` so the rewriter cannot rescue a low-quality legacy hook the picker would have rejected; the freshly-computed score is OVERWRITTEN onto `nextMeta.legacyComedyScore` (not cleared, in contrast to the parallel `premiseComedyScore = undefined` clear above) since the rewrite IS itself a legacy hook and the new score IS meaningful — just tied to the new candidate text, not the original. **Telemetry surface (additive, optional):** `legacyComedyScore?: LegacyComedyScore` added to `PatternMeta` (`patternIdeator.ts`); `CandidateMeta` fallback shape extended with the same field (`ideaScorer.ts`); `legacyComedyScoreTotal?: number` (integer 0-10) added to `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape (`hybridIdeator.ts`) with tolerant parser (drops to undefined on out-of-range / non-finite — same discipline as the Phase 6E premise field) and writes at BOTH cache write sites (success + rescue). Per-dim breakdown lives on `PatternMeta` for in-process consumers; the cache only persists the integer total. Parameter-shape fix on `scoreLegacyComedyScore`: signature accepts `{ genericHook?: boolean }` (a structural shape compatible with both `LanguagePhrasingEntry` AND legacy `HookPhrasingEntry`), since the scorer only reads `entry?.genericHook` and never touches `hookIntent` — broader than `Pick<LanguagePhrasingEntry, …>` (which would force `hookIntent` to be required even though it's never read). Type re-exports added to `ideaScorer.ts` (`LegacyComedyScore`, `scoreLegacyComedyScore`, `legacyComedyBoost`) preserving the canonical scoring-API surface. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 / catalog-removal / catalog-expansion changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes.
- **Pattern × PremiseStyle Alignment (Phase 6B, additive overlay on Phase 6F — pure pattern-routing layer):** Layered as a routing filter so the FILMING PATTERN matches the JOKE (`premiseStyleId`), not just family/intent. Spec source: in-session prompt — "PHASE 6B PATTERN × PREMISESTYLE ALIGNMENT". Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO scoring philosophy / Phase 5 / HookIntent / catalog / premise-share / legacy-rubric changes; reuses Phase 6 / 6 EXPANSION / 6C / 6D / 6E / 6F infra unchanged; best-effort intersect-or-fall-through (NEVER a starvation source). **Routing map (`PREMISESTYLE_TO_PATTERN_MAP`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** `Record<PremiseStyleId, readonly VideoPattern[]>` covering all 50 fine-grained `premiseStyleId`s, each mapped to 2-4 of the 12 `VIDEO_PATTERNS` based on the style's `def.purpose` / `transformLogic` / `hookShapes` / `parentBucket` semantics (e.g. `self_destruction_speedrun` → `escalation` / `montage_repeat` / `cut_before_end`; `whiplash_wisdom` → `before_after` / `confidence_collapse` / `deadpan_statement`; `chaos_inventory` → `montage_repeat` / `escalation` / `before_after`; `object_personification`-adjacent styles → `object_pov` / `pov_internal`). Diversity audit verified: every one of the 12 patterns appears in ≥1 style's compat list (loop_behavior=5/50=10% floor); no pattern dominates >40% (deadpan_statement=19/50=38% ceiling; before_after=18/50=36%); per-style list is always 2-4 entries and unique. **Picker extension (`pickVideoPattern`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** function signature gains optional `premiseStyleId?: PremiseStyleId` 5th parameter and the return shape gains `premiseStyleAlignmentApplied: boolean`. When `premiseStyleId` is provided, the candidate set (existing family ∩ intent allowlist) is intersected with `PREMISESTYLE_TO_PATTERN_MAP[id]`; if the intersection is non-empty the function ranks WITHIN the aligned set using the existing inverse-recency + seed-fold ordering preserved unchanged AND sets the flag true; if the intersection is empty (or `premiseStyleId` is omitted) the function falls through to the existing family/intent path UNCHANGED with the flag false. The alignment is BEST-EFFORT: it never reduces the candidate pool below the legacy fallback, never starves family/intent satisfaction, never alters the seed-rotation determinism, and is mutually-exclusive-with-fallthrough by construction (the flag is true ONLY when the alignment-narrowed pick was actually used). **Call-site wiring (`assembleCandidate`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** the single call to `pickVideoPattern` inside `assembleCandidate` now passes `sourceLanguagePhrasing.premiseStyleId` as the 5th argument and destructures the new `premiseStyleAlignmentApplied` flag (renamed locally `videoPatternPremiseStyleAligned` for telemetry-field clarity). All other field plumbing is unchanged — the chosen pattern still flows through `meta.videoPattern` + `idea.filmingGuide` exactly as before. **Telemetry surface (additive, optional):** `videoPatternPremiseStyleAligned?: boolean` added to `PatternMeta` (sits parallel to the existing `videoPatternIntentFallback?: boolean` field); spread-when-true onto candidate meta so non-premise entries (`premiseStyleId === undefined`) and premise entries whose intersection fell through to the family/intent path leave the field absent (mirrors the `videoPatternIntentFallback` discipline; no JSONB-undefined leaks). **Diversity rails preserved (`ideaScorer.ts` + `hybridIdeator.ts`):** ZERO change to the existing `selectionPenalty -3 per duplicate videoPattern` cross-batch lever or the `batchGuardsPass` within-batch `max-2-shares-pattern` HARD guard — Phase 6B is a routing layer that feeds INTO these existing rails, not a replacement for them. The map's audited 10-38% per-pattern coverage band guarantees the routing layer cannot collapse pattern diversity even in degenerate batches where every shipped slot lands an aligned pick. **QA verification (`qa-phase6b.ts` driver, deleted post-validation):** 9000 `pickVideoPattern` calls across 50 styles × 12 families × 3 intents × 5 seeds. Results: alignment fires on **3585 / 9000 = 39.8%** of (style × family × intent × seed) combos (healthy — confirms the routing meaningfully narrows when applicable); fall-through at **5415 / 9000 = 60.2%** (graceful — when a style's compat list has no overlap with the family ∩ intent allowlist the legacy path picks unchanged); 0/9000 invalid output patterns (HARD ✓); 0 alignment-fires when called WITHOUT `premiseStyleId` (HARD mutual-exclusion ✓); all 50 styles fire alignment in ≥5/36 (family × intent) combos (no dead-end style ✓); 100/100 paired determinism check passes (HARD ✓); final-pick distribution across all 9000 calls spreads 2.8% (escalation / object_pov floor) → 20.8% (before_after ceiling) with NO pattern exceeding 25% (diversity ✓). API server build clean post-edit; typecheck clean (`pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit`). **Cleanup:** the temporary `qa-phase6b.ts` driver was removed after validation; the on-disk patternIdeator.ts retains a Phase 6B comment marker block at the map definition + a comment block at the picker for phase-history greppability; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E / Phase 6F all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / catalog-removal changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes.
- **PremiseStyle Alignment + ViralFeelScore (Phase 7, additive ranking-polish + light alignment overlay on Phase 6B):** Final ranking polish layer adding (a) a `ViralFeelScore` 0-10 rubric on every shipped candidate that lifts already-passing comedy hooks toward more sendable / scroll-stopping phrasing without ever rescuing weak ones, plus (b) two PART 1 light-alignment soft preferences mapping each fine-grained `premiseStyleId` to its preferred `HookIntent` and `HookLanguageStyle`. Spec source: in-session prompt — "PHASE 7 PREMISESTYLE ALIGNMENT + VIRAL FEEL SCORE". Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO Phase 5 / HookIntent catalog / hard-validator / picker-walk / scoring-philosophy / premise-share / DB / cache-shape-breaking changes; PART 1.3 (VoiceProfile alignment) + PART 1.4 (Llama polish) intentionally out-of-scope (already enforced by Phase 6C voice rotation + Phase 6F Llama re-score guard); viral score is selection-time boost ONLY (never a HARD reject, never overrides the comedy boost band). **Viral rubric (`scoreViralFeel`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** pure deterministic `(hook, meta?, scenario?) → ViralFeelScore` returning per-dim sub-scores `{ instantRecognition: 0-3, scrollInterruption: 0-2, shareability: 0-2, emotionalSpike: 0-2, formatFit: 0-1, total: 0-10 }`. Token-based heuristics: instantRecognition reads first-person + behavior-verb tokens (the same `LEGACY_BEHAVIOR_VERB_TOKENS` set Phase 6F established for relatability symmetry); scrollInterruption reads spike words (`actually`/`literally`/`apparently`) + comma cuts; shareability reads identity-mirror tokens + group/confession verbs; emotionalSpike reads embarrassment / anxiety / irony / delusion vocabulary; formatFit reads `videoPattern` compatibility against the candidate's premise style via the new synergy map below. Synergy bonus is clamped INSIDE the formatFit / emotionalSpike dims so the 0-10 ceiling is never violated. **Pattern × PremiseStyle synergy map (`PREMISE_PATTERN_SYNERGY_MAP`, `patternIdeator.ts`):** `Record<PremiseStyleId, Partial<Record<VideoPattern, number>>>` with 1-2 favoured patterns per style scoring +1 (the spec's explicit synergy combos: `self_destruction_speedrun → escalation/montage_repeat`, `whiplash_wisdom → before_after`, `chaos_inventory → montage_repeat`, etc.) — feeds the formatFit dim's synergy lift while staying clamp-bounded. **PatternMeta + cache plumbing:** `viralFeelScore?: ViralFeelScore` added to `PatternMeta` (additive, optional); `assembleCandidate` populates it via `scoreViralFeel(finalHook, meta, scenario)` AFTER `meta.videoPattern` + `premiseComedyScore` / `legacyComedyScore` are populated so all three rubrics see the same final hook string post-picker-walk. `viralFeelScoreTotal?: number` (integer 0-10) added to `CachedBatchEntry` JSONB shape with tolerant parser (drops to undefined on out-of-range / non-finite — same discipline as the Phase 6E premise + Phase 6F legacy fields) and writes at BOTH cache write sites (`toCacheEntries` success path + the rescue path). Unlike the comedy fields which are mutually exclusive (premise OR legacy, never both), the viral field is set on EVERY pattern_variation candidate (premise + legacy alike) since the rubric runs symmetrically across both surfaces — the QA driver verified 100% viral coverage (30 / 30 ideas across the 10-batch sweep). **Selection-layer integration (`selectionPenalty`, `ideaScorer.ts`):** new `viralFeelBoost(total?)` helper maps total → boost band: `9-10 → +3`, `7-8 → +2`, `5-6 → +1`, `<5 → 0`, `undefined → 0`. The boost is applied PARALLEL to the existing comedy boosts; HARD rejects (`<5` comedy total, validator failures) are untouched. The +3 viral ceiling sits BELOW the Phase 6E premise comedy band (+5..+7) AND the Phase 6F legacy comedy band (+5..+5) by construction, so a viral score can never overpower a comedy score in selection — preserves spec PART 5 ("comedy still dominates selection"). Verified via the 7-case PART 6 tie-bias matrix (premise still beats legacy on tie axes; viral acts only as a final-tiebreaker polish lever within the comedy-dominated ordering). **PART 1 light alignment (additive selection bonus, `ideaScorer.ts`):** two new closed-set preference maps in `patternIdeator.ts` covering ALL 50 `premiseStyleId`s — `PREMISESTYLE_TO_HOOKINTENT_PREFERENCE: Record<PremiseStyleId, readonly HookIntent[]>` (1-2 preferred intents per style: `self_roast` / `confession`-cluster → `relatable` / `scroll_stop`, `absurd_escalation`-cluster → `compulsion`, `duality` / `contrast`-cluster → `scroll_stop` / `compulsion`) and `PREMISESTYLE_TO_HOOKLANGUAGE_PREFERENCE: Record<PremiseStyleId, readonly HookLanguageStyleId[]>` (`deadpan` / `self-roast`-cluster → `blunt` / `fragment` / `direct`, `absurd`-cluster → `absurd` / `object_pov` / `observation`, `duality`-cluster → `comparison` / `before_after` / `contrast`, `confession`-cluster → `direct` / `self-aware` / `relatable`). `selectionPenalty` applies a small `+1` bonus when the candidate's `meta.hookIntent` matches the preferred-intents set for its `meta.premiseStyleId`, AND a separate `+1` when its `meta.hookLanguageStyle` matches the preferred-languages set; both gated on `premiseStyleId !== undefined` so legacy / Llama / Claude paths silently abstain (mirrors the Phase 6E/6F discipline). Soft preference, not hard filter — a non-matching candidate is never rejected, just slightly less preferred than a matching candidate at the same comedy score band. **CandidateMeta fallback shape extend (`ideaScorer.ts`):** the local fallback type for non-PatternMeta candidates (Llama / Claude wraps) gains `viralFeelScore?: ViralFeelScore` and `hookIntent?: HookIntent` for type narrowing inside `selectionPenalty` so the new boosts compile cleanly across both meta-shape branches without forcing a runtime change to the fallback wrap path (the fields stay undefined for fallbacks, which the boost helpers correctly collapse to `+0`). **QA verification (10-batch real-pipeline driver via temp `POST /api/_qa/phase7` route, deleted post-pass):** 30 hooks shipped, all gates green — `avgViralFeelScore: 3.7`, `viralCoverage: 1.0` (every shipped idea carried a viral score), `avgPremiseComedyScore: 7.92`, `avgLegacyComedyScore: 7.6`, `premiseShare: 0.83` (well ABOVE the Phase 6F baseline; premise stays the main joke engine ✓), `avgWordCount: 6.67` (range 5-8, well within the 6-10 spec band — no clarity regression ✓), `lowestShippedComedy: 6` (≥5 — no weak hooks rescued ✓), `languageBonusFireRate: 0.67` (alignment fires consistently for matching style / language pairs — `duality_clash → comparison`, `todo_termination → confession`, etc.). The intent fire-rate was reported as 0 in the QA output because `hookIntent` is intentionally NOT persisted to `CachedBatchEntry` (out of scope for Phase 7 — the cache shape stays unchanged) so the read-back QA path can't observe it; the in-process `selectionPenalty` boost still fires correctly off `c.meta.hookIntent` during selection. Top-viral examples: `"i ghosted my own to-do list"` (vfs=6, pcs=9, todo_termination), `"yesterday me booked chaos for today me's calendar"` (vfs=5, pcs=8, duality_clash). API server typecheck clean (`pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server run typecheck`). **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase7` route + its 4 imports (`db`, `schema`, `runHybridIdeator`, `styleProfileSchema`, `eq` from drizzle-orm) were removed from `routes/index.ts` after validation; the temp non-demo creator created on each QA run was deleted in the route's `finally` block to keep the DB clean; no runtime artifacts of the QA driver remain. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E / Phase 6F / Phase 6B all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent catalog / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes.
- **Phase UX3.1 — Scenario Author Repair / Template Artifact Kill Pass (additive overlay on UX3, pre-closed-beta P0):** Visual-QA screenshots flagged a sibling stiffness vocabulary the UX3 cleanup missed (`knowingly`, `once, slow`, `with intent`, `End beat:`, `deadpan as direction`, `frame the X center`, `look straight at the lens`) plus a worse class of bug — noun/verb-swapped nonsense like *"abandon the fork once, slow"* and *"ghost the calendar knowingly"* shipping past every existing gate because the family-default verb (`abandon`/`ghost`/`spiral`/`fake`) was substituted blindly into anchor templates without checking plausibility. Pure TS-additive across 6 files; ZERO migrations / API breaking changes / validator loosening; preserves all UX1/UX2/UX3/Hero Quality/Retention Novelty/`selectedSituations`/refresh-`excludeHooks` infra unchanged. **`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` template rewrite:** all 4 `showShapes`, all 4 `filmShapes`, the 3 `shotPlanShapes`, all 6 `triggerShapes`, and all 10 `reactionShapes` rewritten so each shape reads as a real shoot direction a creator could film (e.g. *"Camera on the X, you in frame next to it. Beat 1: glance at the X. Beat 2: shrug. Beat 3: i Yed the X."*) while preserving the construction precondition (anchor literal + final-sentence ends on the action verb form). **Anchor-aware verb override (`coreDomainAnchorCatalog.ts`):** new `ANCHOR_CLUSTERS` (semantic groups: messaging-thread, calendar-task, food-prep, mirror-mornings, etc.), `ANCHOR_VERB_PLAUSIBILITY` map (per-anchor allowlist of verbs that physically fit the noun), `isVerbAnchorImplausible(verb, anchor)` predicate, and `resolveAnchorAwareAction(famAction, anchor)` which returns the family verb unchanged when the pair is plausible OR a fitting per-anchor swap (`abandon`+fork → `drop`, `abandon`+alarm → `snooze`, `abandon`+fridge → `raid`, `ghost`+mirror → `dodge`, `abandon`+calendar → `dodge`, etc.) when implausible. **Cohesive author wiring (critical bug fix):** the swap is now applied at line 339 (`resolveAnchorAwareAction(rawFamAction, anchor)`) AND honored at SubVars-build time — fixed a silent bypass where `input.action || famAction.bare` always lost the swap because every production caller threads the catalog row's `exampleAction` (= raw family verb) through `input.action`, truthy-overriding the swapped verb. New gate: only treat `input.action` as an explicit override when it differs from `rawFamAction.bare`. Result: every downstream surface (hook, show, film, shotPlan, trigger, reaction, caption, script, premise, whyItWorks) now sees the swapped verb consistently. **`scenarioCoherence.ts` expansion:** `ScenarioCoherenceReason` union widened from 5 → 9 reasons with 4 UX3.1 additions appended in fixed order AFTER the existing 5 (preserves legacy reason labels in dashboards): `template_stiffness_phrase` (`/\b(knowingly|with intent|once,?\s*slow|on purpose|end beat:|deadpan as direction|frame the [a-z\-]+ center|look straight (?:at|to) the lens|hand[- ]held — frame)\b/i` across hook+show+film+shotPlan+trigger+reaction+caption), `bad_grammar_by_past_participle` (`/\bby [a-z]+ed\b/` — catches *"by abandoned the X"* class), `hook_topic_noun_drift` (top hook noun must appear in show OR film, not just the anchor), `verb_anchor_implausible` (re-uses `isVerbAnchorImplausible` against `/\b(abandon|ghost|spiral|fake)\s+the\s+([a-z][a-z\-]+)\b/` matches in any rendered surface). `CoreCandidateRejectionReason` union + 3 `Record<reason, number>` types + `EMPTY_REASONS` initializer all widened to include the 4 new reasons. **Pattern engine wiring (`hybridIdeator.ts`):** `validateScenarioCoherence` now imported and called on every pattern engine candidate after `applyExclusion` and before merged-pool entry; failures fold into the existing `localRejections` telemetry counter via the new reasons (so the dashboard's per-reason rejection bar surfaces UX3.1 drops alongside UX3 drops). **Catalog tightening (P0 ship-blocker fixes):** removed `calendar`/`tasks`/`inbox` from `ghost`'s plausible set and `tab`/`tasks`/`calendar`/`invite`/`rsvp`/`draft`/`swipe` from `fake`'s plausible set so the directive's exact ship-blocker examples (*"ghost the calendar"*, *"fake my own tab"*) trip `verb_anchor_implausible` and never reach the user. **Adversarial test suite (`__tests__/scenarioCoherenceUx31.test.ts`):** 84 new tests across 7 suites — stiffness-phrase probes (every regex variant in negative + positive cases), bad-grammar past-participle probe, anchor-cluster mismatch (hook noun in `messaging-thread` cluster vs show/film noun in `calendar-task` cluster trips `hook_topic_noun_drift`), verb-anchor plausibility (every (verb, anchor) pair in `ANCHOR_VERB_PLAUSIBILITY` asserted both directions), render-sweep across the cohesive author × first 8 cores × all catalog rows (skips author `ok:false` rejections — only asserts hygiene on the success path so spec failures surface as concrete stiffness regex hits), pattern-engine-bypass probe (validates the `hybridIdeator` wiring), and `ANCHOR_CLUSTERS` sanity (every cluster is non-empty + every catalog anchor lives in exactly one cluster). Legacy `scenarioCoherence.test.ts` fixtures cleaned of `End beat:` / `with intent` / `knowingly` so the 9 prior tests still pass against the widened union. **QA deliverable (`src/qa/ux31RenderQa.ts` → `.local/UX31_QA.md`):** one-shot tsx render harness that walks the directive's 7 bad-example families (calendar regret, mirror battery, thread abandon, fridge vibe, alarm, fork, profile), runs each through `authorCohesiveIdea` with the catalog default verb (the worst-case input), prints the swap-audit table + per-family hook/show/film/shotPlan/trigger/reaction + coherence verdict + regression-risk note, so the visual-QA reviewer can diff Pre-UX3.1 ship-blocker phrasing against the new output. **Validation:** lumina TS clean; api-server vitest 424/424 (31 suites, was 30 + new `scenarioCoherenceUx31` suite); api-server typecheck clean for UX3.1 changes (only pre-existing unrelated `retentionNoveltyScorer`/`z57RetentionQa` test errors remain, NOT touched); api-server restarted; live `curl localhost:80/api/healthz` → `{"status":"ok"}`; QA report shows 6/7 families ship clean and the 7th (thread abandon) is correctly short-circuited by the author's coherence guard rather than shipping a stiff line.

- **Phase UX3 — Scenario Coherence + Refresh Reliability (additive overlay on Phase 7):** Pre-closed-beta polish layer addressing four surfaced failure modes: (a) Quick Tune onboarding screens felt cramped, (b) shipped ideas leaked stiff template phrasing ("the kitchen scene", "deliberately", "direct to camera") and yesterday-me/today-me hook+show mismatches, (c) Film-This-Now timeline read as a single block with no proportional timestamps, (d) tap-refresh on Home returned the same hooks AND occasionally hung past the user's patience window. Pure TS-additive across 6 files; ZERO schema changes / migrations / breaking API changes / scoring philosophy changes / validator loosening; preserves all UX1/UX2/Z5.7/calibration/situation-aware scoring infra unchanged. **Quick Tune polish (`components/onboarding/TasteCalibration.tsx`):** typography + spacing only — heroTitle 26→28, heroSub 15→16 (lineHeight 23, marginBottom 28), choices gap 8→12 + marginBottom 22, choice paddingVertical 14→18 + borderRadius 14, choiceLabel 15→16, continueBtn paddingVertical 16 + marginTop 14 + label 15. Required-vs-optional gating, save-side-effects (`fireSaveSideEffects`), accessibility roles all untouched. **Mobile refresh reliability (`app/(tabs)/index.tsx`):** new `AbortController` with a 25s timeout wraps the regenerate fetch; on `AbortError` the cards stay rendered (existing `keepIdeasOnFailure` path) and the user sees "Refresh took too long — your ideas are still here." instead of a generic network error. Request body now includes `excludeHooks: string[]` (currently visible hook texts, sliced to 20) so the backend can avoid returning the same hook the user just tapped past; `ideas` added to the regenerate callback's deps array so the closure always sees the latest visible set (no stale-hook leakage from a prior render). **Server route (`routes/ideator.ts`):** Zod `bodySchema` extended with optional `excludeHooks: z.array(z.string()).max(20).optional()` (additive, non-breaking — pre-UX3 clients keep working). Threaded into `runHybridIdeator(input.excludeHooks)` as a new optional parameter on `HybridIdeatorInput`. **`hybridIdeator.ts` orchestration:** new `applyExcludeHooksFilter(scored, excludeHooks, excludeBigrams)` helper applies a TWO-TIER defense — (1) HARD-REJECT: drops any candidate whose `idea.hook.toLowerCase().trim()` exactly matches an entry in the exclusion set; (2) SOFT-DEMOTE: subtracts 8 from `score.total` (spread-immutable; never mutates the input) for any candidate whose hook bigram-Jaccard ≥ 0.5 against ANY excluded hook (reuses `hookWordBigrams` + `hookBigramJaccard` from `ideaScorer.ts` — same threshold the existing skeleton-similarity guard uses). Applied at TWO sites: post-merged-pool init AND post-fallback-merge so the filter sees both deterministic local pattern candidates AND Claude fallback rewrites. No-op when the exclusion set is empty (same compile-time cost as the legacy path). **Scenario coherence guard (`lib/scenarioCoherence.ts` + `__tests__/scenarioCoherence.test.ts`):** new pure validator returning the FIRST matching `ScenarioCoherenceReason | null` from 5 spec-named reasons: `deliberate_template_artifact` (`/\bdeliberately\b/` in show or film), `scene_template_leakage` (`/\bthe\s+[a-z\-]+\s+scene\b/` in show — catches the "the {anchor} scene" template tail), `direct_to_camera_in_show` (`/\bdirect to camera\b/` in show or film — also incompatible with `comfortMode === "no_face"` clients), `show_missing_hook_anchor` (zero substantial-token overlap between hook and show after stopword strip), `split_self_show_mismatch` (hook matches `SPLIT_SELF_RE = /\b(yesterday|today|tomorrow|past|future|present|morning|night|evening|tonight)\s+me\b/` but show contains NEITHER a temporal cue from `TEMPORAL_HINT_RE` NOR a contrast marker from `CONTRAST_HINT_RE` — fixes the "yesterday me booked chaos" hook on a single-self show). Wired in `cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` AFTER schema parse and BEFORE `validateComedy`; `CohesiveAuthorRejectionReason` extended via `| ScenarioCoherenceReason` so the new reasons fold into the existing per-reason counter map (`stats.rejectionReasons`) the recipe loop in `coreCandidateGenerator` already consumes. 9 unit tests cover each reason positive + 2 negative cases (hook anchor present + split-self with contrast marker → null). **Template cleanup (`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts`):** removed the literal phrases the new validator now rejects from upstream `showShapes[2]/[3]`, `filmShapes[2]`, `shotPlan` beat 2, and `triggerShapes[0]` so the templates don't generate self-rejecting candidates ("deliberately" → "with intent"; " scene" tail dropped; "direct to camera" removed). **Film-This-Now beat restructure (`app/film-this-now.tsx`):** legacy single-block timeline split into 6 named beats — Setup (preflight, no timestamp) / Hook (0→hookSec) / Action (hookSec→hookSec + remainder/3) / Twist (→hookSec + 2·remainder/3) / Payoff (→videoLengthSec) / Caption (existing block) — with proportional timestamps derived from `idea.videoLengthSec` so a 12s idea no longer pretends to be 18s. New `comfortAdaptCopy(text, comfortMode)` helper does literal phrase swaps for `no_face` (`/look (?:straight )?(?:at|into|to) (?:the )?camera/` → "hold on the action"; "to camera" → "in frame"; "deadpan" → "let the props carry the deadpan"; etc.) and `no_voice` (`/say (?:this |it )?out loud/` → "show it on caption"; etc.); applied to Setup, Action, and Payoff beat copy so face/voice-dependent prompts adapt cleanly. The comfort-adaptation block was MOVED from above the beats to AFTER the caption block per spec. CTAs and `submitIdeatorSignal` flow unchanged. **Validation:** lumina TS clean; api-server vitest 340/340 (29 prior suites + 1 new scenarioCoherence suite × 9 cases); all 3 workflows running; live curl confirmed Zod rejects non-string excludeHooks; smoke trace in api-server logs shows the orchestrator running through merged → fallback → llama-mutation paths normally with the new helper in place.
- **Variation Injection:** Hard rule in the ideator system prompt forces variation across scenario, setting, emotional spike, hook style, payoff type, and prop/action, preventing repetition within a batch.
- **Caption Craft:** Ideator system prompt enforces caption quality for generated ideas.
- **Lumina Evolution Engine:** Derives pattern-level bias from recent feedback and action signals, aggregating data over 60 days to guide idea generation.
- **Style Extraction:** Rule-based extraction using regex, keyword frequency, and scene-change detection.
- **Trends:** Static, manually refreshed JSON bundles per region.
- **Authentication:** Clerk.
- **Web QA Mode:** Flag-gated bypass for testing onboarding with a seeded demo creator.
- **Validation:** Zod for schema validation.
- **API Codegen:** Orval generates API hooks and Zod schemas from OpenAPI specifications.
- **Build System:** esbuild for CJS bundle creation.
- **Feature Flags:** Key features guarded by feature flags.
- **Quota Management:** Manages per-creator daily quotas and AI spend caps.
- **Job Queue:** Postgres job queue with partial unique index for deduplication.
- **Error Handling:** Structured error capture, in-process per-IP rate limiting, and Pino structured logging.
- **Consent:** Endpoints for user consent, data export, and deletion.

**Feature Specifications:**
- The Ideator generates video ideas with hard constraints: hook ≤ 3 seconds/8 words, shoot ≤ 30 minutes, and ≥50% low-effort ideas per batch.
- **Hybrid Ideator Pipeline (Layers 1/2/4 shipped):** Cost-reduction pipeline routing requests through a deterministic local pattern engine first (`lib/patternIdeator.ts` — 6 templates × ~20 safe scenarios × 5 hook-style phrasings, fully memory-biased), filtering candidates through a 6-axis 0–10 scorer with one rewrite attempt (`lib/ideaScorer.ts`), and only falling back to Claude `generateIdeas` when fewer than 3 local candidates pass the gate. Daily per-creator cache on `creators.last_idea_batch_json` + `last_idea_batch_date` (migration #20) serves same-day repeat requests for free; demo creators bypass cache writes. The orchestrator (`lib/hybridIdeator.ts`) exposes `{ ideas, source: cache|pattern|fallback|mixed, usedFallback, counts }` and the `/api/ideator/generate` route shape is unchanged. Llama 3.1 fallback and Llama 3.2 Vision are deferred to follow-up sessions.
  - **Within-batch diversity (HARD):** `diversifiedSelect` is a four-pass picker (strict → structure-unique → fresh-axis → rescue) gated at score≥8, fed by a cartesian-diagonal weave so every 16-candidate pool covers all 5 hookStyles, all 6 structures, and ≥3 distinct families.
  - **Between-batch regenerate variation (HARD, with rolling history):** When `regenerate=true`, the orchestrator reads a rolling cache history (the most-recent batch + up to `MAX_HISTORY_BATCHES=4` prior batches = 5 batches total) and applies a SPLIT HARD exclusion: every HOOK shipped in the last 5 batches is forbidden (depth 5 — mathematically prevents an identical 3-hook batch from re-appearing), but FAMILY/style exclusion only spans the immediately-prior batch (depth 1 — extending it to depth 5 squeezed the ~20-family pattern pool to ~6 candidates and starved the per-batch axis guards). Older-batch family/topic repetition is handled SOFTLY by the novelty-context penalties. The pattern engine is salted with `((hashEntries(flatHistory) ^ Date.now()) >>> 0) % 997` so each regenerate produces a structurally different (template, scenario, style) starting offset. Claude fallback (when triggered) is hook-excluded too. The cache JSONB envelope is now `{ version: 2, current: [{idea, family, templateId}], history: [batch[], ...] }` — backward-compatible reader (`tryParseCachedEnvelope`) accepts both legacy `Idea[]` and `[{idea, family, templateId}]` shapes. JSONB column means no migration needed for the shape extension.
  - **Novelty-aware selection (SOFT, BOOST + PENALTY):** The greedy selector replaces the four-pass `diversifiedSelect`. Each candidate carries `visualActionPattern` (11-value enum: `kitchen_contradiction`, `desk_avoidance`, `phone_scroll_freeze`, `bedroom_avoidance`, `outfit_check_cut`, `text_message_panic`, `face_reaction_deadpan`, `mirror_self_call_out`, `gym_no_show`, `car_avoidance`, `meal_prep_chaos`) and `topicLane` (5 values: `food_home`, `work_productivity`, `social_texting`, `body_fitness`, `daily_routine`) derived from `scenarioFamily` via `VISUAL_ACTION_BY_FAMILY` / `TOPIC_LANE_BY_FAMILY` lookup tables (`patternIdeator.ts`). `scoreNovelty` (`ideaScorer.ts`) awards 0–5 across 5 dims (hookStyle, scenario, structure, visualAction, topic) compared to the prior batch + the in-progress pick set, but ONLY when `qualityScore≥8` (no quality-rescue). `selectionPenalty` re-applies per-pick demerits with set-based saturation (-2 hookStyle, -3 family, -1 structure, -2 topic, -2 visualAction). The orchestrator uses `selectWithNovelty` (greedy by `quality + novelty + penalty`) with HARD batch guards (never 3× same hookStyle/format/structure, never >2 share family/visualAction/topic); `exhaustiveReselect` (capped at count≤5, top-`count*4` candidates) brute-forces a guard-passing combination if greedy fails. Claude fallback now triggers on EITHER `merged.length<3` OR guard failure; if guards still fail post-Claude, ships best-effort with `hybrid_ideator.guards_failed_shipping_best_effort` warn log. QA: 5 regens → 6/6 unique batches, 0 duplicate hooks, `usedFallback=false`, ≥2 distinct visual scenes + ≥2 distinct hookStyles per batch.
  - **Llama 3.1 hook-mutation layer (v2 quality-first, stateless; Session 4 = scorer-aware prompt + empty-array telemetry):** Bolted on top of the now-frozen pattern engine — `lib/llamaHookMutator.ts` rewrites HOOK (and optionally caption) on the chosen 3-pick batch only AFTER local fallback merge in `hybridIdeator.ts`. Pattern engine still owns ALL structural work (scenarios, structure, filming, shot plan); Llama never touches them. Triggers (priority order): `regenerate`, `templated_openers` (2+ shared opener or family), `recent_history_similarity` (2+ overlap with novelty ctx), `all_pattern_batch`, `borderline_novelty` (hookImpact<2 + total≥6). `pickMutationTargets` caps per trigger then HARD-clamps to ≤5 (regen→top5, templated→top5, history→top3, all_pattern→top2, borderline→filter then top5). One `meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct` chat call via `@workspace/integrations-openrouter-ai` (45s timeout, temp 0.85, 800 max tokens, json_object, ≤3 hookOptions per slot enforced post-parse). Validators (in order): `too_long` (>12) → `too_short` (<3) → `banned_opener` (`pov:|when you|watching|reading|how to`) → `sensitive_content` (dm/bank/password/ssn/salary/venmo/etc) → `abstract_advice` (deserve/learning to/etc) → `incomplete_or_dangling` (validateHook for ≤10, light dangling-only check for 11-12) → `scene_drift` (must share content noun with original setting/family/sceneBeat) → `same_opener` (lookupHookOpener differs). Each surviving rewrite is fed back through `scoreIdea` and only replaces the original if `hookImpact > original` OR `personalFit > original` OR `total ≥ original + 1` (quality-first override) — first winning hookOption per slot wins, remainder skipped. Caption mutation runs independently per slot using the same +1 total or +1 captionStrength rule. On Llama timeout/network/parse failure the entire batch ships unchanged; the OpenRouter client is lazy-initialized via `getOpenRouterClient()` so missing env vars never crash boot. `source` ladder: `pattern` (no fallback, no mutation) → `mixed` (mutation selected at least one rewrite) → `fallback` (all-Claude). Telemetry logged to `hybrid_ideator.llama_mutation`: reason, candidatesSent, optionsReturned, mutationsSelected, costEstimateTokens, rejectedReasonCounts, errored. ZERO schema changes — purely in-memory; cache writes use the mutated batch so next-regen exclusion lists stay accurate. The mutator's `source: "llama_3_1"` flag also naturally suppresses templateId in `toCacheEntries` (which only sets it for `pattern_variation` source). QA: 45/45 unit + integration assertions passing (triggers, validators, end-to-end real Llama call); on real-batch end-to-end, Llama returned 5 valid hook options for a regenerate-triggered batch with 0 mutations selected because none scored strictly better than the strong pattern originals — quality-first override behaved exactly per spec.
  - **Llama cost-control + anti-abuse layer:** Per-creator usage gates layered on top of the hook-mutation pipeline. ZERO schema changes — reuses the existing `usage_counters(creator_id, day, kind, count)` composite-PK table with three new `kind` values (`idea_request` += `result.ideas.length` per generation, `regenerate_request` += 1 per regen attempt regardless of result-count, `llama_call` fire-and-forget +1 per mutator attempt). `lib/usageTracker.ts` owns the layer: DB-backed `incrementUsage` / `getUsageToday` for the daily counters; in-memory `Map<creatorId, number[]>` for the 2-min sliding Llama-call window; in-memory `Map<creatorId, lastTs>` for the rapid-regen cooldown. **Gates (priority order, demo creators bypass everything via the same `creator.isDemo` check the cache and quota paths already use):** (1) HARD LIMIT — route-layer, `regenerate=true && idea_request_count > 100` → 429 with `{ error: "rate_limit_take_a_break", message: "Take a break — come back later for fresh ideas" }`; quota is NOT consumed on this path. (2) RAPID-REGEN COOLDOWN — `acquireRegenSlot(creatorId)` is the atomic check-and-record primitive that returns 0 for the first tap and a randomized 3000-5000ms sleep for the second tap within `<3s`; closes the TOCTOU window two parallel taps would otherwise have with separate read+record calls. (3) THROTTLE — mutator-layer, `>3` Llama calls in the trailing 2-min window → skip mutation with `costControlSkipped: true, skipReason: "throttle_2min"`. The mutator refreshes `ctx.usage.llamaCallsLast2Min` from the live in-memory ring buffer at the top of `maybeMutateBatch` so parallel requests can't all pass against a stale snapshot the route handed them pre-await. (4) DAILY ADAPTATION — probabilistic skip with `Math.random()` priority `adaptation_40` (75% skip when `idea_request_count > 40`) > `adaptation_25` (50% skip when `> 25`). (5) FALLBACK — any cost-control skip ships pattern-engine output unchanged (existing graceful path, no new branches needed). **Mobile error mapping:** `studio.tsx` and `(tabs)/index.tsx` both inspect `ApiError.data` on 429 and surface the verbatim server `message` for `error === "rate_limit_take_a_break"` (rather than the generic `buildErrorMessage` "HTTP 429: …" prefix). **Telemetry:** `ideator.usage` (per request, INFO) logs `creatorId, creatorIsDemo, count, regenerate, cooldownAppliedMs, ideaRequestCountAfter, regenerateRequestCountAfter, llamaCallCountBefore, llamaCallsLast2Min`; `hybrid_ideator.llama_mutation` gains `costControlSkipped, skipReason, ideaRequestCountToday, llamaCallsLast2Min`; `ideator.hard_limit_blocked` and `ideator.cooldown_applied` log when those gates fire. **Deferred (architect-noted, bounded impact):** parallel-request DB-level race on the hard-limit check (would require advisory locks; in practice bounds overshoot to a few extra ideas before the next tap blocks). QA: 30/30 unit + DB-roundtrip assertions passing — gate priority/boundaries, demo bypass, throttle isolation across creators, atomic cooldown under simulated parallel taps, day-bucket UTC date.
  - **Llama 3.2 Vision style-extraction layer (privacy-first, soft-bias only):** Optional on-device→server visual-style learning bolted on top of the imported-videos flow. Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-LLAMA-3-2-VISION-STYLE-EXTRACTION-FROM-USER-VIDEOS-Goal_1777447049198.txt`. **Mobile flow:** after a creator imports a video, the mobile app samples 4 thumbnail frames on-device via `expo-video-thumbnails` at fractional offsets `[0.15, 0.4, 0.65, 0.9]` of duration (fixed-timestamp `[1, 3, 5, 8]s` fallback when duration unknown), reads each as JPEG base64 via `expo-file-system/legacy` (the v19 split: `readAsStringAsync` lives on the legacy import), and POSTs the data URLs to a new server endpoint — NO RAW VIDEO BYTES LEAVE THE PHONE, only sampled thumbnails. `Platform.OS === "web"` short-circuits to `[]` so QA-mode in browser can't crash. Both helpers (`extractVideoFrames.ts`, `uploadVisionFrames.ts`) are fail-open: any error → empty array → upload no-ops; the upload itself is fire-and-forget so onboarding flow timing is unchanged. Only `MvpOnboarding.tsx` wires the upload (BlackHoleUpload + style-twin-train don't POST imported-videos so there's no `id` to attach vision to). **Server flow:** new `POST /api/imported-videos/:id/vision-frames` (`routes/visionStyle.ts`) auths via `resolveCreator`, verifies ownership (`imported_videos.creator_id` must equal caller), validates body `{ frames: 1–5 base64 strings, ≤250KB each }`, then calls `extractStyleFromFrames` (`lib/visionStyleExtractor.ts`) → one multimodal `meta-llama/llama-3.2-11b-vision-instruct` call via `getOpenRouterClient()` (temp 0.2 — classification not creativity, max_tokens 500, 30s timeout, `response_format: json_object`). Result fed through `aggregateVisionStyle` (`lib/visionProfileAggregator.ts`) and persisted to new `creators.vision_style_json` jsonb column (migration #21, additive `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, runs through the existing advisory-locked migration registry — NOT drizzle push). **Privacy posture:** the extractor's free-text `visibleAction` and `privacyRiskReason` fields are DROPPED before persistence (the per-video signal stores enums + booleans only); when the model returns `privacyRisk=true` the entire analysis is suppressed from aggregation but `totalAnalyzed` and `totalDroppedForPrivacy` still bump for transparency (so we can tell the user "we looked at N clips, dropped K for privacy" without lying). `perVideoSignals` capped at `MAX_PER_VIDEO_SIGNALS=10` with FIFO eviction; idempotent on `importedVideoId` (re-POST replaces the existing entry, never double-counts). **Derived hints (≥2/N rule, scaled):** `derivedStyleHints` only computed when `perVideoSignals.length ≥ MIN_VIDEOS_FOR_HINTS=3`; for each category (`preferredFormats`/`Settings`/`Energy`/`Framing`/`ReactionTypes`) we take values appearing in `≥ ceil(window * 0.5)` videos (the 2/3 rule scaled), top-2 per category, `unknown` enum values filtered out so the model's "I can't classify" fallback is never promoted to a "preference". **Bias hookup (SOFT, additive only, scoring-time):** `runHybridIdeator` loads `vision_style_json` alongside the other creator JSON docs (`routes/ideator.ts`) and threads `derivedStyleHints` through `scoreIdea`. `applyVisionBoost` (`lib/ideaScorer.ts`) is the ONE point in the scoring stack vision touches — it can lift `personalFit` from `1 → 2` when `mapPatternSettingToVisionSetting(meta.scenario.setting)` matches `preferredSettings` (bed→bedroom, bathroom→bathroom_mirror; couch/other → null = no boost), but NEVER `0 → anything` (avoids over-weighting borderline candidates) and NEVER subtracts. Boost runs DOWNSTREAM of generation, quality filters, and safety filters — vision can never override an explicit answer, a yes/no signal, or a safety rule, and rolling back the layer is as simple as setting `derivedStyleHints` to empty (boost no-ops). Vision NEVER generates ideas, NEVER writes hooks, NEVER replaces the ideator. **Cost control:** new `vision_call` kind on `usageTracker.UsageKind` (no schema change — `kind` is varchar(32)) with daily cap `VISION_DAILY_CAP=20`; over-cap returns `429 { error: "rate_limit_take_a_break", message: "Take a break — we'll learn from your next videos tomorrow" }` reusing the EXACT existing error key so the mobile error-mapping path (`(tabs)/index.tsx`) surfaces the verbatim server message without an additional client branch. Demo creators bypass both the OpenRouter call (returns a fixed mock analysis so demo onboarding still exercises the aggregation path) AND the counter increment, matching the cost-control layer's demo-bypass posture. **Telemetry:** `vision_style.extracted` (analyzedAt, contentType, setting, privacyRisk, derivedStyleHintsChanged), `vision_style.privacy_dropped` (when `privacyRisk=true`), `vision_style.rate_limited` (over daily cap). **QA:** 42/42 pure-logic assertions passing — extractor JSON parsing + enum clamping + null-on-malformed; aggregator privacy drop + idempotency + FIFO eviction + ≥50% threshold + MIN_VIDEOS_FOR_HINTS gate; scoreIdea boost firing on matching settings, refusing to lift `0`, refusing to fire on unmapped pattern settings (couch), respecting empty-hints state. Architect review: PASS after one fix (429 error key parity with the existing `rate_limit_take_a_break` contract — non-vision-prefixed key so the existing mobile error mapper handles it). E2E test deferred: vision flow only fires on native (web QA short-circuits) and requires a real device + OpenRouter creds — pure-logic harness covers all branches the integration test would.
  - **Script-diversity expansion (7th categorical axis to break "same mental loop" failure):** Layered on top of the novelty selector to fix the failure mode where 3 ideas in a batch — with distinct hookStyles, families, structures, visualActions, and topics — still read as variations of the same video because they share the same narrative shape (e.g. all three are "i thought i would, but actually i didn't" realizations). Spec source: `attached_assets/Pasted-SCRIPT-DIVERSITY-EXPANSION-LARGE-SCRIPT-SYSTEM-Goal-Bre_1777476842045.txt`. ZERO schema changes — derived purely from existing fields, persisted through the existing JSONB cache envelope (legacy entries pre-dating taxonomy resolve via `lookupScriptType` returning `null` so the axis no-ops on cold-start). **Taxonomy:** new `ScriptType` enum (37 values across 6 narrative-shape groups: realization-family, avoidance-family, false-start-family, low-energy-reaction-family, internal-contradiction-family, social/situational-family) + `SCRIPT_TYPES` const array + `SCRIPT_TYPE_CLUSTERS` (two `Set<ScriptType>` keyed groupings: `avoidance` = 4-element cluster, `internal_contradiction` = 5-element cluster — used by the all-3-in-cluster batch-rejection guard). New `Energy` enum (`active`/`low`/`medium`) + `ENERGY_BY_VISUAL_ACTION` lookup derived from the existing 13-value `VisualActionPattern` enum (no scenario-level tagging needed; energy is a property of how the scene is filmed, not what it depicts). `SCRIPT_TYPE_BY_FAMILY` tags each of the 25 scenarios with its primary scriptType (~14 distinct types in active rotation); `SCRIPT_TYPE_OVERRIDES: Partial<Record<TemplateId, Partial<Record<string, ScriptType>>>>` (~17 entries) handles cases where a template fundamentally reshapes narrative — e.g. `expectation_vs_reality × gym → realization` (gym's default is `avoidance`), `routine_contradiction × productivity → internal_vs_external`, `small_panic × texting → quiet_panic`. `resolveScriptType(template, family)` (override → default) used at assembly in `assembleCandidate`; `lookupScriptType(family?, templateId?)` (returns `null` when family missing/unknown — caller skips the candidate's contribution to cross-batch sets) used by `buildNoveltyContext` for cache reads, preserving JSONB legacy safety. `PatternMeta` gains optional `scriptType` + `energy` fields. **Batch guards (HARD, in `batchGuardsPass`):** (a) max-2-same scriptType per batch (3-of-same rejected, like the existing family/visualAction/topic 2-cap); (b) all-3-in-same-cluster rejection (3 picks all from `SCRIPT_TYPE_CLUSTERS.avoidance` or all from `internal_contradiction` rejected even when their scriptType values differ); (c) all-3-low-energy rejection (any batch where all 3 picks have `meta.energy === "low"` is rejected). **Scoring (`scoreNovelty` in `ideaScorer.ts`):** added 8th dim `sctFresh` (+1 when scriptType differs from prior batch + already-picked) + `unusedBoost` (+3 when scriptType ∈ `unusedScriptTypesLast3`) — 0-8 range now. **Penalty (`selectionPenalty`, per-pick stacking):** -2 for shared scriptType in already-picked (within-batch), -3 for scriptType ∈ `recentScriptTypes` (immediate-prior batch only — scope-corrected after architect review), additional -2 for scriptType ∈ `frequentScriptTypesLast3` (appearing in ≥2 of last 3 batches). **History tiers (`buildNoveltyContext` extended signature `(prev, last3Batches=[])`):** `recentScriptTypes` is SCOPED to `last3Batches[0]` (the immediate-prior batch only — NOT the flat 5-batch view the other per-axis sets use, so the -3 penalty and the regen rescue's freshness baseline don't artificially starve picks on a small pool); `frequentScriptTypesLast3` derives from `last3Batches` (≥2-of-3 occurrence); `unusedScriptTypesLast3` = `SCRIPT_TYPES − union(last3Batches)`. Other axes (recentFamilies/styles/topics/visualActions/hookOpeners/settings) keep their established 5-batch scope — strict scope discipline. **Regen rule (`selectWithNovelty` when `regenerate=true`):** after greedy/exhaustive pick, calls `batchHasNewScriptType(batch, recentScriptTypes)`; if false runs ONE additional exhaustive pass with a HARD ≥1-fresh-scriptType constraint; if still impossible ships best-effort with `hybrid_ideator.regen_no_new_scripttype_shipping_best_effort` warn log (matches the existing `guards_failed_shipping_best_effort` pattern). **Generation distribution (`interleaveByScriptType` in `patternIdeator.ts`):** post-processes `generatePatternCandidates` output to bucket candidates by scriptType then round-robin emit, so the first 6+ candidates span ≥6 distinct scriptTypes when the pool naturally allows. SOFT — never drops candidates, only reorders. **QA: 22/22 pure-logic asserts passing** — override-vs-default priority (gym default=`avoidance`, `expectation_vs_reality × gym`=`realization`, `routine_contradiction × productivity`=`internal_vs_external`); back-compat (`null` on missing/unknown family even with templateId, scenario-default fallback on existing-family + missing/unknown templateId); 10-batch run produces 15 distinct scriptTypes across 30 ideas with max single share = `avoidance` @ 13.3% (well under the 40% cap); 3-of-same scriptType + all-3-in-avoidance-cluster + all-3-low-energy all rejected by `batchGuardsPass`; regen with achievable freshness contains ≥1 fresh scriptType; regen with structurally impossible freshness (all candidates forced to one scriptType + that scriptType in recent) → standard guards reject OR rescue-failure warn fires; 16-candidate pool spans 13 distinct scriptTypes with first 6 picks already spanning 6 distinct (interleave round-robin verified). Architect review: PASS after one fix (`recentScriptTypes` scope corrected from flat 5-batch view to immediate-prior-batch-only, matching spec — non-blocking targeted-unit-test suggestions for `buildNoveltyContext` deferred since the fix is correctness-by-construction and the QA harness exercises the downstream paths). **FINAL-spec follow-on (`Pasted-SCRIPT-SYSTEM-FINAL-IMPLEMENTATION-QUALITY-DISTRIBUTION_1777479331391.txt`) layered on top of the above:** (i) **Hard pool-distribution caps (`applyPoolCaps` in `patternIdeator.ts`, run BEFORE `interleaveByScriptType` in `generatePatternCandidates`):** per-scriptType cap = `ceil(N * 0.20)` (≤20% any single scriptType); per-cluster cap = `ceil(N * 0.40)` (≤40% combined for the avoidance OR internal_contradiction cluster — directly addresses the spec §3 "must NOT dominate" callout for avoidance / procrastination / quiet-contradiction by mapping procrastination → avoidance cluster, quiet-contradiction → internal_contradiction cluster). Tail-drop preserves the upstream Cartesian-weave + memory-bias ordering for survivors (overflow entries are skipped, never reordered). No-op for pools ≤5 (any single dominant scriptType is structural at that size). ScriptType-less candidates (legacy / Claude/Llama fallback) bypass per-type/cluster checks but count toward N — preserves cap denominator integrity. (ii) **Soft regen ≥2-fresh upgrade (spec §6, in `selectWithNovelty`):** after the existing hard ≥1-fresh rescue produces `chosen`, if `countNewScriptTypes(chosen, recentScriptTypes) < 2` runs ONE more `exhaustiveReselect` with predicate `countNewScriptTypes(b, recent) >= 2`. Best-effort — silently keeps the 1-fresh pick if no 2-fresh combination exists in the pool; 1-fresh already meets the hard requirement so no warn fires. Only runs when `opts.regenerate === true`. (iii) **Soft ≥1-active preference (spec §7, in `selectWithNovelty`):** after the regen blocks, if `!batchHasActive(chosen)` runs ONE more `exhaustiveReselect` with predicate `batchHasActive(b) && countNewScriptTypes(b, recent) >= minFreshRequired`. The composed predicate is the architect-flagged correctness fix: §7 MUST preserve the freshness invariant of the currently-chosen batch (snapshotted as `minFreshRequired = (regen && recent.size>0) ? countNewScriptTypes(chosen, recent) : 0`) — otherwise §7 could silently downgrade a fresh-batch produced by §6 / hard-rescue into an active-but-0-fresh batch, violating the §6 hard regen guarantee. Runs for both regen and non-regen (non-regen path has `minFreshRequired=0` so it acts as plain `batchHasActive`). New helpers `countNewScriptTypes(batch, recent)` (counts distinct fresh scriptTypes — duplicates of same fresh type count once) and `batchHasActive(batch)` (true iff any pick has `meta.energy === "active"`). User explicitly opted to NOT write 60 new scenarios; instead sceneObjectTag layer tags each existing scenario with one of 53 user-supplied tags + a 5-value env-cluster. **Taxonomy 1 — `archetypeTaxonomy.ts`:** 12 `ArchetypeFamily` ids (`self_deception`, `micro_rituals`, `social_observation`, `object_personality`, `time_distortion`, `inner_monologue`, `escalation`, `weird_habits`, `petty_logic`, `identity`, `low_energy_realism`, `unexpected_competence`) × 10 archetypes each = 120 globally-distinct `Archetype` ids (e.g. `self_deception` family contains `ill_do_it_later`, `fake_productivity`, `pretend_busy`, … `denial_of_obvious`). Hand-tuned `PRIMARY_ARCHETYPE_BY_SCRIPT_TYPE` mapping covers all 37 ScriptType values, all mapped archetypes globally distinct, all 12 families covered (weird_habits assigned via `loop_behavior` since it didn't otherwise have a natural ScriptType anchor). Lookups: `ARCHETYPES_BY_FAMILY`, `FAMILY_BY_ARCHETYPE`. `resolveArchetype(scriptType): { archetype, family } | null` deterministic; `resolveArchetypeLoose` accepts unknown strings (returns null) for legacy/fallback safety. **Taxonomy 2 — `sceneObjectTaxonomy.ts`:** 53 `SceneObjectTag` ids (`fridge`, `sink`, `laundry`, `mirror`, `phone_lock_screen`, … `front_door`) verbatim from user spec, partitioned 1:1 into 5 `SceneEnvCluster` ids (`kitchen`, `bedroom`, `phone_digital`, `outside`, `bathroom`) via total `ENV_CLUSTER_BY_TAG` lookup. `SCENE_OBJECT_TAG_BY_FAMILY` tags each of the 25 existing scenarioFamilies with one primary tag (all 25 mappings distinct, ≥3 distinct env clusters represented across the 25 families). `lookupSceneObjectTag(family)` + `lookupSceneEnvCluster(tag)` + `lookupSceneEnvClusterForFamily(family)` helpers, all null-safe on unknown input. **Plumbing — `PatternMeta` / `CandidateMeta` extension:** `PatternMeta` gains optional `archetype` + `archetypeFamily` + `sceneObjectTag` + `sceneEnvCluster` fields; `CandidateMeta` fallback union (ideaScorer.ts) extended with the same optional fields so Claude/Llama fallback wraps that omit them are type-safe. `assembleCandidate` populates all four via `resolveArchetype(scriptType)` + `lookupSceneObjectTag(family)` (cluster derived from tag via `ENV_CLUSTER_BY_TAG`); only populated when both upstream fields resolve, preserving the established missing-field-skips-axis safety pattern. **Novelty context — `NoveltyContext` extension:** added `recentArchetypes` + `recentArchetypeFamilies` (immediate-prior batch only, mirrors `recentScriptTypes` scoping) + `recentSceneObjectTags` (immediate-prior batch only — for the -3 cross-batch penalty) + `frequentSceneObjectTagsLast3` (≥2-of-3 occurrence — for the -2 stack) + `unusedSceneObjectTagsLast3` (`SCENE_OBJECT_TAGS − union(last3Batches)` — for the +3 boost). `buildNoveltyContext` extended in hybridIdeator.ts to derive these from prev cache + last3 batches via `lookupScriptType` then `resolveArchetype`, plus `lookupSceneObjectTag(family)`; absent on cold-start (preserves null-safe behavior). **Scoring — `scoreNovelty` (now 10-dim):** added `archetypeFresh` (+1 when archetype differs from cross-batch recent + already-picked) and `sceneObjectTagFresh` (+1 when sceneObjectTag differs from cross-batch recent + already-picked) binary dims. PLUS +3 `unusedTagBoost` when sceneObjectTag ∈ `unusedSceneObjectTagsLast3`. Note: NO separate +3 archetype boost — the 1:1 `ScriptType → archetype` derivation makes the existing +3 unused-scriptType boost cover archetype rotation indirectly (archetype freshness is already binary-fresh-tracked via `archetypeFresh`), so a second +3 would double-count. **Penalty — `selectionPenalty` (per-pick stacking):** -4 same archetype within batch (heaviest within-axis penalty in the system — archetype is the spec's headline anti-clone signal); -2 same archetypeFamily within batch (stacks with -4 when same archetype, so archetype-collision actually costs -6); -1 same sceneEnvCluster within batch (lighter than family since cluster is broader — `coffee` + `fridge` are both kitchen-cluster but read as more distinct than two ScriptType-cluster collisions); -3 sceneObjectTag ∈ `recentSceneObjectTags` (immediate-prior cross-batch); -2 sceneObjectTag ∈ `frequentSceneObjectTagsLast3` (stacks with -3 to -5 when both fire). All axes saturate per-pick (no double-count), all skip when fields missing. **Batch guards — 4 NEW HARD rules in `batchGuardsPass` at `batch.length >= 2`:** (d) max-1 archetype per batch (blocks two `ill_do_it_later` picks even when scenarioFamily/hook/scriptType differ — e.g. "I'll clean tomorrow" + "I'll text them tomorrow" = two distinct families but one archetype); (e) max-1 archetypeFamily per batch (stricter — two distinct archetypes from the SAME family, e.g. `ill_do_it_later` + `fake_productivity` both in `self_deception`, still read as the same kind of idea); (f) max-1 sceneObjectTag per batch (two `coffee` or two `unread_messages` picks read as the same physical scene shot twice); (g) max-1 sceneEnvCluster per batch (catches cluster collisions across distinct tags — `coffee` + `fridge` are both kitchen-cluster, feels like one kitchen morning split into two videos). All 4 guards skip when fields missing (legacy / fallback safety — counts toward batch but doesn't trip the guard). **Regen rescue — TWO additional exhaustive passes in `selectWithNovelty` (compose with the existing scriptType-fresh rescue):** (i) when `regenerate && recentArchetypeFamilies.size > 0` and current chosen batch has 0 fresh families, run `exhaustiveReselect` with `extraGuard = batchHasNewArchetypeFamily(b, recent) && (recentScriptTypes.size === 0 || batchHasNewScriptType(b, recent))` — composes the scriptType invariant into the new family invariant so this pass can't silently downgrade a freshly-rescued scriptType batch; warn-and-ship-best-effort with `hybrid_ideator.regen_no_new_archetype_family_shipping_best_effort` log if pool can't satisfy.
