New `lib/trendCatalog.ts`: `TrendItem { id, type: object|behavior|phrase, label, freshnessScore ∈ [0.3,1.0], compatibleFamilies[], compatibleArchetypeFamilies[] }`, `TREND_CATALOG` (27 hand-curated items: 12 objects + 10 behaviors + 5 phrases), `TREND_BY_ID` lookup, `MIN_FRESHNESS = 0.3`, `TREND_INJECTION_RATE_PCT = 30`. **Selector** `selectTrendForCandidate({slotIndex, scenarioFamily, archetypeFamily, salt})`: deterministic FNV-1a `hashTriple` → `bucket = h%100`; `bucket >= 30` → null (gate skips ~70% by design); else filter `getActiveTrends()` by strict `trendFitsCandidate` (BOTH family and archetypeFamily must match — null/undefined inputs ALWAYS reject so cold-start / fallback candidates without resolved derivation pipeline can't accidentally receive a graft); empty fit set → null (NO forced trend); else freshness-weighted pick using upper-16-bits of the same hash for reproducibility. **Caption transform** `applyTrendToCaption(caption, trend, scenarioTopicNoun)`: `object` → first-occurrence substitute of `topicNoun` with `trend.label` (no-op when noun absent — caller's validator catches it as "substitution failed silently"); `behavior` → append ` (${trend.label})` if result ≤ 80-char ceiling, else no-op; `phrase` → append ` — ${trend.label}` if result ≤ 80, else no-op. Idempotent (`f(f(x)) === f(x)`) for all 3 types. **Validation** `validateTrendInjection(original, transformed, isCleanCaption)` rejects when transform was a no-op OR caller-supplied predicate fails. In `assembleCandidate`: `isCleanCaption = lookupBannedHookPrefix||containsGenericFiller||containsVoiceViolation` (substring-only validators — `validateHook` requires 3-10 word count and would false-reject most captions). On rejection: caption REVERTS to original and `meta.trendId` stays undefined — candidate STILL ships (soft skip per spec — never a whole-batch reject). `assembleCandidate` signature gained `slotIndex`/`slotSalt` params (defaults 0/0); resolutions hoisted above `idea` literal so trend selection sees them; inner-loop call site passes `(out.length, scenarioSeed)`. `PatternMeta.trendId?: string` + `CandidateMeta` fallback union extended with same. **Cross-batch novelty** (light): `NoveltyContext.recentTrendIds?: ReadonlySet<string>` populated by `buildNoveltyContext` from immediate-prior batch envelope's `trendId` field directly (no derivation step needed). `selectionPenalty`: -2 when `meta.trendId ∈ recentTrendIds`, single-tier ONLY (no frequent-last-3 stack and no unused-last-3 boost — trends are an OPTIONAL overlay not a forced rotation axis); skips silently when `trendId === undefined` (the ~70%-by-design norm — gate skip + soft-skip both leave trendId undefined and the penalty NEVER fires against an absent tag). Same -2 sizing as voice-profile cross-batch lever (also single-tier) — strong enough to break ties, soft enough that a high-quality pattern with a repeated trend can still win. `toCacheEntries` + `rescueEntries` write trendId; `tryParseEntries` tolerantly parses (any non-empty string passes — catalog is curator-managed and grows/decays without code deploy, so no enum whitelist; empty strings drop to undefined so the Set never holds a `""` sentinel). NO batch guard, NO regen rescue — trends are an OPTIONAL overlay per spec; we never force ≥1 trend per batch. **QA harness** (`__qa_trend_context.ts`, deleted post-green): 6 sections — catalog invariants (27 items, all 3 types, freshness ∈ [0.3,1.0], unique ids, archetype IDs resolve to known taxonomy), `trendFitsCandidate` strict AND + null-input rejection, selector reproducibility (50 inputs same → same) + emission rate (1000 samples = 26.3% — under the ≤30% target) + fit-only emission (0 forced trends when archetype unsupported), `applyTrendToCaption` idempotency + length cap + per-type behavior, `validateTrendInjection` no-op/clean-predicate gating, `selectionPenalty` -2 cross-batch repeat + 0 fresh + missing-field skip + undefined-set skip — all green. Architect re-review with `includeGitDiff=true`: PASS — selector gate structurally `<=30%`, strict fit predicate enforced, soft-skip/revert behavior verified in `assembleCandidate`, NO schema/DB writes (additive JSONB only), cross-batch penalty wiring correct + skip on absent trendId, `tryParseEntries` keeps trendId optional + drops empty/non-string to undefined preserving legacy cache compatibility, `applyTrendToCaption` idempotency + 80-char ceiling enforced, no caption mutation when validator rejects.
  - **QA hardening (anti-clone, scene-specific copy, no broken hooks):** Layered on top of the novelty selector to fix the "different ideas that read like the same video filmed three ways" failure mode. (1) **Hook completeness validator** — `validateHook` rejects hooks ending in dangling words (`and`, `vs`, `with`, `to`, `the`, `my`, `me`, etc.), unsubstituted `${...}` leaks, ellipsis truncation, or word-count outside 3–10. The old `clampHookWords` chop-to-10 is gone; instead `pickValidatedPhrasing` walks all variants for the chosen style and `assembleCandidate` returns `null` if none ship — the generator silently skips that (template, scenario, style) triple. The `tryRewrite` rescue path (`ideaScorer.ts`) likewise iterates every other style + every variant and returns `null` if nothing validates, never truncating. (2) **HookOpener taxonomy + within-batch HARD guard** — new `HookOpener` enum (9 values: `i_just`, `i_really`, `me_saying`, `the_way_i`, `why_did_i`, `pov_check`, `tell_me_why`, `what_i_planned_vs`, `the_audacity`) tagged on each `HookPhrasingEntry` and resolvable from any hook string via `lookupHookOpener` regex table; `batchGuardsPass` HARD-caps each opener at 1/batch (so a batch can't ship three "I just realized…" hooks even when hookStyle differs). (3) **Setting expansion + within-batch HARD guard** — scenario pool grew to 25 entries spanning all 8 settings (`bed`/`couch`/`desk`/`bathroom`/`kitchen`/`car`/`outside`/`other`) — added new families (`skincare`, `mirror_pep_talk`, `walk`, `doom_scroll_car`, `closet_pile`); `batchGuardsPass` HARD-caps each `setting` at 1/batch so three kitchen scenes never ship together. (4) **Per-visualAction `howToFilm`** — `HOW_TO_FILM_BY_VISUAL_ACTION` lookup with 13 framing snippets keyed by `visualActionPattern` replaces the v1 boilerplate "Phone propped at chest height". `batchGuardsPass` also HARD-rejects byte-identical `howToFilm` strings within a batch as defense in depth. (5) **Scene-specific `whatToShow`** — new `sceneBeat` field on every `Scenario` (1–2 sentence physical moment, e.g. "You step in front of the mirror in the new outfit, hold the look for one beat, then turn away") drives `buildWhatToShow`, replacing the generic template. (6) **Cross-batch novelty extension** — `NoveltyContext` gained `recentHookOpeners` (derived from cached hook text via `lookupHookOpener`, zero cache-shape change) and `recentSettings` (from `idea.setting`); `scoreNovelty` is now 0–7 (added opener + setting axes); `selectionPenalty` adds -2 same-opener and -2 same-setting. **QA gate (5 regens, deleted post-pass):** every hook validated, no 2+ openers per batch, no 2+ settings per batch, no identical `howToFilm`, all `whatToShow` ≥20 chars + scene-specific, no v1 boilerplate substring, `source: "pattern"` and `usedFallback: false` on all 5 batches.
  - **Trend context layer + archetype pairing system:** Lightweight cultural-relevance overlay so the deterministic engine doesn't sound stuck-in-2023, layered on top of the novelty selector + QA validators without any schema/cache shape changes. (1) **Curated catalog (`trendCatalog.ts`)** — 31 hand-curated `TrendItem`s spanning 4 types: `object` (substitute the scenario topic noun, e.g. "matcha" replacing "coffee"), `behavior` (parenthetical append, e.g. "(stanley cup obsession)"), `phrase` (em-dash append, e.g. " — quiet luxury"), and `format` (parenthetical append describing a video format, e.g. "(voice memo style)"). Each item carries `compatibleFamilies` (positive scenario fit), `compatibleArchetypeFamilies` (positive archetype fit), `freshnessScore ∈ [0.3, 1.0]`, optional `region` (creator-locale gate), and optional `avoidArchetypeFamilies` (negative compat — hard-rejects e.g. matcha + social_observation, stanley_cup + escalation, tiktok_dance_format + low_energy_realism). (2) **Strict-fit selector** — `selectTrendForCandidate` hashes `(slotIndex, scenarioFamily, salt)` into a 100-bucket gate; `bucket >= 30` returns null (caps emission rate at 30%). Surviving candidates are filtered by `trendFitsCandidate` (negative compat hard-reject FIRST, then positive scenario + archetype fit, then optional region match with global-default semantics — either side absent → accept). Final pick is freshness-weighted via the upper-16-bits of the same hash, fully deterministic for cache replay. (3) **Caption injection + soft-skip validator** — `applyTrendToCaption` is pure/idempotent with a tight 80-char ceiling per type; `validateTrendInjection` rejects no-op transforms (`original === transformed`) AND any transform that fails the caller's `isCleanCaption` predicate (banned-prefix / generic-filler / voice-violation). Soft-skip: when validation fails, the candidate STILL ships, just without the trend tag (no whole-batch rejection — trends are an OPTIONAL overlay). **Frequency tuning (Session 3 — spec source `attached_assets/Pasted-TREND-FREQUENCY-TUNING-SAFE-MOVE-TOWARD-20-Goal-Increas_*.txt`):** moved Session 2's freshness-weighted random pick to a 0–10 best-score selector to lift visible emission from ~12% into the 15–25% target band WITHOUT forcing weak pairings. ZERO schema changes — purely additive optional fields on `TrendItem`. (a) **Schema additions** — `secondaryFitArchetypes` / `secondaryFitFamilies` (relaxed positive fit, only consulted when primary pool empty), `avoidFamilies` (negative scenario compat — hard-rejected by predicate alongside existing `avoidArchetypeFamilies`), `niche` flag (-2 score penalty for too-online/reference-locked items like labubu + delulu_planning). (b) **Selector overhaul** — `selectTrendForCandidate` keeps the 30% hash-bucket gate, then builds a PRIMARY pool via `trendFitsCandidate`; if empty, falls back to a SECONDARY pool via the new `trendFitsCandidateSecondary` predicate (union of secondary + primary fit lists, same hard-reject discipline). Every candidate scored via NEW exported `scoreTrendFit(trend, scenarioFamily, archetypeFamily, region?, recentTrendIds?)`: +4 primary archetype, +3 primary family, +2 secondary archetype (only if no primary archetype matched), +1 secondary family (only if no primary family matched), +1 region/global (predicate-pass implicit), +1 freshness ≥ 0.7, -5 avoid (defensive double-defense), -3 weak fit (BOTH primaries missing), -3 decorative phrase/format with no archetype anchor, -2 niche, -2 repeated trend (`recentTrendIds` accepts `Set` OR readonly array, narrowed via `Array.isArray`). Threshold `TREND_FIT_THRESHOLD = 6`; sub-threshold candidates skipped (return null rather than ship a forced graft). Highest-score wins; ties broken deterministically by `(hash >>> 16) % tied.length`. (c) **Catalog tightening** — `girl_dinner` removed `identity` from `compatibleArchetypeFamilies` and added `avoidFamilies: ["productivity","errands","emails"]` per spec ("girl dinner avoids productivity / to-do list / planning / work-task"); secondary tags added to `hot_girl_walk`, `quiet_luxury`, `fake_busy_mode`, `voice_memo_format` so the secondary pool has live coverage; `niche: true` on `labubu` + `delulu_planning`. (d) **Validation** — pure-logic harness `__qa_trend_tuning.ts` (deleted post-pass — 203/203 PASS) covered score-boundary matrix (every bonus/penalty), threshold gating (6 keep / 5 reject), `girl_dinner` full archetype matrix × 3 forbidden families, secondary fallback discipline (only consulted when primary empty, never stacks on top), per-combo simulation across 5000 random samples (18.7% emission — squarely in 15-25% band), all Session 1+2 invariants preserved (idempotency, region matrix, hard cap, format type, ~30% gate, no positive ∩ negative overlap). Runtime QA across 10 batches (mixed regions western/india/philippines/nigeria, count 3+5, regenerate=true, full-catalog label net): **17.5% rate (7/40 ideas)**, zero `girl_dinner` + productivity-flavor pairings, hard cap held in all 10 batches, 4 distinct trends fired (`zara_dress`, `girl_dinner`, `lazy_GRWM`, `doomscroll_arc`), all 4 regions covered. Architect verdict: PASS — no HIGH defects; predicate ↔ score semantic consistency confirmed; tie-break deterministic and modulo-bias-immaterial; `recentTrendIds` union-narrowing correct. (4) **Within-batch HARD CAP (`enforceTrendCap` in `hybridIdeator.ts`)** — finalization pass enforces ≤ N-1 trend-injected candidates per N-pick batch (so a 3-pick batch can never ship 3-of-3 trended). When the cap fires, the LOWEST-priority trend-injected candidate has `meta.trendId` cleared AND its caption reverted from `meta.originalCaption` (a paired snapshot captured by `assembleCandidate` at injection time) — the candidate STILL ships, just untagged. Priority semantics: main path uses `score.total` (drops lowest-scoring), rescue path uses `-i` (drops last in slice). Cap formula `Math.max(1, n-1)` allows single-pick batches to carry 1 trend. (5) **Cross-batch novelty lever** — `meta.trendId` persisted on the JSONB cache envelope alongside `voiceProfile` / `hookLanguageStyle`; `buildNoveltyContext` reads `recentTrendIds` from the immediate-prior batch and `selectionPenalty` applies -2 demotion so the same trend doesn't dominate back-to-back generations. **QA harness (`__qa_trend_pairing.ts`, deleted post-pass — 39/39 PASS):** format type produces parenthetical + idempotent + length-capped; avoidArchetypeFamilies hard-rejects (predicate-only); region matrix (US/US accepts, US/EU rejects, none/EU accepts, US/none accepts, none/none accepts); selector emission rate ≈ 30% over 1000 samples within ±5pp band; catalog invariants (≥28 items, all 4 types present, no positive ∩ negative archetype overlap, freshness ∈ [0.3, 1.0], TREND_BY_ID coverage); enforceTrendCap (3-of-3 → drops exactly 1, 2-of-3 no-op, 0-trend no-op, 1-pick allows 1, rescue drops LAST); idempotency for all 4 types + validator soft-skip rejects/accepts. **Architect verdict:** PASS — no medium/severe defects; pairing semantics sound; trendId ↔ originalCaption pairing preserved across `tryRewrite` / `maybeMutateBatch` (both spread `meta`); `final` const→let reassignment correctly propagates capped state to cache write + source counters.
- Users provide "Yes / Maybe / No" feedback on ideas, influencing future generation and trending boards.
- AI-generated ideas are the sole primary entry into the filming/create flow.
- The import stage supports adding 1-2 clips with "Film" or "Upload" options.
- The "Ready to post?" stage confirms video readiness with hook + clip + caption and offers "Export video" or "Make another version."
- Film-screen UX includes a "Why this works" block derived from idea metadata.
- Camera permission denial is handled gracefully, allowing users to upload instead.
- Four fixed timing templates are deterministically selected based on the Ideator's `templateHint`.
- **Enhancement Brain:** Provides up to 3 typed suggestions (caption, hook, start hint, manual) for video improvement, reusing style derivation and viral pattern memory.
- **Semi-auto Suggestion Apply:** Allows applying suggestions with immediate visual feedback in the Before/After frame, triggering an `applied_enhancement` signal.
- **Semi-auto Edit (stitch + trim):** Offers `stitch_clips` and `trim_start` actions with visual confirmation in the Before/After frame. No on-device video processing; changes are intent-only for future processing.
- **QA-mode onboarding bypass:** Allows skipping onboarding for e2e tests.
- **Visible adaptation flow (Quick Tune):** A 3-step auto-advancing flow (format → tone → hook) that biases idea generation based on user preferences, with visual feedback and a "Better match?" prompt.
- **Quick Tune onboarding trigger:** Triggers the Quick Tune flow based on client-side state after a certain number of ideas are viewed or scrolled.
- **Daily-habit copy lock:** Home screen H1 and sub are locked to "3 ideas for today" / "Made for your style." Daily return messages vary based on user history.
- **Single-idea swipe feed (preview):** New `/feed` route renders one idea at a time via `SwipeIdeaCard` (hero hook + non-numeric viral-feel badge + pattern preview + why-it-works). Static visual-direction pass — no gestures, no reaction persistence, no backend changes; reuses `dailyIdeasCache` with a built-in mock fallback. Existing tab nav untouched.
- **PHASE X — Default Taste Engine (Steps 1+2):** Backend lever that biases the existing 3-layer Ideator pipeline toward premise-first comedy. New `defaultTasteProfile.ts` is the single source of truth for mechanism/joke-shape/language taste mappings. Layer-2 `filterAndRescore` adds a bounded boost (cap +4) to candidates whose `premiseStyleId`, `hookLanguageStyle`, and `usedBigPremise` flags align with the profile (the +1.5 `PREMISE_FIRST_BONUS` is the dominant lever). Layer-3 (`ideaGen.ts`) Claude fallback prompt now requires a `premise` sentence FIRST, then derives hook + trigger + reaction + whatToShow + howToFilm from it; `premise` is added to `ideaSchema` as optional and stripped from the public API response (server-internal, same pattern as `meta.viralFeelScore`). PART 4 anti-loop (last-5 domains/mechanisms) was already implemented via the existing `MAX_HISTORY_BATCHES=4` + `recentPremiseStyleIds`/`recentFamilies` machinery — no code change required.
- **PHASE X2 — Default Taste Engine completion (heuristic, no LLM verifier).** New `comedyValidation.ts` adds three deterministic gates that fire inside `filterAndRescore` after scoring + DefaultTaste boost but before the score-floor cut: (1) PART 1 hard comedy validation requires ≥2 of {tension, contradiction, intention/reality clash, escalation, specific behavior, identity exposure, self-as-other framing} via regex, plus a softness-token rejection; vacuous-passes Layer-1 candidates whose `source === "pattern_variation"` OR `usedBigPremise === true` (curated catalog IS comedy ground truth). (2) PART 2 alignment guarantee: `whatToShow` must share ≥2 content tokens (length-3+ alphanum, stop-words removed) with the hook OR trigger individually (not summed); `howToFilm` must share ≥1 with `whatToShow`; when `idea.premise` is present (Layer-3 only), the hook must share ≥1 token with the premise. (3) PART 4 anti-copy guard fingerprints normalized hooks against ~200 curated `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS.executions[].example` strings (lazy module-scope cache via `loadSeedHookFingerprints`); pattern_variation candidates exempt because they ARE the seed corpus by design. Premise-skeleton dup check uses a `recentPremises` set built from the last-5 cached batches' `idea.premise` fields, threaded into both local + Claude-fallback `filterAndRescore` calls from `hybridIdeator`. PART 3 cross-batch mechanism demotion bumped from -2 to -3 in `selectionPenalty` so a repeat fine-grained `premiseStyleId` stacks with the bucket-level -2 (combined -5 vs typical 3-4pt premise-vs-alt spread). PART 5 fail-open: no retry loop — the existing rescue path in `hybridIdeator` (final.length===0 ⇒ ship unfiltered top-of-pool) absorbs over-rejection. PART 6 telemetry: `FilterAndRescoreResult.rejectionReasons` per-reason counters surfaced in a new `hybrid_ideator.validation_summary` info log (always fires) and added to the existing `guards_failed_shipping_best_effort` warn log. PART 7 QA: 5-batch smoke against demo creator confirms 14/16 keep rate with measurable rejections (`hook_scenario_mismatch`, `filming_mismatch`) and zero empty batches. NO UI changes. NO Premise Core Library yet.
- **PHASE Y2 — Layer-1 Core-Aware Wiring (additive, surgical, NO UI/DB/schema changes).** Layered on PHASE Y to lift premise-core coverage from the Y1 baseline of ~3% (2/75 ideas) to ~9% (5/57 ideas) by promoting the Claude-with-cores call onto the PRIMARY `regenerate=true` path instead of only firing on Layer-1 underfill / guards-fail. When Claude short-delivers, the merge falls back to today's behavior (claudeKept ∪ localKept). The promotion-vs-merge decision is recorded in `promotionReason` (`claude_solo_promoted` / `merged_core_aware_short` / `merged_local_only_short`). **`hybridIdeator.ts` PART 1c (core-priority swap, post-architect-iteration fix):** added a post-`selectWithNovelty` swap phase that forcibly displaces the lowest-scored non-core picks with any core-tagged Claude candidate from `merged` that didn't make the cut. Required because the +2 fresh-core scorer lever (`ideaScorer.ts` L3186-3192) self-suppresses on cold-start when `recentPremiseCoreIds.size === 0` — meaning the very batches we need to bootstrap core coverage on are also the ones where core-tagged candidates get ZERO selection bias against the local pattern pool's same-hook duplicates (e.g. `"i ghosted my own to-do list"` scoring composite ~10 vs core-tagged candidates' ~3). The Y2 round-1 QA (without the swap) shipped 1/57 = 1.8% core-tagged WORSE than Y1 baseline; round-2 (with the swap) shipped 5/57 = 8.8% — 3× Y1 baseline. Telemetry: new `phase_y2.core_priority_swap` info log on every fired swap with `swappedIn` / `coreIdsAdded` / `postCoreCount` fields. **`ai.ts` (SDK timeout):** added `timeout: 60_000` + `maxRetries: 1` to the `Anthropic` SDK constructor — without this, a stalled Claude call inherited the SDK's ~10min default which hung Y2 batches in `top-up`. Caller code already has graceful try/catch degradation; this just bounds the wait so undercount can fall through to local-pool top-up cleanly. **QA verification (`POST /api/_qa/phase-y2` temp route, 11 batches: 8×regenerate=true count=6 + 3×regenerate=false count=3, 57 shipped ideas total, JSON saved /tmp/qa_phase_y2.json):** `premiseCoreId` coverage 5/57 = 8.8% vs Y1 3% (3× lift, all 5 from regenerate-only slots = 5/48 = 10.4% on the regen path); top hook repeat 10× ("i ghosted my own to-do list") vs Y1 14×; cheap-path `regenerate=false` batches (8/9/10) shipped 0 core-tagged ideas as designed (preserves sub-second latency); 3 core-priority swaps fired across 8 regen batches contributing to the 5 shipped core ideas in 3 distinct batches; per-batch claudeKept variability remains the binding ceiling (Claude returns 1-3 valid candidates per call after `applyExclusionToFallback` + `filterAndRescore`, then top-up adds 1-2 more — net mean 0.6 per batch). Heuristic post-worthy (59.6%) and hook/scenario mismatch (80.7%) numbers used a strict programmatic 5+char-shared-noun rubric and are NOT directly comparable to Y1's 9% / 21% manual review numbers — the trustworthy comparators are the `premiseCoreId` coverage delta and top-hook repeat count. **Architect review (PASS, no blockers):** wiring is correct, telemetry fires, cheap path preserved, swap logic is bounded (only displaces non-core picks). The remaining ceiling is Claude's post-validation survival rate (out of scope for Y2 — flagged for a Y3 follow-up: rewrite the local pattern catalog's top scorers to stop dominating the merge OR tag the local pool's pattern variations with synthesized premise-core ids OR route a fixed slot quota to core-tagged candidates in `selectWithNovelty` itself). **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phase-y2` route file (`_qaPhaseY.ts`) + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; route returns 404 post-cleanup; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. - **PHASE Y — Premise Core Library (additive, surgical, NO UI changes).** Adds 40 ultra-refined comedic-engine "cores" (8 families × 5) as the PRIMARY seed for the LLM (Layer-3 / Claude-fallback) generation path, working WITH (not replacing) `defaultTasteProfile.ts` + the 50-id `PremiseStyle` layer + the Layer-1 `pattern_variation` catalog. Spec source: in-session prompt — "PHASE Y PREMISE CORE LIBRARY". Pure TS-additive; ZERO schema changes; ZERO Phase 3-7 / Phase 6-series / Phase X / Phase X2 / hard-validator / cache-shape-breaking / scoring-philosophy changes; Layer-1 batches NEVER see cores (cores only injected on the Claude fallback path so the curated catalog remains untouched ground truth). **NEW MODULE `premiseCoreLibrary.ts` (~1255 lines):** exports `PremiseCore` type, `PremiseCoreFamily` union (`self_betrayal`, `absurd_escalation`, `self_as_relationship`, `adulting_chaos`, `dopamine_overthinking`, `social_mask`, `confident_vs_real`, `identity_exposure`), and `PREMISE_CORES` — `Object.freeze`d array of EXACTLY 40 cores (5-per-family invariant asserted at module load alongside count===40, unique-id, and `compatiblePremiseStyles ⊆ PREMISE_STYLE_IDS` checks). Each core carries `id` / `family` / `mechanism` / `tension` / `description` / `generatorRule` (the rule the LLM must use to write the premise sentence) / `compatibleDomains` / `compatiblePremiseStyles` / `examples` (2-3 anti-copy seeds — explicitly forbidden phrasings) / `antiCopyHints`. `FAMILY_DEFAULT_TASTE_WEIGHT` mirrors the `defaultTasteProfile.ts` mechanism-weight bias so the selector's family-level prior aligns with the system's existing taste prior without re-encoding it. **Selector (`selectPremiseCores`):** weighted-without-replacement draw with three stacked recency demotions — id-recency ×0.2 (last-5 batches' core ids), mechanism-recency ×0.4 (last-5 batches' mechanisms), per-pick family-demotion ×0.5 (re-applied after each pick to discourage same-family back-to-back inside the seed set), all clamped to a `>=0.01` floor so the picker never starves. Post-pick the selector enforces a `≥1 fresh core` invariant when `recentIds.size > 0`: if all picks are recently-seen, the selector swaps the lowest-effective-weight pick for the highest-effective-weight unpicked-and-fresh candidate using the SAME composite (family taste × id-recency × mechanism-recency × accumulated family-demotion) the main draw uses (post-architect-review fix — earlier draft used raw family weight which mis-aligned the swap with the rest of the picker). Returns `{ cores, hasFreshCore }`. `formatPremiseCoresForPrompt(cores)` renders the SYSTEM-prompt block listing each core's id / family / mechanism / tension / generatorRule / compatibleDomains / forbidden-seed-phrasings (built from `examples`) / anti-copy hints, with the explicit instruction header forbidding example-phrasing regurgitation. `_resetPremiseCoreStateForTests()` ships as a no-op forward-compat seam (the catalog is frozen with no module-scope mutable state today). **`ideaGen.ts` integration:** `ideaSchema` gains optional `premiseCoreId: z.string().min(1).max(120).optional()` (server-internal — same strip-from-public-response discipline as `premise`). `GenerateIdeasInput` gains `premiseCoreSeeds?: readonly PremiseCore[]`. The system prompt array prepends `premiseCoreBlock` (rendered via `formatPremiseCoresForPrompt`) ABOVE the existing PHASE X premise-first instructions; when seeds are absent the block is `""` and `.filter(Boolean)` collapses it to a no-op. Both `=== TASK ===` JSON-shape directives (the count==1 path at L1100 and the count>1 path at L1271) list `premiseCoreId` alongside `premise` so the model knows to emit the chosen core's id back. **`routes/ideator.ts`:** L305 destructure now strips `premiseCoreId` alongside `premise` from the public response (verified: shipped JSON contains neither field). **`hybridIdeator.ts`:** imports `selectPremiseCores` + `getPremiseCoreById`. `wrapFallbackIdea` mirrors `idea.premiseCoreId` → `meta.premiseCoreId` so the scorer's meta-accessor sees it on Claude-fallback candidates (Layer-1 catalog candidates never carry the field). `buildNoveltyContext` populates `recentPremiseCoreIds` from `last3Batches` reading `e.idea.premiseCoreId` directly off the cached envelope (NO cache-shape change — pre-PHASE-Y rows simply contribute nothing, since the field is opportunistically read as `undefined`). Pre-Claude-fallback the function builds `recentPremiseCoreIdsForSeeding` + `recentMechanismsForSeeding` from a `last5BatchesForPremises` window and calls `selectPremiseCores({ count: desiredCount + 2, recentCoreIds, recentMechanisms })`, threads `coreSelection.cores` into `generateIdeas` via `premiseCoreSeeds`, and emits a `phase_y.premise_cores_selected` info log (always when fallback fires) with `selectedCoreIds` / `selectedFamilies` / `recentCoreCount` / `recentMechanismCount` / `hasFreshCore`. **`ideaScorer.ts`:** `CandidateMeta` Claude-fallback branch gains optional `premiseCoreId?: string`; new `metaPremiseCoreId` accessor mirrors `metaPremiseStyleId`. `NoveltyContext` gains optional `recentPremiseCoreIds?: ReadonlySet<string>`. `selectionPenalty` adds a -3 cross-batch demotion when the candidate's `meta.premiseCoreId` is in `recentPremiseCoreIds` and a +2 fresh-core boost when it's not — exactly mirroring the existing `premiseStyleId` -3/+2 lever (so a Claude wrap that re-uses BOTH a core AND a premiseStyleId from a recent batch eats -6, while a fresh-on-both wrap gains +4; intentionally aggressive rotation given the +3 PREMISE_PREFERENCE bonus + typical 1-2pt scoring spread, treated as a deliberate calibration lever). **QA verification:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server run typecheck` clean; 5 sequential normal batches all HTTP 200 with 3 ideas each (no Layer-1 regression); forced-fallback batch (`count=6, regenerate=true`) HTTP 200 with 6 ideas, `phase_y.premise_cores_selected` log fired with `seedCount=8` (=6+2), 8 distinct cores spanning 7 of 8 families, `hasFreshCore=true`, and the `usedFallback=true / fallbackKept=2` validation summary confirming the cores propagated into the Claude prompt and produced shipping ideas; public response keys exclude both `premise` and `premiseCoreId`. **Architect review (PASS, no blockers):** core library integrity strong, selector math sound (non-starvation guaranteed), integration surgical/additive, cache compatibility correct (pre-PHASE-Y rows tolerate the new field's absence), score-stack magnitude flagged as a deliberate calibration lever; one non-blocking math fix (fresh-swap effective-weight alignment) applied in this same task. - **PHASE Y4 — Strengthened Cross-Batch Repeat Penalties (additive, surgical, NO UI/DB/schema changes).** Layered on PHASE Y3 to fix the Y3 top-hook regression (Y2 10× → Y3 14× because Y3's D-lite +3 cap left `min(+7,+3) − 2 = +1` still positive — capped premium hooks still beat neutral legacy 0). Pure selection-pressure tightening; ZERO mapping / library / Claude / quota / UI / API / schema / cache-shape / scoring-philosophy / Phase 3-7 / Phase 6-series / Phase X-series / Phase Y-series changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged); LLM cost flat. **`ideaScorer.ts` `selectionPenalty` (PART 1 — strengthen recent-id demotes):** the existing per-axis cross-batch demotes were tightened in place — `premiseStyleId` recent: `−3 → −5`; `executionId` recent: `−2 → −5`; `premiseCoreId` recent: `−3 → −5`. Symmetric `+2` fresh-axis boosts kept unchanged so a fresh creator's first batches still get the cold-start premium. Y3 D-lite `Math.min(baseBoost, 3)` cap on `premiseComedyBoost` PRESERVED unchanged — the Y3 lever is still useful as the upper bound on the boost itself. **PART 2 — combo demote when style + execution both recent:** new `if (styleRecent && execRecent) p −= 4;` block immediately after the per-axis blocks; fires even when the candidate's `premiseCoreId` is fresh, so a same-(style, execution) shell with a different core still loses to a fresh neutral candidate. **PART 3 — near-shell demote when style + execution + core ALL recent:** stacks an additional `if (coreRecent) p −= 4;` inside the same combo block (only fires when PART 2 already fired), so a complete (style, execution, core) re-pick is the worst-case candidate the selector can see. Combined worst-case math (documented in JSDoc): score-10 premium with all three axes recent and D-lite cap engaged = `min(+7, +3) − 5 − 5 − 5 − 4 − 4 = −20` (strictly loses to fresh neutral legacy 0); fresh-axis premium unchanged at `+7` (still wins vs fresh legacy `+5`). **`hybridIdeator.ts` telemetry on existing `hybrid_ideator.served` log (additive, no new event):** 5 new fields appended to the served log — `selectedRepeatedPremiseStyleCount` / `selectedRepeatedExecutionCount` / `selectedRepeatedPremiseCoreCount` / `selectedSameStyleExecutionCount` / `selectedSameStyleExecutionCoreCount`. Computed in-memory from `final[]` ∩ `noveltyContext.recent*` sets at zero LLM cost; the (style+exec+core)-all-recent counter is the binding acceptance metric (a near-shell shipped despite stacked −20 demote = penalty failure). The early `source: "cache"` return path emits the same five fields with literal `0` values so the served-log schema is identical across all paths (cache replay doesn't run `selectionPenalty` against a fresh novelty context, so the counters aren't measurable there — emitting 0 keeps downstream parsers / dashboard aggregations correct without NPE on missing keys). **QA verification (`POST /api/_qa/phaseY` temp route, 15 batches: 10×regenerate=true count=6 + 5×regenerate=false count=6, 77 shipped ideas total — 13 short of 90 due to harness-side daily AI cost cap exhaustion mid-run, JSON saved `.local/reports/qa_phase_y4.json` + report `.local/reports/phase_y4_report.md` + computed metrics `.local/reports/y4_metrics.json`):** **top hook repeat 6 vs Y3 14 (−57%) ✅ — Y3 regression undone.** All 15 served events emit the new selected-set counters; across the full run, sum of `selectedSameStyleExecutionCount` = 0, `selectedSameStyleExecutionCoreCount` = 0, `selectedRepeatedPremiseCoreCount` = 0 (zero near-shells shipped — exact spec PART 6 acceptance); `selectedRepeatedExecutionCount` = 1 in 2 of 15 events, 0 elsewhere; `selectedRepeatedPremiseStyleCount` = 0 across all 15. Distinct hooks 43/77 = 55.8% (vs Y3 30.0% — +25 pp). Honest caveats called out in report: (1) daily AI cap (`$10.0992 of $10.00`) hit at batch ~6 — subsequent batches degraded to local+fallback only, dropping `premiseCoreId` coverage from Y3 baseline 40.0% → 16.9% (cap-driven, NOT a Y4 regression), and (2) batches #11-14 served from same-day cache (`durationMs: 0`) so the normal slice's apparent variety is effectively n=1 — both artefacts are harness-level, not Y4-changes-level, but they mean the cap-driven rows of the delta table (latency / coverage / underfill) are NOT informative deltas vs Y3. **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phaseY` route file (`_qaPhaseY.ts`) + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; route returns 404 post-cleanup; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6B / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E / Phase 6F / Phase 7 / Phase X / Phase X2 / Phase Y / Phase Y2 / Phase Y3 all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent catalog / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes, no UI changes; public response keys still exclude both `premise` and `premiseCoreId`.
- **PHASE Y3 — Local-Pool premiseCoreId Tagging + D-lite Boost Cap (additive, surgical, NO UI/DB/schema changes).** Layered on PHASE Y2 to lift premise-core coverage from the Y2 baseline of 8.8% (5/57 ideas) to 40.0% (36/90 ideas — 4.5× lift) by deterministically tagging local pattern-pool (Layer-1) candidates with a `premiseCoreId` synthesized from a high-confidence `(premiseStyleId, executionId) → premiseCoreId` lookup table, AND capping runaway `premiseComedyBoost` at +3 (D-lite) when the candidate's premise style/execution is already in the recent set. ZERO schema / DB / UI / cache-shape / Phase 3-7 / Phase 6-series / Phase X / Phase X2 / Phase Y / Phase Y2 / hard-validator / scoring-philosophy / LLM-cost changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged). **`lib/premiseCoreLocalMapping.ts` (new module):** exports a 41-entry frozen `LOCAL_CORE_MAPPING_ENTRIES` tuple list + a derived `Map<string, string>` keyed `${premiseStyleId}::${executionId}` → `premiseCoreId`, plus a pure deterministic `resolvePremiseCoreIdForLocalCandidate({ premiseStyleId, executionId })` resolver returning `string | undefined`. Mapping is conservative: a pair is mapped only when its `premiseStyleId` appears in the chosen core's `compatiblePremiseStyles[]` allow-list AND the `executionId` semantics align with the core's `mechanism` / `tension` (verified against `premiseCoreLibrary.ts` source). 8 distinct premiseStyleIds × 4-5 executions = 41 high-confidence pairs covering the most prolific premium catalog families (`todo_termination` / `procrastination_paradox` / `self_destruction_speedrun` / `self_sabotage_scrollstop` / `main_character_meltdown` / `mundane_meltdown` / `overdramatic_reframe` / `collapse_core` / `duality_clash` / `dream_disappointment` / `pattern_exposure` / `self_roast_reactor`); ambiguous pairs (e.g. `burnout_betrayal × metaphor_mayhem`, `dopamine_denial × *`) deliberately left unmapped — telemetry surfaces them for follow-up. **Boot-time drift validation (cycle-safe):** the mapping module deliberately has ZERO runtime import on `premiseCoreLibrary.ts` — only `import type { PremiseStyleId }` from `patternIdeator.ts` (erased at emit). Any runtime back-edge would close a 3-way cycle on the hot path (`patternIdeator → premiseCoreLocalMapping → premiseCoreLibrary → patternIdeator`) whose worst case is ESM partial-snapshot TDZ on whichever module the entry point loads first. Drift detection moved to an exported `validateLocalCoreMappingAgainst(cores)` function called once from `src/index.ts` `boot()` BEFORE `runMigrations()` + `app.listen()` — the api-server refuses to start (boot().catch logs + exits) if any mapped `premiseCoreId` is missing from `PREMISE_CORES`. Earlier draft tried lazy first-call validation; architect review surfaced that the static `import { PREMISE_CORES }` participates in module resolution itself (not just first-read), so the lazy guard could not actually neutralize the cycle — only removing the runtime import edge does. **`patternIdeator.ts` wiring (additive):** new optional `premiseCoreId?: string` field on `PatternMeta` (with detailed JSDoc explaining the cache-resident `idea.premiseCoreId` mirror vs the runtime-only `meta.premiseCoreId` mirror — same value, two surfaces). `assembleCandidate` computes `localPremiseCoreId` once via `resolvePremiseCoreIdForLocalCandidate` (returns undefined when entry is not `bigPremise`, when either fine-grained tag is missing, or when the pair is intentionally unmapped); spread-when-present onto BOTH `idea.premiseCoreId` (cache-resident, picked up by `buildNoveltyContext`'s existing `e.idea.premiseCoreId` read site introduced in PHASE Y for Layer-3 Claude candidates — no envelope-shape change required) AND `meta.premiseCoreId` (runtime-only, mirrors hybridIdeator's existing meta.premiseCoreId mirroring at the Claude wrap site for in-flight `recentCoreIds` rescue-filter dedup). **`ideaScorer.ts` D-lite cap:** the existing unconditional `premiseComedyBoost(c.meta.premiseComedyScore?.total)` at the `usedBigPremise` site is now wrapped in a recent-id check — when `c.meta.premiseStyleId` is in `ctx.recentPremiseStyleIds` OR `c.meta.executionId` is in `ctx.recentExecutionIds` (same OR-discipline as the existing `-2` cross-batch demote levers below), the boost is capped via `Math.min(baseBoost, 3)`; fresh entries get the full boost unchanged. JSDoc block walks through the math: fresh score-10 premium = +7 (preferred over fresh legacy +5); recent score-10 premium = `min(+7, +3) − 2 = +1` (loses to fresh legacy +5, ties / wins vs neutral legacy 0); fresh score-5 = -2 unchanged; recent score-5 = `min(-2, +3) − 2 = -4` (unchanged demote). **`hybridIdeator.ts` telemetry on existing `hybrid_ideator.served` log:** 5 new fields appended (no new event) — `localPremiseCoreTaggedCount` (count of `pattern_variation` candidates with `usedBigPremise === true` AND a resolved `meta.premiseCoreId`), `localPremiseCoreTaggedRate` (tagged / (tagged + unmapped-with-fine-grained-tags)), `localPremiseCoreUnmappedCount` (premium with both fine-grained tags but no resolved core — the actionable signal), `mappedPremiseCoreIds` (array of distinct cores resolved this batch), and `topUnmappedPremiseHooks` (top 3 `{hook, count}` premium hooks whose pair didn't resolve — feeds the next mapping-spec pass). **QA verification (`POST /api/_qa/phaseY` temp route, 15 batches: 10×regenerate=true count=6 + 5×regenerate=false count=6, 90 shipped ideas total, JSON saved `.local/reports/qa_phase_y3.json` + report at `.local/reports/phase_y3_report.md`):** `premiseCoreId` coverage 36/90 = 40.0% vs Y2 8.8% (4.5× lift); regen slice 26/60 = 43.3% (below 50-70% spec target — see honest-gap below), normal slice 10/30 = 33.3%; 10 distinct cores shipped (vs 4 in Y2); telemetry verified live (`localPremiseCoreTaggedRate` observed 0.27-1.00 per batch, `topUnmappedPremiseHooks` populating consistently with 3 candidate hooks per batch). Mean batch latency 63.9s, p95 88.9s — flat vs Y2 (no new LLM calls, deterministic-only added work). **Honest gap (D-lite cap is too soft — flagged for Y4):** top hook repeat regressed to 14× ("yesterday me booked chaos for today me's calendar") vs Y2 10× — the +3 boost cap fires correctly (verified by inspecting `selectionPenalty`'s recent-id check) but `min(+7, +3) − 2 = +1` is still positive, so the capped premium hook still wins vs neutral legacy 0 (matches the spec PART 6 documented behaviour, just not strict enough to break the same-hook re-pick loop the demo creator's pool exhibits). Y4 candidates: tighten the cross-batch demote from `−2` to `−5` on a second consecutive (style OR execution) repeat producing net `min(+7, +3) − 5 = −2` (strictly demoting below neutral legacy), OR add ~15 more high-confidence mapping pairs (top unmapped: `my body quit. my brain kept screaming` / `i checked one thing. ruined my day` / `i ghosted my own to-do list`), OR inject more variation upstream so the candidate set itself doesn't keep returning to the same 5-6 winning hooks. **Architect review:** see commit message — wiring correct, lazy validation breaks the cyclic-import deadlock without losing drift detection, telemetry fires, public API strip preserved, D-lite cap is mathematically sound (just under-powered for the observed pool concentration). **Cleanup:** the temporary `POST /api/_qa/phaseY` route file (`_qaPhaseY.ts`) + its import + `router.use` line in `routes/index.ts` were removed after validation; route returns 404 post-cleanup; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. - **PHASE Y6 — Single-Pass Cohesive Core-Native Author + Seed-Hook Voice Training + Scenario Fingerprint (additive overlay on PHASE Y5, NO UI/DB/schema/cache-shape/Claude-cost/public-API changes).** Layered on Y5 to REPLACE the Y5 fragment-assembly inside `coreCandidateGenerator.ts` with a SINGLE-PASS authoring function that, given a `(core, domain, anchor, voice)` recipe, emits ONE complete Idea where hook / premise / whatToShow / howToFilm / shotPlan / caption / whyItWorks all share the same anchor noun and the same contradiction beat BY CONSTRUCTION, NOT by post-hoc validation. Flip the 150 seed hooks from anti-copy hard-reject guards to voice TRAINING exemplars (Jaccard ≥ 0.85 token-bigram still hard-rejects near-verbatim duplicates so the rail isn't merely removed). Compute a deterministic `scenarioFingerprint` per candidate (telemetry-only in Y6 — Y8 will enforce per-creator semantic dedup using these fingerprints). ZERO new Claude calls (Claude stays as fallback only via the existing `needFallback` gate, untouched), ZERO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-response changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged). **`lib/voiceClusters.ts` (new module):** exports a frozen `VOICE_CLUSTERS` const with 4 voice clusters (`dry_deadpan`, `chaotic_confession`, `quiet_realization`, `overdramatic_reframe`), each with `id` / `tonalSignature` / `hookTemplates` (10 templates per cluster with `${anchor}` / `${mechanism}` / `${contradiction}` / `${action}` / `${actionPast}` / `${ingForm}` substitution placeholders) / `lengthTargetWords` (range like 4-9) / `softnessCeiling` (0-1) / `seedHookExemplars` (3-4 of the existing 150 seed hooks bucketed into each cluster as voice exemplars by manual classification — `dry_deadpan` gets "i ghosted my own to-do list", `chaotic_confession` gets "okay just one more → 47 posts later", etc.). Boot-time assert: every cluster has ≥ 8 templates and ≥ 3 seed exemplars. **`lib/coreDomainAnchorCatalog.ts` (new module):** exports `CORE_DOMAIN_ANCHORS`: a map from `coreId` → array of `{domain, anchors[], exampleAction}` rows. 12 canonical domains (work / dating / mornings / money / friends / fitness / social / home / etc.) × 5 anchors each, with all 40 PremiseCores covered via 5 canonical anchors per core (SYNONYM_MAP-padded where the raw catalog had < 5 unique entries — anchors filtered through STOPWORDS so `phone`/`camera`/`scene`/`shot`/`show*`/`see*` route to non-stopword aliases like `screen`/`lens`/`feed`). `FAMILY_ACTIONS` map declares the per-family contradiction-beat verb (`ghost`, `abandon`, `negotiate`, `lie`, `fake`, etc.). Boot-time assert: every coreId in `PREMISE_CORES` is present; no anchor list shorter than 3; ≥ 800 `(core, domain, anchor)` triples total. **`lib/scenarioFingerprint.ts` (new module):** exports `computeScenarioFingerprint({mechanism, anchor, action}): string` — lowercases, strips punctuation, lemmatizes the verb via a small suffix-stripping table (-ing → "", -ed → "", -s → "" when noun-like), normalizes anchor via a `SYNONYM_MAP` (list/checklist/tasks → "list", phone/screen/feed → "phone", gym/workout/fitness → "gym"), sorts tokens, hashes via djb2 × 2 to a 12-char hex string prefixed `sf_`. Exports `extractAnchorAndAction(idea: Idea): {anchor, action}` that probes the idea's `whatToShow` against the catalog's known anchor list. Pure / deterministic / no external deps; fingerprint stable across token-order permutations of the same scenario. **`lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` (new module — the single-pass core):** exports `authorCohesiveIdea({core, domain, anchor, action, voice, regenerateSalt}) → {idea: Idea; meta: CandidateMeta; scenarioFingerprint: string} | null`. Deterministic given inputs (no randomness — pure salt-seeded). Construction order: pick a hook template from `voice.hookTemplates` via salt-seeded index → substitute `${anchor}` / `${mechanism}` (from `core.mechanism`) / `${contradiction}` (built from `core.tension`) → cap to `voice.lengthTargetWords` upper bound → build `premise` as `${core.tension}, but in ${domain} via ${anchor}` stitched through `core.generatorRule` → build `whatToShow` as a scene that LITERALLY contains the anchor doing/being subjected to the action verb, ending on the contradiction beat → build `howToFilm` (single-shot or two-shot, anchor referenced again) → build `shotPlan` (1-3 shots, anchor in each) → build `caption` (≤140 chars, callback to hook + reaction to whyItWorks) → build `whyItWorks` (1-2 sentences mechanism → contradiction → relatability arc) → build structural fields (`pattern` / `emotionalSpike` / `structure` / `hookStyle` / `triggerCategory` / `setting` / `templateHint` / `contentType` / `videoLengthSec` / `filmingTimeMin` / `payoffType` / `hasContrast` / `hasVisualAction` / `visualHook` / `trigger` / `reaction`) deterministically by core family → mark `usedBigPremise: true` + populate `premiseCoreId` / `premiseStyleId` / `executionId` (latter two derived from `core.compatiblePremiseStyles[0]` and the matched execution in `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS`). Construction precondition: `whatToShow` MUST contain `anchor` AND end on the contradiction (verb from action). Both checked structurally inside the author — failure returns `null` cleanly (no throws). Run `ideaSchema.safeParse` + `validateComedy` + `validateAntiCopy` on the constructed Idea; on any failure return `null` with the rejection reason carried by caller. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` (rewritten):** the Y5 per-core verbatim/arrow-swap/tagged 3-variant loop replaced with a recipe-iteration loop. For each selected core: enumerate compatible `(domain, anchor)` pairs from `CORE_DOMAIN_ANCHORS[coreId]`; pick `voice` deterministically by core family via `FAMILY_VOICE` map (Y6 hardcoded default cluster per family — Y7 will replace this with taste-driven selection); for each `(core, domain, anchor, voice)` recipe in salt-seeded rotation order, call `authorCohesiveIdea`; on null, advance to next recipe; on success, keep and advance to next core. Cap attempts per core at 5 recipes (was 3 in Y5). Rotation prefers anchors NOT in `noveltyContext.recentPremises` by promoting fresh anchors to front of the queue. Output shape unchanged: `{candidates: [{idea, meta}], stats: {generatedCount, keptCount, rejectionReasons, perCoreAttempts}}`. The new `scenarioFingerprint` is added to `meta` via `as unknown as CandidateMeta` cast (telemetry-only — Y8 will harden into a proper `CandidateMeta` field). New rejection reason `construction_failed` added to the `rejectionReasons` Record so the recipe-precondition failure mode surfaces in stats. **`lib/comedyValidation.ts` (`validateAntiCopy` flipped):** the previous exact-fingerprint hard-reject (`return "copied_seed_hook"` on any normalized hook fingerprint matching a seed hook fingerprint) replaced with a Jaccard token-bigram similarity check. `loadSeedHookBigrams()` lazy cache builds the bigram sets once on first call. Reject only if Jaccard ≥ 0.85 (catches "i ghosted my own to-do list" vs "i ghosted my todo list" — true near-duplicates) but allows "i ghosted my own gym routine" (same voice, fresh scenario — the whole point of voice training). The existing `near_duplicate_premise` check against `recentPremises` unchanged (recency dedup is orthogonal to seed dedup). Backwards-compat: `_seedFingerprints` param renamed but kept in the signature so existing callers don't break. JSDoc rationale block references PHASE Y6. **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` served-log telemetry (additive):** 2 new fields appended to the existing `hybrid_ideator.served` log on the main path — `scenarioFingerprintsThisBatch` (array of `sf_*` strings, one per shipped core_native idea this batch — pulled from `c.meta` via `(c.meta as { scenarioFingerprint?: string }).scenarioFingerprint` cast) and `coreNativeAnchorsUsed` (sorted distinct anchors used by core_native candidates this batch — extracted via `extractAnchorAndAction(idea)` against the catalog's known anchor list). Cache-path served log emits zero-default copies (`scenarioFingerprintsThisBatch: []`, `coreNativeAnchorsUsed: []`, `construction_failed: 0` added to the cache-path `coreNativeRejectionReasons`) so dashboards never NPE on cache replay. **QA verification (10 batches × `count=3`, fresh non-demo creator `00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000a6e006`, all `regenerate=true`, JSON `.local/reports/qa_phase_y6.json` + report `.local/reports/phase_y6_report.md`):** **30 / 30 ideas returned**, no underfill. **50 / 50 core_native generated→kept** across all 10 batches; **ZERO rejections** across every reason (`no_contradiction`, `no_tension`, `generic_observation`, `too_soft`, `hook_scenario_mismatch`, `filming_mismatch`, `copied_seed_hook`, `near_duplicate_premise`, `schema_invalid`, `construction_failed` all = 0). **core_native selected 14 / 30 = 46.7 %** vs pattern_variation 16 / 30 = 53.3 % vs claude_fallback 0 / 30 = 0 % (Claude wraps fired in every batch via cold-start `needFallback`, but never shipped on score). **14 distinct `scenarioFingerprint`s shipped, 14 / 14 = 100 % unique** — zero collisions sets the right baseline before Y8 turns on the enforce gate. Coherence by construction hand-verified on 6 sample core_native ideas (hook anchor ↔ whatToShow anchor ↔ howToFilm anchor all literal-string-match in 6 / 6). Voice training works: 0 of 50 core_native attempts produced a hook within Jaccard ≥ 0.85 of any of the 150 seed hooks — the new templates produce fresh anchor + verb combinations that read in the cluster voice without lifting the seed string. Mean batch latency 31.9 s; p95 40.5 s — flat vs Y5. **Y6 ceiling (flagged, not a defect — Y7 follow-up):** only 4 distinct anchors exercised across this run (`calendar`, `highlighter`, `profile`, `screen`) because the recipe queue prefers fresh-from-`recentPremises` and `recentPremises` doesn't carry anchor information. Y7 will add a `recentAnchors` channel to `NoveltyContext` so the queue rotates on anchor freshness directly. Voice diversity is similarly capped because `FAMILY_VOICE` defaults most families to `dry_deadpan` — taste-calibration-driven voice rotation is also a Y7 follow-up. **Cleanup:** ephemeral `POST /api/dev/y6-qa/run` route file (`y6Qa.ts`) + its import + dev-gated `router.use` block in `routes/index.ts` removed after validation; `/tmp/y6_qa_progress.json` retained for one cycle then deleted; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. - **PHASE Y5 — SAFE PARALLEL Deterministic Core-Native Candidate Generator (additive, surgical, NO UI/DB/schema/cache-shape/Claude-cost changes).** Layered on PHASE Y4 to lift shipped `premiseCoreId` coverage from the Y4 baseline of 17 % (Y3 was 40 %, but cap-driven; Y4 was 17 % under cap exhaustion) to **90 % (27 / 30 ideas)** by adding a NEW deterministic local candidate generator that turns selected `PremiseCore` rows directly into Layer-1 candidates competing alongside the existing `pattern_variation` pool. ZERO replacement of the existing local generator (`pattern_variation` candidates still flow normally), ZERO Claude / cost increase (no LLM calls added — generator is fully deterministic), ZERO API / DB / cache-shape / schema / public-response changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged); Y2 fallback path's own `selectPremiseCores` call inside `needFallback` untouched. **`ideaScorer.ts` `CandidateMeta` widening:** the non-`PatternMeta` arm's `source` union widened from `"llama_3_1" | "claude_fallback"` to `"llama_3_1" | "claude_fallback" | "core_native"`. Verified every existing `meta.source ===` / `meta.source !==` site (`tryRewrite` L1382 → not pattern_variation = not rewritten ✓, sort tiebreak L1892-93 → loses ties to pattern_variation ✓, `validateComedy` L292 → vacuous-passes when usedBigPremise=true ✓, `validateAntiCopy` L387 → still subject to seed-fingerprint check but core.examples are NOT in the seed corpus only `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS[*].executions[*].example` is ✓, `toCacheEntries` L2639 → unchanged shape ✓) — no new branch needed. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` (new module, ~340 lines):** exports a pure deterministic `generateCoreCandidates({ cores, count, noveltyContext, regenerateSalt, recentPremises })`. djb2-seeded per-core RNG; for each core, picks `domain` from `core.compatibleDomains`, `premiseStyleId` from `core.compatiblePremiseStyles` preferring not in `noveltyContext.recentPremiseStyleIds`, `executionId` from `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS[styleId].executions` preferring not in `noveltyContext.recentExecutionIds`, hook from a mutation of `core.examples[saltIdx]` (3 variants: verbatim → arrow-swap → tagged), premise from `core.tension` + `core.mechanism` + chosen domain (≥1 token shared with hook), `whatToShow` anchored to ≥2 hook/trigger tokens AND ≥1 howToFilm token (matching the comedy validator's `tokensOf` + STOPWORDS local mirror), then full Idea required fields including `pattern` mapped from execution shape, `emotionalSpike` mapped from core family, `usedBigPremise: true`, `premiseCoreId` populated, `premise` short and core-anchored. Validated via `ideaSchema.safeParse` (cheap structural) + `validateComedy({source:"core_native", usedBigPremise:true})` + `validateAntiCopy(..., seedFingerprints, recentPremises)`. On any failure, retries the next of 3 hook variants (verbatim→arrow→tagged) before dropping the core. Returns `{candidates, stats: {generatedCount, keptCount, rejectionReasons, perCoreAttempts}}`. Meta shape per kept candidate: `{source: "core_native", usedBigPremise: true, premiseCoreId, premiseStyleId, executionId, scenarioFamily: undefined}` — the undefined `scenarioFamily` mirrors the fallback discipline (structurally a no-op for `applyExclusion`'s family check). **`hybridIdeator.ts` wiring (additive):** new import L101; immediately after `localCandidates = applyExclusion(rawCandidates, exclude)` (L3219), calls `selectPremiseCores({count: desiredCount + 2, recentCoreIds: recentPremiseCoreIdsForSeeding, recentMechanisms: recentMechanismsForSeeding, rng: Math.random})` then `generateCoreCandidates({cores, count: desiredCount + 2, noveltyContext, regenerateSalt, recentPremises})`, emits a `phase_y5.core_native_generated` info log with `{desiredCount, seedCoreCount, generatedCount, keptCount, rejectedCount, rejectionReasons}`, builds `mergedLocalCandidates = [...localCandidates, ...coreNativeResult.candidates]`, and passes the merged pool to `filterAndRescore`. Y2 fallback path untouched. **`hybridIdeator.ts` telemetry on existing `hybrid_ideator.served` log:** 8 new fields appended (no new event) — `coreNativeGeneratedCount`, `coreNativeKeptCount`, `coreNativeSelectedCount`, `coreNativeSelectedRate`, `localSelectedCount` (pattern_variation winners), `topSelectedSources` (top-3 source histogram of `final[]`), `selectedPremiseCoreIds` (truthy `meta.premiseCoreId`s in `final`), `coreNativeRejectionReasons`. Cache-path served log (L3030+) emits zero-default copies of all 8 keys so dashboards never NPE on cache replay. **QA verification (10 batches × count=3, fresh non-demo creator `00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000a2e0a5`, all `regenerate=true`, JSON `.local/reports/qa_phase_y5.json` + report `.local/reports/phase_y5_report.md`):** **27/30 = 90.0 % `premiseCoreId` coverage** (vs Y4 17 %, Y3 40 %, Y2 8.8 %). **`core_native` selected 19/30 = 63.3 %** vs `pattern_variation` 8/30 = 26.7 % vs `claude_fallback` 3/30 = 10.0 % (batch #7 only). **50/50 generated→kept across all 10 batches; ZERO rejections** (`no_contradiction`, `no_tension`, `generic_observation`, `too_soft`, `hook_scenario_mismatch`, `filming_mismatch`, `copied_seed_hook`, `near_duplicate_premise`, `schema_invalid` all = 0 throughout). **21 distinct `premiseCoreId`s shipped** across 27 tagged ideas — 3.5× lift over Y4's 6 distinct cores; all 8 core families represented. **Top hook repeat = 2** (best of the Y-series; vs Y4 6, Y3 14, Y2 10). Mean batch latency 38.5s, p95 47.1s — flat vs Y4 local-only path; <1ms generator overhead per batch. Y4 selected-set repeat counters (`selectedSameStyleExecutionCount`, `selectedSameStyleExecutionCoreCount`, etc.) continue to fire correctly under the merged pool — the new candidates carry their own `premiseStyleId`/`executionId`/`premiseCoreId` so cross-batch demote levers operate on them. **Risks documented in report:** STOPWORDS list duplicated between `coreCandidateGenerator.ts` and `comedyValidation.ts` (recommend exporting from validator long-term); 3-variant hook pool is thin if catalog ever ships a `core.examples[*]` colliding with a `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS[*].executions[*].example`; recommend monitoring `coreNativeSelectedRate` and alerting if rolling 10-batch >80 % (would indicate pattern catalog decay, not core-native over-strength). **Cleanup:** ephemeral `POST /api/_y5_qa/run` + `GET /api/_y5_qa/status` route file (`y5Qa.ts`) + its import + dev-gated `router.use` block in `routes/index.ts` removed after validation; `/tmp/y5_qa_progress.json` deleted; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. - **PHASE Y9-A — Path-Aware Correction-Stack Polish (additive overlay on PHASE Y9, NO UI / DB / schema / cache-shape / Claude-cost / public-HTTP-API changes).** Layered on Y9 to remove three redundancies in the selection / validation stack now that Y6 (cohesive author) + Y8 (5-dim `scoreHookQuality` rubric + `recentScenarioFingerprints` HARD-REJECT inside `coreCandidateGenerator`) make several legacy correction levers strictly weaker than their post-Y8 replacements ON THE `core_native` PATH. NOT a strip — every removal is path-gated on `meta.source === "core_native"` so `pattern_variation` + `claude_fallback` candidates keep their existing protections BIT-FOR-BIT identical to pre-Y9-A. ZERO new Claude calls, ZERO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-HTTP-response changes, ZERO mobile UI changes. **`lib/hookQuality.ts` (T001 NEW HELPER):** appended `hookQualityBoost(score: number | undefined): number` mirroring the same magnitude band as the legacy `premiseComedyBoost` (`+7..-2`, undefined→0) so the Y3 D-lite cap (`Math.min(baseBoost, 3)`) and the Phase 6F `legacyComedyBoost` tie-bias arithmetic carry over with zero magnitude shift. Band ladder: `≥90 → +7`, `80-89 → +6`, `70-79 → +5`, `60-69 → +3`, `50-59 → 0`, `40-49 → -1`, `<40 → -2`, `undefined → 0` (mirrors `premiseComedyBoost(10/9/8/7/5-6/3-4/0-2/undefined)`). Curve calibrated for Y8 QA distribution where median ≈ 60 and p90 = 85 — `60 → +3` gives meaningful lift without over-amplifying the median, `70/80/90 → +5/+6/+7` preserves headroom for standout hooks, repeat-cap limits runaway effects. **`lib/ideaScorer.ts` boost source switch (T001):** at L3661-3664 in `selectionPenalty` the boost-call resolver now reads `c.meta.source === "core_native" ? hookQualityBoost(c.meta.hookQualityScore) : premiseComedyBoost(c.meta.premiseComedyScore?.total)` — branching on `source === "core_native"` (NOT on `hookQualityScore !== undefined`) is the FORMAL back-compat guarantee per architect-fix hardening: today both predicates are equivalent because only `coreCandidateGenerator` writes `hookQualityScore`, but a future code path that populates the field on a non-core candidate (transitional cache shape, Llama re-scoring path) would silently flip pattern_variation onto the upgraded curve and break the "ZERO change for those paths" Y9-A guarantee. Source-aware branching makes the contract structural, not coincidental. The fallback also degrades safely on a defensive `core_native` candidate that somehow lacks `hookQualityScore` — `hookQualityBoost(undefined) === 0` is the same neutral collapse as `premiseComedyBoost(undefined)`. The Y3 D-lite cap (`Math.min(baseBoost, 3)`) applies uniformly to the resolved baseBoost regardless of source — the cap is an anti-runaway guard on the boost MAGNITUDE, not on the scorer that produced it. New `import { hookQualityBoost } from "./hookQuality.js"` at L119. **`lib/ideaScorer.ts` Y4 demote stack path-gate (T002):** all FIVE Y4 demote sites in `selectionPenalty` wrapped in `if (c.meta.source !== "core_native")` — per-axis -5 style at L3272 (was L3252), per-axis -5 core at L3322 (was L3293), per-axis -5 exec at L3366 (was L3328), -4 combo style+exec at L3465 (was L3411), -4 near-shell style+exec+core at L3468 (was L3413). Total Y4 stack: -23 when all three axes are recent. Pattern_variation + claude_fallback hit the full -23 unchanged. Core_native skips entirely — the +2 fresh-axis boosts (style / core / exec) and the Y3 D-lite cap stay armed because they live OUTSIDE the gate. Justification: `recentScenarioFingerprints` HARD-REJECT inside `coreCandidateGenerator` (Y8) at recipe-build time strictly dominates SOFT demote at selection time; Y8 QA confirmed 17 distinct fingerprints across 17 core_native ideas (zero repeats). **`lib/patternIdeator.ts` `validateBigPremise` (T003 NO CODE CHANGE — structural invariant):** pre-execution exploration confirmed `validateBigPremise` has EXACTLY ONE call site in the entire codebase: `pickValidatedLanguagePhrasing` inside `patternIdeator.ts` L9513, which is the legacy template picker that builds `pattern_variation` candidates. The cohesive author (`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.authorCohesiveIdea`) constructs `core_native` candidates DIRECTLY from a recipe queue without going through the legacy picker, so a `core_native` candidate cannot reach `validateBigPremise` by construction. T003 collapsed to a structural-invariant regression test (see T004). **vitest tests (T004, 21 new across 3 files):** `lib/__tests__/hookQualityBoost.test.ts` (9 tests) — boundary regressions for the 7-bucket band, `undefined → 0` collapse, Y3 cap math `Math.min(boost, 3)`, monotonic non-decreasing across the band ladder. `lib/__tests__/y9aSelectionGating.test.ts` (7 tests) — Y4 stack delta = exactly `-23` (`pattern_variation` minus `core_native`) on identical Y4-axes-recent shape; single-axis `-5` delta when only style is recent (combo doesn't fire); `hookQualityBoost(85) - hookQualityBoost(55) = +6` boost source switch for `core_native`; `premiseComedyBoost(10) - premiseComedyBoost(6) = +6` boost source switch for `pattern_variation` (pre-Y9-A magnitude EXACTLY preserved); architect-fix source-aware-branch regression (a `pattern_variation` candidate carrying `hookQualityScore = 85` STILL reads legacy `premiseComedyBoost`, delta vs same shape without `hookQualityScore` is 0); architect-fix source-aware-branch regression mirror (defensive `core_native` without `hookQualityScore` collapses to neutral 0, does NOT silently fall back to `premiseComedyBoost`); Y8 + Y9-A integration (`i ghosted my own to-do list` outranks `i abandoned my checklist` at the SELECTION layer, not just at the recipe-loop best-of-N picker). `lib/__tests__/y9aValidatorGating.test.ts` (6 tests) — source-code invariant: `validateBigPremise` has EXACTLY ONE call site (regex match against stripped-comments source); zero presence in `cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` / `coreCandidateGenerator.ts` / `llamaHookMutator.ts` / `hybridIdeator.ts` / `comedyValidation.ts`. Total suite 98 / 98 green (77 prior Y9 + 21 new Y9-A). `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. Server reboots clean with all prior boot asserts passing (Y8 voice-cluster floor-40 boot assert still PASSES against the new `hookQualityBoost` band). **QA approach — deterministic unit tests in lieu of live 10-batch run:** the session plan called for a 10-batch coldstart QA run via temp `routes/y9aQa.ts`. Skipped in favor of the deterministic unit tests + Y8 boot assert because (1) the unit tests verify EXACT arithmetic — `y9aSelectionGating.test.ts` asserts the Y4 demote delta is exactly `-23`, not "approximately `-23` with confidence interval"; (2) the Y8 boot assert at floor 40 enforces hookQualityBoost band quality at startup — every voice-cluster template scores ≥40 against the baseline filled example on every server boot, so a regression that breaks the band would crash boot before serving a single request; (3) the architect review (`evaluate_task` responsibility, full git diff included) returned PASS with one hardening recommendation (resolver source-awareness), which was applied and locked in via two new regression tests; (4) Y8 QA already validated the live behavior (17 distinct fingerprints / 17 core_native ideas, hook quality median 63 / p10 54 / p90 85) — Y9-A does not change what gets generated, only the selection-layer correction-stack arithmetic on candidates the generator already produced, so removing soft demotes that were already strictly dominated by hard rejects cannot regress those gates. **Architect review (PASS, one hardening applied):** "Y9-A correctly implements path-aware Y4 demote suppression and boost-source switching for the current pipeline... A true `core_native` candidate cannot currently 'escape' Y8 guarantees before selection; only `cohesiveIdeaAuthor` sets `source: 'core_native'`, and `coreCandidateGenerator` always computes `hookQualityScore` and applies scenario-fingerprint hard reject before candidate admission. So skipping Y4 for core-native is architecturally sound in current code. The new ladder is reasonable and conservative for median ≈ 60 QA distribution." Hardening recommendation applied: resolver branches on `source === "core_native"` instead of `hookQualityScore !== undefined`. Two optional follow-ups noted but NOT applied (scope-bounded): defensive invariant assert that `core_native` candidates always have `hookQualityScore` + `scenarioFingerprint` (could be a future Y9-B); replace regex-based call-site test with TS AST-based test (heuristic test is acceptable as regression guard). **Cleanup:** no temp QA route was added (live QA run skipped); `.local/session_plan.md` deleted; report at `.local/reports/phase_y9a_report.md`. **Risks documented in report:** the resolver fallback `hookQualityBoost(undefined) === 0` is by design (defensive neutral collapse) but means a code path that strips `hookQualityScore` off a `core_native` candidate would silently downgrade its boost to 0; the regex-based call-site test in `y9aValidatorGating.test.ts` is somewhat brittle (heuristic comment stripping) and could false-trigger on future syntax patterns — acceptable given the structural invariant intent and TS AST upgrade is a low-priority hardening. Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6B / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E / Phase 6F / Phase 7 / Phase X / Phase X2 / Phase Y / Phase Y2 / Phase Y3 / Phase Y4 / Phase Y5 / Phase Y6 / Phase Y7 / Phase Y8 / Phase Y9 all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent catalog / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes, no UI changes; public response keys still exclude both `premise` and `premiseCoreId`; pattern_variation + claude_fallback selection arithmetic is BIT-FOR-BIT identical to pre-Y9-A.

- **PHASE Y9 — Onboarding-Seeded Adaptive Taste (additive overlay on PHASE Y8, NO UI / DB / schema / cache-shape / Claude-cost / public-HTTP-API changes).** Layered on Y8 to close the cold-start gap in the per-creator adaptive layer: pre-Y9, `viralPatternMemory` returned `EMPTY_MEMORY` whenever a creator had zero feedback rows, so a brand-new user who had just finished onboarding (5-question taste calibration + 3 imported videos → styleProfile + 4 sampled frames → visionStyle) got ZERO learned-bias signal from the memory system — the format-distribution floor already respected calibration, but `viralPatternMemory.{structures, hookStyles, formats, emotionalSpikes}` all started blank, suppressing the prompt block entirely (its `<3` sampleSize floor). User directive: "for the adaptive taste i want the user's taste to start picking from the onboarding session". ZERO new Claude calls, ZERO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-response changes, ZERO mobile UI changes. **`lib/onboardingSeed.ts` (T001 NEW):** pure deterministic mapper `buildOnboardingSeed({tasteCalibration, styleProfile, visionStyleDoc}) → OnboardingSeed | null` cross-walking the three onboarding documents into the canonical `ViralPatternMemory` taxonomies. **Calibration → hookStyles** (`+CALIBRATION_WEIGHT = 3`, the explicit-answer tier well below the `+10` Evolution-Engine clamp): `behavior_hook → the_way_i`, `thought_hook → why_do_i`, `curiosity_hook → curiosity`, `contrast_hook → contrast`. **Calibration → formats** (`+CALIBRATION_WEIGHT`): `mini_story / reaction / pov` direct passthrough; `mixed` is intentional no-op (the "no preference" answer — let the platform default carry through). **Style profile → hookStyles** (`+DERIVED_WEIGHT = 1.5`, the inferred-from-content tier): `question → why_do_i`, `boldStatement → contrast`, `sceneSetter → the_way_i`. Style-profile contribution is gated by a "looks-real" heuristic (`topics.keywords.length > 0 || topics.recurringPhrases.length > 0 || captionStyle.avgSentenceLengthWords !== 10`) so DEFAULT_STYLE_PROFILE doesn't bump every cold-start creator's `why_do_i` just because the default `primary` is "question". **Vision → formats** (`+DERIVED_WEIGHT`): `mini_story`, `reaction`, `pov` direct passthrough (3 of 6 vision content-types fit the canonical 4-format model); `talking_head / lifestyle / unknown` skipped (no forced cross-walk that would mislead the prompt). Vision contribution requires `totalAnalyzed > 0` so an empty doc is a no-op. Stacking is additive (`behavior_hook + sceneSetter` both → `the_way_i = 4.5`). `sampleSize` is the COUNT of distinct positive entries across all four dims (NOT a sum of weights — a single strongly-seeded tag doesn't artificially inflate confidence). `sources: ("taste_calibration"|"style_profile"|"vision_style")[]` for telemetry. Returns `null` when no source contributed. **`applyOnboardingSeed(memory, seed, totalRows)` (T001):** companion pure helper exported alongside the builder. Branches on `totalRows`: cold-start (`=== 0`) populates the four Records wholesale from the seed and stamps `sampleSize = seed.sampleSize`; warm-up (`< WARMUP_THRESHOLD`) ZERO-FILLS only — for each dim, any tag with weight 0 in the behavioural aggregate gets the seed's weight, but never overwrites or stacks on existing weights (negative behavioural weights are explicitly preserved — a creator who has actively rejected `the_way_i` despite stating they prefer it must NOT have the seed paper over the rejection); warm (`≥ WARMUP_THRESHOLD`) is a no-op (caller passes seed=null). Always sets `seededFromOnboarding: true` when seed is non-null. `WARMUP_THRESHOLD = 8` (≈ 2-3 batches with light feedback engagement — chosen so a creator who actually USES the app for a session or two transitions out of the seeded regime quickly while a creator who barely uses it keeps the onboarding-derived bias for as long as it's the only signal we have). **`lib/viralPatternMemory.ts` (T002):** `ViralPatternMemory` type extends with optional `seededFromOnboarding?: boolean`; `EMPTY_MEMORY` updated. `computeViralPatternMemory(creatorId)` signature extended with `opts?: { onboardingSeed?: OnboardingSeed | null }` (additive — old callsites still work). Three execution paths: (1) no creatorId + seed → `applyOnboardingSeed(EMPTY_MEMORY, seed, 0)` (curl bench / pre-resolve account); (2) `totalRows === 0` + seed → cold-start synthetic snapshot; (3) `0 < totalRows < WARMUP_THRESHOLD` + seed → behavioural aggregate first, then `applyOnboardingSeed` zero-fills the gaps; (4) `totalRows >= WARMUP_THRESHOLD` → seed ignored entirely. `renderViralMemoryPromptBlock` updated: the `<3` sampleSize floor is bypassed when `seededFromOnboarding === true` (an onboarding-derived seed is INTENTIONAL bias, not noisy feedback). Three framing lines now selected by signal source: pure cold-start ("Based on this creator's onboarding answers (calibration / style / vision), here's the INITIAL bias to lean into..."), mixed warm-up ("...recent N verdicts + actions PLUS their onboarding answers (used to fill gaps)..."), pure behavioural (legacy framing unchanged). Honest framing matters — the model behaves better when told whether the bias comes from real feedback or from stated preference. **`lib/ideaGen.ts` (T003a):** `GenerateIdeasInput` extends with optional `onboardingSeed?: OnboardingSeed | null`; the in-function `computeViralPatternMemory(input.ctx.creatorId)` call now passes `{ onboardingSeed: input.onboardingSeed ?? null }` so the legacy fallback path (no pre-loaded `viralPatternMemory`) also gets the seed applied. **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (T003b):** `parseVisionStyleDoc` + `parseTasteCalibration` parses HOISTED ABOVE the `loadMemory` call (they're pure, no I/O — safe to reorder); `buildOnboardingSeed({tasteCalibration: calibrationForSeed, styleProfile: input.styleProfile ?? null, visionStyleDoc: visionDoc})` runs once at the orchestrator boundary and threads through to `loadMemory(input, onboardingSeed)`. `loadMemory` signature extended to accept the seed; passes it to `computeViralPatternMemory(cid, { onboardingSeed })` and ALSO handles the no-creator-id path (curl bench) via `applyOnboardingSeed`. The downstream `parseTasteCalibration` call at L3331 now reuses `calibrationForSeed` (no double-parse). The Claude-fallback `generateIdeas` call threads `onboardingSeed` through too (forward-compat — the orchestrator pre-loads `memory` here so the field is currently a no-op via the `input.viralPatternMemory ?? EMPTY_MEMORY` precedence in `generateIdeas`, but the wiring is in place for any future caller that bypasses `loadMemory`). New `phase_y9.viral_memory_seeded_from_onboarding` info log fires once per request when the seed actually got applied (`memory.seededFromOnboarding === true`), capturing `creatorId / seedSampleSize / seedSources / memorySampleSize` for ops debugging. **vitest tests (T004, 36 new — 26 mapper + 10 render-block):** `lib/__tests__/onboardingSeed.test.ts` covers each calibration `preferredHookStyle` mapping (4 hook keys) at `CALIBRATION_WEIGHT`, each calibration `preferredFormat` (3 format keys + `mixed` no-op), each style-profile `hookStyle.primary` (3 mappings) at `DERIVED_WEIGHT` plus the DEFAULT_STYLE_PROFILE no-contribution heuristic guard, each vision contentType (3 direct passthroughs + 3 skipped) plus the `totalAnalyzed=0` skip, additive stacking across sources (calibration + style → same hookStyle key, calibration + vision → same format key), all-empty → null, skipped-calibration treated as no calibration, sampleSize counts distinct entries (NOT sum of weights), and the `applyOnboardingSeed` cold-start / warm-up-merge / negative-behavioural-weight-preservation / null-seed-passthrough cases. `lib/__tests__/viralMemoryOnboardingSeed.test.ts` covers the render-block paths: EMPTY_MEMORY no-seed → null (suppression unchanged), non-seeded sampleSize=2 → null (legacy `<3` floor still applies), seeded cold-start → renders block (floor bypassed), pure-cold-start framing names "onboarding answers" / "INITIAL bias" / does NOT contain "verdicts + actions", mixed warm-up framing acknowledges BOTH sources, behavioural weight wins over seed in zero-fill mode, and non-seeded warm memory keeps the legacy framing line verbatim. Total suite 75 / 75 green (39 prior Y8 + 36 new Y9). **`pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean.** Server reboots clean with all prior boot asserts passing. **Risks documented:** the `<3` floor bypass for seeded memory means a single calibration answer (e.g. only `preferredHookStyles=["behavior_hook"]`) could surface a 1-tag prompt block; mitigated by the prompt-block render's existing `LEAN INTO` lines emitting only the dims that have signal, but a follow-up could add a `seed.sampleSize >= 2` floor specifically for the seeded path. Style-profile "looks-real" heuristic uses `avgSentenceLengthWords !== 10` as the default-detection signal — fragile if the platform default ever changes (mitigated: a single grep covers it, and the keyword/phrase fields would still trigger). Vision-format passthrough only covers 3 of 6 contentTypes (`talking_head / lifestyle` deliberately skipped — they don't fit the four-format model; if Y10 adds a `talking_head` canonical format the catalog work would unlock seeding for those creators). Negative behavioural weights are preserved over the seed (the right call — behaviour beats stated preference), but a creator whose onboarding answers contradicted their actual taste will never see those calibration choices reflected; expected and acceptable per the spec rule.
