- **PHASE Y10 — Per-Creator History-Aware Generator (4-Axis Exclusion, additive overlay on Y7+Y8+Y9, NO UI/DB/schema/cache-shape/Claude-cost/public-HTTP-API changes).** Lifts the cross-batch freshness window from **5 → 7 batches** across all axes AND adds a **4th exclusion axis: voice clusters** (the Y6 4-cluster taxonomy was previously rotated only per-batch via family-biased salt rotation, with no cross-batch memory). After Y10 the seed budget for a new batch EXCLUDES recent fingerprints (Y8 HARD-REJECT), anchors (Y7 HARD-REJECT), AND voice clusters (Y10 NEW — least-recently-used min-count pick) used in the last 7 batches. ZERO new Claude calls, ZERO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-HTTP-response changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged). **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (T001):** `MAX_HISTORY_BATCHES` bumped 4 → 6 (visible window = current + 6 history = 7 total); rename `last5BatchesForPremises` → `last7BatchesForFreshness` (+ `slice(0,5)` → `slice(0,7)`) which now feeds `recentPremises` / `recentAnchors` / `recentScenarioFingerprints` / `recentVoiceClusters` (one shared slice for all 4 axes so the creator sees a coherent freshness window). Doc comments at MAX_HISTORY_BATCHES, buildExclusion, recentPremises / recentAnchors / recentScenarioFingerprints all updated to reflect the 7-batch widening. **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (T002 — voiceClusterId cache widening + histogram build):** `CachedBatchEntry` widened with optional `voiceClusterId?: VoiceClusterId` (mirrors how Y8 widened for `scenarioFingerprint`); `tryParseEntries` reads the field through the canonical `isVoiceClusterId` guard tolerantly (legacy envelopes without the field contribute `undefined` → simply don't increment any histogram bucket; NO crash, NO schema migration, NO data loss); `toCacheEntries` validates `c.meta.voiceClusterId` through the same guard before persisting (corrupt / legacy values can never poison the histogram); new histogram build `recentVoiceClusters: Map<VoiceClusterId, number>` over the 7-batch slice; threaded into the `noveltyContext` object passed to `generateCoreCandidates`. **`lib/voiceClusters.ts` (architect-fix consolidation):** new exported `isVoiceClusterId(s: string): s is VoiceClusterId` guard added next to the `VOICE_CLUSTERS` registry — the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH for taxonomy membership (reads off the existing `_byId` map). Replaces an earlier draft's local `_ALL_VOICE_CLUSTER_IDS` literal tuple in `hybridIdeator.ts` so a future taxonomy expansion (5th cluster) automatically widens the guard with NO duplicated tuple to maintain. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` (T003 — history-aware `resolveVoiceCluster`):** `CoreNoveltyContext` extended with optional `recentVoiceClusters?: ReadonlyMap<VoiceClusterId, number>`. `resolveVoiceCluster` signature accepts the optional histogram. Priority chain UNCHANGED for taste-pinned (`preferredTone` direct map remains priority 1 short-circuit); Y10 only modifies the salt-rotation arm. Inside the salt-rotation: walk the existing 9-slot `biasedTable` in salt-rotated order and pick the FIRST cluster whose recent count equals the MIN over all 4 clusters — family bias preserved as natural tiebreak (the family default appears 3× in the table → among equally-cold clusters the family-curated default still wins by walk-order). When `recentVoiceClusters` is undefined OR empty (`hist.size === 0`), behavior is **bit-for-bit identical** to pre-Y10 (the gate `if (recentVoiceClusters && recentVoiceClusters.size > 0)` short-circuits). `generateCoreCandidates` recipe loop reads `recentVoiceClusters` from the new noveltyContext field and passes it through to `resolveVoiceCluster`. **Histogram-not-Set rationale:** a `Set<VoiceClusterId>` would saturate after 1-2 batches (taxonomy is exactly 4 ids; ~3 ideas/batch × 7 batches = 21 usages vs 4 slots) and stop being actionable. The histogram preserves rotation pressure indefinitely; voice clusters intentionally use SOFT (min-recency rotation) instead of HARD-REJECT (Y7/Y8) because the 4-cluster taxonomy is too small for hard exclusion. **vitest tests (T004 — 19 new):** `lib/__tests__/y10VoiceClusterRotation.test.ts` (9 tests) — cold-start parity (no histogram = pre-Y10 deterministic salt-rotation), empty Map equivalence (Map.size===0 short-circuits identically to undefined), 1 hot cluster → resolver picks one of OTHER 3, 2 hot → picks one of OTHER 2, 3 hot 1 cold → ALWAYS picks the cold one across 64 (salt, recipeIdx) sweeps, all-4-unequal → picks min-count cluster, all-4-equal → falls through to salt-rotated start (parity with cold-start), taste-pinned `preferredTone` short-circuit STILL wins even with hot histogram, multi-recipe in-batch rotation (compounding histogram → different cluster per recipeIdx). `lib/__tests__/y10HistoryWindow.test.ts` (5 tests) — structural type contracts on `CoreNoveltyContext`: 21-entry fingerprint Set (7 batches × 3 ideas), 4-cluster histogram, empty Map cold-start, optionality back-compat with pre-Y10 callers, all-4-cluster taxonomy keys. `lib/__tests__/y10WindowBehavioral.test.ts` (5 tests + parity regression) — 7-batch saturation behavioral, 8-batch overflow proves resolver trusts caller-side cap, single-batch cold-warm 2-cluster, 4-recipe full-coverage rotation, AND **parity regression block** sweeping 16 (family × salt × recipeIdx) tuples asserting `undefined ≡ empty Map ≡ baseline` for every one (architect-fix follow-up). Total suite **117 / 117 green** (98 baseline + 19 new Y10). **Architect review (`evaluate_task`, includeGitDiff=true) returned PASS with 3 actionable follow-ups, ALL applied:** (1) added the behavioral 7-batch window test file (was previously only structural); (2) added the cold-start parity regression block; (3) consolidated the `_ALL_VOICE_CLUSTER_IDS` literal tuple into the canonical `isVoiceClusterId` export. **Cache back-compat verified:** pre-Y10 envelopes have NO `voiceClusterId` field — parser returns `undefined`, write path validates through the guard, histogram simply doesn't increment for missing values; ZERO data loss, ZERO migration. **Frozen-surface verification:** ZERO new Claude calls; the `wrapFallbackIdea` Claude path untouched; ZERO DB schema changes; ZERO public HTTP API changes; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; api-server boots clean on port 8080 with all Y8 voice-cluster floor-40 boot asserts still passing. **Risks documented in report:** (1) the 9-slot `biasedTable` in `coreCandidateGenerator.ts` is still hardcoded for 4 clusters — a 5th-cluster addition would require updating `BIASED_TABLE_SIZE` and table-construction math (out of Y10 scope; `isVoiceClusterId` guard auto-widens); (2) histogram is shared cross-family — a creator who shipped 7 `dry_deadpan` ideas in family `self_betrayal` sees the picker demote `dry_deadpan` even on a NEW family `absurd_escalation` batch (intended design — rotation is creator-global); (3) in-batch sibling cores still don't share a per-recipe voice tracker — Y10 only widens the cross-batch axis; a single batch that ships 3 ideas with the same voice cluster remains theoretically possible (rare given salt-rotation index varies per recipeIdx). - **PHASE Y11 — QA Validation of Phases Y7+Y8+Y9+Y10 (ephemeral, NO production code change, NO new Claude calls, NO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-HTTP-API changes; merged-and-removed harness).** Pure dual-scenario QA pass against the frozen Y10 ideator surface to verify three claims independently: (a) **coherence** holds (Y8 `hookQualityScore` floor) on both fresh and engaged creators; (b) **variety** holds (Y7 anchor / Y8 scenario-fingerprint / Y10 voice-cluster freshness windows actually suppress recent picks across the 7-batch envelope); (c) **adaptation** holds (Y9 `tasteCalibration.preferredTone` priority-1 short-circuit in `resolveVoiceCluster` actually pins the voice cluster, not just decorates the creator row). **Harness `routes/y11Qa.ts` (T001 NEW, T003 DELETED):** ephemeral dev-gated Express router mounted at `/api/y11-qa/*` ONLY when `process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production"` (with a defense-in-depth handler-entry re-check that 404s in production); inserted two random-UUID NON-demo creators per run with grep-friendly `authUserId = "_y11qa_<scenario>_<ts>_<rand>"` so any orphan from a crashed run is identifiable, and DELETEd both rows in `finally{}` (best-effort — errors logged then swallowed so a transient db hiccup never blocks the response). **Scenario A "fresh":** `tasteCalibrationJson = null`, no prior history. **Scenario B "engaged":** `tasteCalibrationJson = { preferredTone: "dry_subtle", ... }` (full TasteCalibration shape). Both scenarios called `runHybridIdeator` directly N batches with `regenerate=true` (so cache rotates and the recipe loop re-fires); the harness REFETCHED the creator after each batch so `lastIdeaBatchJson` history accumulated naturally and the 7-batch freshness window actually saw real prior fingerprints/anchors/cores by batch 2+. Per-scenario aggregates computed: hookQualityScore quantiles (min/p10/median/p90/max), distinct fingerprints/anchors across all batches, voice cluster histogram, first-half-vs-second-half distinct-count split (directional evidence the window kicks in over time), `pinnedClusterShare` (voice cluster pin verification). Aggregates written to `.local/reports/qa_phase_y11.json` (best-effort fs write, also returned in HTTP response). **Run config:** `batches=5, countPerBatch=3` per scenario (15 ideas/scenario, 30 ideas/run). **Results (`.local/reports/qa_phase_y11.json` + `.local/reports/phase_y11_report.md`):** **Coherence:** fresh n=6 → median 71.5 / p10 61.5 / max 75; engaged n=9 → median 63 / p10 60 / max 85. Both scenarios cleared the Y8 floor with margin (no idea below 60 in either). Engaged's wider p10-p90 spread (17 vs fresh's 12.5) is the cost of voice pinning — some core/anchor combos fit `dry_deadpan` less well, but best-fit ones pop higher (max 85 vs 75). **Variety:** fresh 6 distinct fingerprints / 6 distinct anchors out of 6 telemetry-tagged ideas; engaged 9/9 — ZERO repeats on either axis in either scenario. Engaged H1→H2 distinct-fingerprint count went 2→7 (variety EXPANDED with history because the window had more priors to avoid by batch 2+ and pivoted to fresh anchors `tripod`/`gym`/`bio`/`savings`/`wallet` instead of repeating early `inbox`/`doc`). **Adaptation:** fresh dry_deadpan share = 0.33 (2/6 ideas, 4 distinct clusters used: `chaotic_confession`, `dry_deadpan`, `quiet_realization`, `overdramatic_reframe`); engaged dry_deadpan share = **1.00 (9/9 ideas)** — exact match for the priority-1 `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER` short-circuit's stated behavior. **Honest caveats documented in report:** (1) `qaTelemetry.perIdea` is constructed for every shipped idea via `final.map(...)` in `hybridIdeator.ts`, but `anchor` is explicitly source-gated on `core_native` and `hookQualityScore`/`voiceClusterId`/`scenarioFingerprint` are sparse for `pattern_variation` ideas — so the per-axis distinct counts are core-native-biased (true counts ≥ reported); (2) N=5 batches × 3 ideas means H1/H2 split uses `floor(batches/2) = 2` so halves are unequal — directional evidence not precise ratio; (3) `pinnedClusterTarget` was hard-labeled `dry_deadpan` for both scenarios so the fresh "share" reads as a baseline frequency for that cluster, not adaptation evidence on its own — adaptation is the GAP between fresh (0.33) and engaged (1.00); (4) `usedFallback: true` on every batch is normal under `regenerate=true` cold/rotated cache, no new Claude call types added; (5) per-batch duration 26–46s matches Y10 baseline. **Architect review (T003, includeGitDiff=true):** evaluated harness soundness + interpretation accuracy. Flagged 2 amendments to the markdown report (telemetry scope claim was overstated as "core-native-only" when the array is built for all ideas with sparse per-row fields; "no orphan rows" was absolute when cleanup is best-effort) — both PATCHED into the report before cleanup. Harness security risk classified as not release-blocking because the route was about to be deleted in T003 and was never mounted in production. **T003 cleanup (this commit):** DELETED `artifacts/api-server/src/routes/y11Qa.ts`, REVERTED both edited lines in `artifacts/api-server/src/routes/index.ts` (the `import y11QaRouter from "./y11Qa"` line and the dev-gated `if (NODE_ENV !== "production") router.use(y11QaRouter)` block) so the file is bit-identical to its pre-Y11 state; verified the route returns 404 post-cleanup; verified tsc clean; verified the full vitest suite remains 117/117 green. The `.local/reports/qa_phase_y11.json` (raw aggregates) + `.local/reports/phase_y11_report.md` (interpretation) are the only artifacts that persist past Y11. **Verdict (committed in report):** Phase Y10's coherence + variety + adaptation invariants hold under realistic dual-scenario QA. No production fix needed. Phases through Y10 remain frozen.
- **PHASE Z5.6 — Always-On Hero Quality Ranker + Adaptive First-Session Boost (additive overlay, NO UI/DB/schema/migration/API-shape changes).** Adds a 10-dimension deterministic hero quality scorer (`scoreHeroQuality` in `ideaScorer.ts`, 0-100 total: hookPunch, filmNowEase, payoffClarity, comedicSpecificity, scenarioCoherence, voiceNaturalness, safetyConfidence, freshness, lowEffortSetting, captionSynergy) folded into `IdeaScore.total` at 0.06× weight (0-6 additive, raised from 0.02× in Z5.6b). Willingness scorer adds `heroBoost = min(20, round(heroQuality × 0.25))` for top-card ordering (raised from 0.15×/15 in Z5.6b). Adaptive first-session boost (`computeFirstSessionBoostFactor`) returns 1.0→0.7→0.4→0.15→0 as batch history depth grows 0→4, drops to 0 immediately when taste calibration exists. `selectionPenalty` applies first-session boosts (POV +3, safe structures +2, internal_thought +2, low-effort settings +2, short hooks +1) and caps (small_panic -3, panic spike -2, high-lift filming -3), all scaling linearly with the factor. `hybridIdeator.ts` computes the factor from `priorBatches.length` + `tasteCalibrationJson` presence and threads it through `NoveltyContext.firstSessionBoostFactor`. 24 new tests in `z56HeroQualityRanker.test.ts`.
- **PHASE Z5.7 — Sustainable Retention Novelty Loop (additive overlay on Z5.6b, NO UI/DB/schema/migration/API-shape changes).** New `retentionNoveltyScorer.ts` module adds 4-dimension returning-user scoring overlays that wire into the existing `selectionPenalty` pipeline via `NoveltyContext.retentionMemory` + `NoveltyContext.retentionProfile`. Activates ONLY for returning creators (batchDepth ≥ 2 AND viralPatternMemory sampleSize ≥ 3) — first-session creators get zero retention penalty (immunity). **Signal alignment** (`computeSignalAlignment`): reads `viralPatternMemory.{structures, hookStyles, emotionalSpikes, formats}` weights + `momentumBoosts` + `stalePenalties` + `tasteShiftPromotions` to compute a per-candidate -5 to +7 alignment score; positive-signal patterns get boosted, negative-signal patterns get demoted, momentum/stale/taste-shift modifiers stack. **Overfit penalty** (`computeOverfitPenalty`): detects when any single axis dominates ≥50% of the last-3-batches history (-3 structure, -2 hookStyle/emotionalSpike/format), with a lighter -1 at 40%; clamped at -6. **Fatigue risk** (`computeFatigueRisk`): composite 3-axis frequency metric (structure + hookStyle + format); fires only at batchDepth ≥ 3; -3 at ≥50% avg, -2 at ≥35%, -1 at ≥25%. **Novelty distance** (`computeNoveltyDistance`): counts axes fresh vs history (0-3 for 0-3+ fresh axes). **Batch composition** (`applyBatchComposition`): post-selection reordering for batches ≥ 3 from returning creators — classifies each candidate as hero (highest total score) / taste (highest signal alignment) / novelty (highest novelty distance) and reorders to ensure slot diversity when the three slots differ. Wired in `hybridIdeator.ts` after Llama mutation and before final ship. **`retentionSelectionBonus`**: composite penalty/boost (clamped -8 to +5) combining half the signal alignment + overfit penalty + fatigue risk + novelty boost (+2 at ≥3 fresh axes, +1 at ≥2), applied at the end of `selectionPenalty` when retention context is present. 40 new tests across `retentionNoveltyScorer.test.ts` (28 unit) + `z57RetentionQa.test.ts` (12 QA scenarios covering signal boost/deweight/fatigue). All 309 tests pass, TypeScript clean, server healthy.
- **PHASE Z5.8 — Closed-Beta Quick Tune Calibration v2: 4-screen flow + 2 new enum values + situations field (additive overlay on Z5.7; ZERO migrations because every new field lives inside the existing `creators.tasteCalibrationJson` JSONB blob; ZERO API-shape changes — POST/GET response envelope is still `{ calibration: ... }`; ZERO Claude-cost changes; ZERO scoring philosophy changes).** Restructures the 3-step Quick Tune (format → tone → opener) into a 4-screen flow: 3 REQUIRED screens (`format` ≤3, `tone` ≤3 with NEW `high_energy_rant` 5th option, NEW `situations` ≤4) followed by 1 OPTIONAL screen (`opener` ≤3 with NEW `pov_hook` 5th option, keeps "Skip for now"). Required screens block forward at 0 selections (Continue only renders when count > 0); only the optional opener step renders Skip. Cap-reaching tap auto-advances on every multi step (3/3/4/3 caps). **Server zod (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** `preferredToneEnum` widened with `"high_energy_rant"`; `preferredHookStyleEnum` widened with `"pov_hook"`; new `situationEnum` with 6 closed-set values (`food_home`, `dating_texting`, `work_school`, `social_awkwardness`, `health_wellness`, `creator_social`); new `selectedSituations: z.array(situationEnum).max(4).default([])` field. Old persisted docs lacking `selectedSituations` parse via the `.default([])` discipline (same back-compat pattern as Z4's `preferredTones` default and Z5.6's hero fields). **Voice-cluster pin (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts`):** `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER` extended with `high_energy_rant: "high_energy_rant"` (intentionally same-name pin — the rant tone targets the rant voice cluster directly). **Patterns priority chain (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/patternIdeator.ts`):** `CALIBRATION_TONE_TO_VOICE` (5-key Record) widened to map `high_energy_rant → "chaotic"` VoiceProfile (closest peer in the existing 8-VoiceProfile taxonomy — both register as "loud, expressive"); `VoiceSignalInputs.calibrationTone` literal union widened to include the 5th option so `selectPrimaryVoiceProfile` typechecks across the whole signal-tier resolver. The two mappings agree on the rant's expressive register but live at different granularities — `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER` operates on the finer voice-CLUSTER axis, `CALIBRATION_TONE_TO_VOICE` operates on the coarser VoiceProfile axis. **Onboarding seed (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/onboardingSeed.ts`):** `CALIBRATION_HOOK_TO_MEMORY` extended with `pov_hook: "internal_thought"` (best-fit among the 5-value memory taxonomy — POV openers are framed as the speaker's internal POV). **Prompt guidance (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** new `TONE_GUIDANCE` entry for `high_energy_rant` ("loud, animated, takes-no-prisoners energy — picture a rant with stakes, not whining") and new `HOOK_STYLE_GUIDANCE` entry for `pov_hook` ("frame the opener as the speaker's POV — 'me when…', 'POV: you…', 'why do I always…' — making the audience the camera"); both feed the existing `getToneGuidance` / `getHookStyleGuidance` helpers that thread into the comedy hook prompt unchanged. **Route observability (`artifacts/api-server/src/routes/tasteCalibration.ts`):** the POST route's `req.log.info` now stamps `selectedSituationsCount` alongside the existing format/tone/hook counts so closed-beta usage can be analyzed without raw-doc reads. **Mobile types (`artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** new `Situation` literal union mirroring the server's `situationEnum`; `PreferredTone` widened with `"high_energy_rant"`; `PreferredHookStyle` widened with `"pov_hook"`; `TasteCalibration` gains `selectedSituations: Situation[]`; `EMPTY_CALIBRATION` updated with `selectedSituations: []`. **Mobile component restructure (`artifacts/lumina/components/onboarding/TasteCalibration.tsx`):** step indices renumbered 0=format, 1=tone, 2=situations, 3=opener(optional), 4=confirmation. New `SITUATION_CHOICES` (6 closed-set entries with `value` + `label` + short body copy explaining what each lane biases toward), new `SITUATION_SUMMARY` Record for confirmation-card chip labels, new `SITUATIONS_MAX = 4` cap. New state `situations: Situation[]`, new handlers `handleSituationToggle` (cap-reaching tap auto-advances to step 3) and `handleSituationContinue` (1-3 selections require Continue tap). Tone step's `TONE_CHOICES` + `TONE_SUMMARY` extended with the rant entry; opener step's `HOOK_CHOICES` + `HOOK_SUMMARY` extended with the POV entry. Step kicker copy updated: required steps render "{n} of 4" (no "optional" suffix), opener renders "4 of 4 · optional". **`fireSaveSideEffects` signature widened** from `(formats[], tones[], hooks[])` to `(formats[], tones[], situations[], hooks[])`; both terminal entry points on the opener step (cap-reaching auto-advance INSIDE the `setHookStyles` updater AND the explicit `handleHookContinue`) thread `situations` through unchanged. **Skip semantics changed for closed-beta:** the opener Skip path now calls `fireSaveSideEffects(formats, tones, situations, [])` — i.e. it persists a NORMAL completed save with the 3 required selections AND `preferredHookStyles: []` AND `skipped: false`, rather than the prior `skipped: true` "user opted out entirely" doc. Rationale: pre-Z5.8, Skip was a single-step bail on a 3-required flow with no notion of partial progress; in Z5.8 the user has already committed format + tone + situations as required signal before the optional step appears, so persisting a `skipped:true` doc would discard that signal. The legacy `skipTasteCalibration` helper is still exported (in case any other caller needs the full-skip semantics) but is no longer imported by `<TasteCalibration />`. **`ConfirmationCard` widened:** new `situationLabels: string[]` prop renders 1-4 situation chips in the same flexWrap cluster between tone chips and hook chips. **Profile read-back (`artifacts/lumina/components/profile/YourStyleSection.tsx`):** `TONE_LABELS_CAL` Record gains `high_energy_rant: "High-energy rant"` and `HOOK_LABELS_CAL` gains `pov_hook: "POV opener"` so the user-facing "Your style" recap renders correctly when a creator has a Z5.8-shaped doc. (TypeScript `Record<PreferredTone, string>` exhaustivity is what surfaced this — it's a label gap that would silently fall through to `undefined` at runtime if missed.) **Z5a invariant inversion (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/__tests__/z5aHighEnergyRantCluster.test.ts`):** the prior Z5a test asserted "high_energy_rant tone is NEVER pinned to high_energy_rant cluster" (because Z5a kept the cluster floor-only, not enum-pinned). Z5.8 explicitly inverts that — the spec calls for the rant tone to PIN. The test now asserts: (1) `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER.high_energy_rant === "high_energy_rant"` (mapping pin); (2) when calibration sets `preferredTone: "high_energy_rant"`, the rant cluster's per-batch share is ≥40% (dominance — pinned, not just preferred); (3) when calibration sets a NON-rant tone (e.g. `dry_subtle`), the rant cluster's share stays ≤30% (bounded — the floor doesn't leak into non-rant calibrations). **Test backfill:** two existing test fixtures that hand-construct calibration docs were updated — `__tests__/onboardingSeed.test.ts` (`baseCal` helper) added `selectedSituations: []`; `__tests__/y10VoiceClusterRotation.test.ts` (D1 priority test) added `selectedSituations: []`. **Known gap (intentional, deferred):** `selectedSituations` is persisted, logged, and round-tripped through the calibration doc, but is NOT YET consumed by the candidate generator (no `getSituationGuidance` helper, no scenario-pool filter, no candidate scoring weight). Closed-beta priority is collecting the signal first; consumption is a follow-on phase. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean for all Z5.8-touched files (the 2 remaining typecheck errors in `retentionNoveltyScorer.test.ts` + `z57RetentionQa.test.ts` are pre-existing baseline issues about `rewriteAttempted` and `emotionalSpike: "guilt"` — confirmed unchanged in `git diff HEAD`); full api-server vitest 28/28 files / 310/310 tests green; api-server restarted; healthz clean. **Frozen scope:** ZERO migrations, ZERO API-shape changes, ZERO Claude-cost changes, ZERO scoring philosophy changes, ZERO retention/hero/novelty/comedy-rubric changes. - **PHASE Z5.8b — Selected-situations soft alignment (additive overlay on Z5.8; ZERO migrations, ZERO API-shape changes, ZERO validator loosening, ZERO Claude-cost changes, ZERO scoring-philosophy changes — pure additive soft-preference signal layered on top of the existing scoring pipeline).** Closes the Z5.8 known gap: `selectedSituations` was persisted, logged, and round-tripped through the calibration doc but NOT consumed by the candidate generator. Z5.8b wires the 6-value enum (≤4 selected) into `selectionPenalty` as a +4/+2/0/-1 additive boost band that sits BELOW comedy (+5..+7) and Hero Quality (0..+6), so Hero/comedy/retention rankers continue to dominate selection. **`lib/tasteCalibration.ts`:** added `import type { Setting, TopicLane } from "./patternIdeator"`; new exported `SituationProfile` type and frozen `SITUATION_PROFILES` Record covering all 6 situations × {strongTopicLanes, adjacentTopicLanes, strongSettings, adjacentSettings, familySubstrings} signal axes; new pure exported `scoreSituationAlignment(candidate, selectedSituations) → number` returning the additive delta. Strong match (+4) fires when ANY selected situation matches via `topicLane ∈ strongTopicLanes` OR `scenarioFamily.includes(familySubstring)` OR `setting ∈ strongSettings AND lane ∈ strongTopicLanes`; adjacent match (+2) fires when `topicLane ∈ adjacentTopicLanes` OR `setting ∈ strongSettings` OR `setting ∈ adjacentSettings`; mismatch (-1) fires ONLY when ≥3 situations selected (strong stated preference) AND candidate matches none. Silent abstain (returns 0) when candidate has no usable signals (Llama/Claude wraps with no `topicLane` AND no `setting` AND no recognized `scenarioFamily`) so the -1 nudge never fires on a candidate we can't even classify. **`lib/ideaScorer.ts`:** added import for `scoreSituationAlignment` + `Situation` type; widened `NoveltyContext` with optional `selectedSituations?: ReadonlySet<Situation>` (silent no-op for cold-start / skipped-calibration creators); appended `p += scoreSituationAlignment({topicLane: metaTopicLane(c.meta), setting: c.idea.setting as Setting, scenarioFamily: c.meta.scenarioFamily}, ctx.selectedSituations)` at the END of `selectionPenalty`, after `retentionSelectionBonus` so all soft levers compose linearly. **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts`:** added a small block right after the `firstSessionBoostFactor` wiring that re-parses `input.tasteCalibrationJson` via `parseTasteCalibration`, reads `selectedSituations`, and populates `noveltyContext.selectedSituations = new Set(sitArr)` only when non-empty. The downstream `parseTasteCalibration` call at line ~3500 (existing seed/taste path) is intentionally left untouched — additive only. **Tests (`__tests__/z58bSituationAlignment.test.ts`, NEW, 21 tests):** profile coverage (all 6 situations present, each has ≥1 strong axis, only valid TopicLane + Setting values used); additive contract (cold-start no-op, +4 strong via lane, +4 strong via familySubstring without lane, +2 adjacent via adjacent lane, +2 adjacent via strongSetting alone, 0 when 1-2 situations selected and candidate matches none, -1 only when ≥3 selected AND zero match, strong-match overrides ≥3-mismatch, silent abstain on no-signal Llama wraps even with ≥3 selected, never exceeds +4 with multiple matches, max 4 selected with one strong still capped at +4); back-compat parsing (pre-Z5.8b doc without `selectedSituations` parses cleanly with `[]` default, Z5.8b doc round-trips, malformed enum value → safe parse to null, max 4 constraint enforced); boost-band invariants (+4 < +5 premise comedy and < +6 Hero Quality; -1 > -1000 hard-reject floor). **Validation:** full api-server vitest 29/29 files / 331/331 tests green (310 baseline + 21 new); api-server typecheck unchanged from baseline (the 2 pre-existing errors in `retentionNoveltyScorer.test.ts` + `z57RetentionQa.test.ts` about `rewriteAttempted` and `emotionalSpike: "guilt"` confirmed unchanged via git diff before changes); api-server restarted clean (port 8080, migrations idempotent); architect code review returned no critical/high issues — confirmed (a) additive composition preserves Hero/comedy/retention dominance invariant, (b) the -1 mismatch lever cannot stack to starve a slot (single -1 max per candidate, no summing across situations), (c) silent-abstain guard correctly handles unclassifiable candidates, (d) placement after retention/first-session boosts composes linearly as intended. **Frozen scope:** ZERO migrations, ZERO API-shape changes, ZERO Claude-cost changes, ZERO retention/hero/novelty/comedy-rubric changes, ZERO new HTTP routes, ZERO cache-shape changes. - **PHASE Z5.6b — Hero Threshold + Payoff Sharpening (additive overlay on Z5.6, NO UI/DB/schema/migration/API-shape changes).** Lifts combined hero pass rate from 33.3% → 70.0%, avg top-card hero score from 64.3 → 71.8, returning-profile payoff clarity from 5.0/12 → 8.0/12. Six scorer changes: (1) `AWKWARD_PHRASE_RX` penalties (-4 hookPunch) for template-artifact phrasings ("Xing me back", "body quit…brain kept screaming", "watched myself fake", "still Xing the Y at this hour"); (2) `WEAK_HOOK_SKELETON_RX` penalties (-3 hookPunch) for vague skeletons ("my body quit", "brain kept screaming/going", "it/this happened", "life collapsed"); (3) `OBJECT_ANTHROPOMORPHISM_RX` bonus (+2 hookPunch) for object-betrayal hooks ("X knows/keeps/won't/is lying/judging"); (4) payoffClarity expansion — reaction/transformation payoffType now earns +1 (was 0), panic/regret emotionalSpike earns +2 (was 0), cap still 12; (5) captionSynergy broadening — base word-overlap reduced (≥2→4, ≥1→2), comedy amplifier words +2 (`CAPTION_COMEDY_RX`: always/never/every time/wins/still/literally/again/somehow/apparently/honestly), specific noun in caption +2, cap still 8; (6) payoff-clarity floor in `selectionPenalty` — ideas with no visual action AND no contrast AND not punchline/reveal payoff lose -2 so personalization cannot promote vague-payoff ideas. Hero weight in `IdeaScore.total` raised 0.02→0.06 (3×); willingness heroBoost raised 0.15→0.25 (cap 15→20). 20 new tests in `z56HeroQualityRanker.test.ts` + 11 QA harness tests in `z56bQaHarness.test.ts`, all 265 tests pass.
- **PHASE Y8 — Scenario-Fingerprint Dedup Gate + Hook Quality Scoring (additive overlay on PHASE Y7, NO UI/DB/schema/cache-shape/Claude-cost/public-HTTP-API changes).** Layered on Y7 to close the structural-repeat gap Y7 left open ("different words, same joke") AND raise the captivating-hook bar so dedup can't silently degrade into bland synonym swaps. ZERO new Claude calls (Claude stays as fallback only via the existing `needFallback` gate, untouched), ZERO DB / schema / cache-shape / public-HTTP-response changes; public API still strips `premiseCoreId` (route strip site at `routes/ideator.ts` L305-308 unchanged). User's gold-standard hook example threaded through the spec: "every hook title must be captivating and intriguing — `i ghosted my own to-do list` is better than `i abandoned my checklist`" — the new scorer picks the former by 40 points and the recipe loop now ships the highest-scoring recipe per core instead of first-pass-wins. **`lib/patternIdeator.ts` `PatternMeta` (T001):** promoted `scenarioFingerprint?: string` from a Y6-era `as unknown as` cast on `CandidateMeta` to a proper optional typed field on both the fallback arm of `CandidateMeta` AND on `PatternMeta` (mirrors how Y7 added `voiceClusterId`); also added `hookQualityScore?: number` on both arms (additive, optional, populated by the recipe loop on the winning candidate so QA + Y9 can read it without log scraping). **`lib/ideaScorer.ts` `NoveltyContext` (T001):** added `recentScenarioFingerprints?: ReadonlySet<string>` (optional so legacy callers keep working). **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` `CoreNoveltyContext` (T001):** mirrors the `recentScenarioFingerprints` field. **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (T001):** builds `recentScenarioFingerprints` from the last 5 cached batches by reading `meta.scenarioFingerprint` / `idea.scenarioFingerprint` off each cached candidate (cold-start gets empty set); threads through both `pattern_variation` and `core_native` paths; the Y6/Y7 `as unknown` cast at the `qaTelemetry.perIdea` map site cleaned up — fields now read directly off the union. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` recipe loop (T002 hard-reject + T003 rewrite):** OLD behavior shipped the FIRST recipe that passed `validateAntiCopy`, advanced to next core. NEW behavior COLLECTS all passing recipes for a core (up to the new `RECIPES_PER_CORE_CAP = 8`, raised from 5 to give the iterator more room when both anchor freshness AND fingerprint dedup constrain choices), scores each via `scoreHookQuality`, ships the highest-scoring one. If all 8 fail, falls through with `keptCount` unchanged. After the existing `validateAntiCopy` block, a new hard-reject fires: if `recentScenarioFingerprints.has(sf)` → reject with new reason `scenario_repeat`, advance to next recipe (added to `EMPTY_REASONS` and the rejection counter). New in-batch tracker `usedFingerprintsThisBatch` so sibling cores in the same batch can't ship duplicate fingerprints (mirrors Y7's `usedAnchorsThisBatch`). `meta.hookQualityScore` written on the winning candidate. **`lib/hookQuality.ts` (T003 NEW):** pure deterministic `scoreHookQuality(hook, family) → 0-100` plus `{visceral, anthropomorph, brevity, concrete, contradiction}` breakdown. Components: `visceralVerbScore` (table of ~30 high-impact verbs by family — `ghost / fake / lie / betray / negotiate / expose / abandon`; bland verbs `did / got / had / made / took / was` score 5 instead of 0 so a hook can't be zeroed out by a single weak verb — Y8 fix vs initial draft); `anthropomorphScore` (regex `my own`, `itself`, `back at me`, `at me`, `to me`, `me back` — last added in Y8 to catch `the inbox came back at me`; plus IMPLICIT pattern matching family verbs as their own subject like `the venmo keeps avoiding itself`); `brevityScore` (1.0 at 5-7 words, decay outward); `concretenessScore` (anchor presence + non-stopword noun count); `contradictionScore` (em-dash / arrow `→` / "but" / numeric blow-ups `47 posts later`; plus DRAMATIC_NOUNS `villain / apocalypse / scientists / papers` → 10 so dramatic-noun hooks like `the slippers ruined my villain arc` score appropriately). **`lib/voiceClusters.ts` `hookTemplates` (T003 CURATE):** 8 templates rewritten to remove bland verbs (`did / got / had / made / took / was`) and add anthropomorph markers / concrete anchors: `dry_deadpan #4/#6/#8`, `quiet_realization #2/#4/#7/#9/#10`, `overdramatic_reframe #5/#7`. Boot-time assert at floor 40 against a fill example (anchor=`list`, action=`abandoned`) — every template now scores ≥40 against the baseline filled example. Server boot logs the assert PASSING for all 40 templates. **vitest tests (T004, 14 new — 9 initial + 1 architect-fix gaming-guard regression):** `lib/__tests__/hookQuality.test.ts` (10 tests) — `i ghosted my own to-do list` > `i abandoned my checklist` (user's exact example, 40-point gap), visceral verb beats bland, anthropomorph `my own X` > `my X`, brevity 6-word > 11-word, concrete anchor present > absent, bland-verb floor 5, detailed return shape, family-specific verb table, boot-assert sanity, AND **`Y8 GAMING GUARD: 'my own' alone (no verb / anchor / contradiction signal) is capped to IMPLICIT tier`** (architect-fix regression — see below). `lib/__tests__/scenarioRepeatDedup.test.ts` (4 tests) — `recentScenarioFingerprints` containing `sf_X` rejects a recipe authoring to `sf_X` with reason `scenario_repeat`; empty set ships the same recipe; cross-batch hard-reject (batch N → batch N+1); in-batch sibling-core hard-reject. Total suite 39 / 39 green (25 prior Y7 + 14 new Y8). **Architect review fix — gaming guard on EXPLICIT anthropomorph:** architect flagged that the `EXPLICIT_ANTHROPOMORPH` regex (`my own`, `itself`, `myself`, `back at me`, …) is worth a full 25 — large enough that a hook could fake personhood by prefixing any bland statement with `my own X was Y` and clear the median bar. Fix in `scoreHookQualityDetailed`: the EXPLICIT marker only earns its full 25 when the hook ALSO shows real captivating signal somewhere (visceral verb above bland, OR concrete catalog anchor, OR contradiction beat). When the marker is the ONLY signal, credit is capped at the IMPLICIT tier (12). IMPLICIT credit is unaffected because its structural pattern (`the X verbed me`) already requires a real animate-coded verb. The user's gold example `i ghosted my own to-do list` keeps its full 25 (visceral=30 + concrete>0 satisfies the guard). Boot asserts re-verified: every voice-cluster template still scores ≥40. **QA verification (T005, ephemeral `routes/y8Qa.ts` mounted dev-gated under `/api/y8-qa/*`, removed in T006):** **COLDSTART (10 batches × count=3, fresh non-demo creator `00000000-0000-0000-0000-00000000a8e8`, no taste calibration, all `regenerate=true`, `isDemo=false` so persistCache writes lastIdeaBatchJson and `recentScenarioFingerprints` rotation actually feeds across batches):** **17 distinct fingerprints / 17 core_native ideas (100% per-idea unique, ZERO repeats — primary acceptance gate)**, **17 distinct anchors / 17 core_native ideas (Y7 floor of 12 held with margin)**, **3 of 4 voice clusters represented (`chaotic_confession` 7, `overdramatic_reframe` 6, `dry_deadpan` 4; `quiet_realization` absent in this 17-idea cold-start sample but present in Y7's 16-idea sample, n-variance not regression)**, **hook quality median 63 / p10 54 / p90 85 / min 48 / max 85 — all four acceptance gates green** (zero fingerprint repeats, median ≥60, p10 ≥40, anchor diversity ≥12). Source histogram: 17 core_native + 13 pattern_variation = 30 total ideas; ZERO `construction_failed`, ZERO `copied_seed_hook`. Sample winning hooks demonstrating scorer pick quality: `i exposed my own dishes` (85, anthropomorph + visceral + 5 words), `watched myself ghost the profile live` (85, dramatic verb stack + anthropomorph + anchor), `the venmo keeps avoiding itself` (63, IMPLICIT anthropomorph + visceral + concrete anchor). **`HybridIdeatorResult.qaTelemetry.perIdea[].hookQualityScore`:** new optional `hookQualityScore?: number` field (additive, populated by recipe loop on winning candidate). KEPT after T006 cleanup (strictly additive, useful for Y9, costs ≤ batch_size object allocations per call); the "no public API change" guarantee in this phase refers to HTTP API (no new endpoint, no body shape change for `/api/ideator/generate`), which holds. **Cleanup (T006):** ephemeral `routes/y8Qa.ts` + dev-gated `router.use` block in `routes/index.ts` removed after validation; final aggregates persisted to `.local/reports/qa_phase_y8.json`; report at `.local/reports/phase_y8_report.md`; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; 39 / 39 vitest tests pass; server reboots clean with all 40 voice-cluster boot asserts passing. **Risks documented in report:** voice-cluster `quiet_realization` absent in this cold-start sample (small-sample variance, present in Y7 QA — 9-slot biased rotation unchanged); hook quality `min` is 48 (above floor of 40 but 15 points below median — recipe loop is correctly picking best of 8, the floor-shipper means SOME core has only weak recipes; Y9 could raise cap to 12 OR add hard floor of 50); `pattern_variation` candidates don't get a `hookQualityScore` (scoring only fires inside core recipe loop, Layer-1 patterns use existing `premiseComedyBoost` lever — acceptable separation of concerns; Y9 could surface scorer as soft selection bonus on the scoring stack); family-specific visceral-verb table is small (~30 verbs, hand-curated and family-tagged, expansion needs new family→verbs mapping pass — produces 63 median which clears bar). Phase 3 / 3B / 3C / 3D / Phase 4 / Phase 5 / Phase 6 / Phase 6 EXPANSION / Phase 6B / Phase 6C / Phase 6D / Phase 6E / Phase 6F / Phase 7 / Phase X / Phase X2 / Phase Y / Phase Y2 / Phase Y3 / Phase Y4 / Phase Y5 / Phase Y6 / Phase Y7 all frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent catalog / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape changes, no DB schema changes, no premise-share gate changes, no UI changes; public response keys still exclude both `premise` and `premiseCoreId`.

- **PHASE D1 — Five surgical quality fixes (post-Y11 trash-ideas user report; additive overlay, NO UI/DB/schema/cache-shape/Claude-cost/public-HTTP-API changes).** Triggered by user report of 14 trash ideas in a single batch despite Y11 shipping. Failure modes confirmed in code: (a) Y10 freshness window dedups on `scenarioFingerprint` only — no hook axis; near-duplicate hooks like "my body quit. my brain kept screaming" recurred 4× because the exact-string `normalizeHookForDedup` only lowercases + trims; (b) legacy `patternIdeator.ts` doesn't enforce hook ↔ scene anchor (cohesive author DOES at L441) producing hooks like "the fridge knows i'm lying" with scenes that never showed the fridge; (c) `coreCandidateGenerator.ts:284` `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER[tone]` was a hard 1.00 short-circuit collapsing every recipe to one voice cluster; (d) `scoreHookQuality` had no AI-cliché penalty so generic AI dialect ("my body quit", "is unwell", "filed for emotional bankruptcy") cleared the floor; (e) verbatim deterministic templated tails — `patternIdeator.ts:7436-7437` 2-option ternary, `cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts:362-371` single-shape caption + whyItWorks — produced 6+ identical tails per 14-idea window. **Taste-as-core thread:** user emphasized hooks must draw from the calibrated voice cluster's seed corpus (150+ blessed exemplars in `voiceClusters.ts seedHookExemplars` + `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS` examples), NOT a generic AI dialect. The AI-cliché list deliberately EXCLUDES "i specialize in" because that shape is at `voiceClusters.ts:85` ("i specialize in disappointing myself") — penalizing it would work against stated taste. **Fix #1 — Hook fingerprint axis (`lib/scenarioFingerprint.ts` + `lib/hybridIdeator.ts` + `lib/ideaScorer.ts`):** new exported `canonicalizeHookForFingerprint(hook) → "hf_<12hex>" | ""` runs the same lemma + synonym + stop-word + sort + djb2 pipeline as the scenario fingerprint, plus a `HOOK_STOPWORDS` set (`a/an/the/i/im/my/me/to/and/or/but/of/...`). All cosmetic variants of "my body quit. my brain kept screaming" — punctuation drift (`.` → `;`), tense drift (`kept` → `keeps`), filler drift (`and my brain still screaming`) — collapse to the same `hf_*`. `buildNoveltyContext` populates a parallel `recentHookFingerprints: Set<string>` in the SAME walk as `recentHookStrings` over the FULL visible cache (no separate read). New optional `recentHookFingerprints?: ReadonlySet<string>` field on `NoveltyContext`. `selectionPenalty` adds a SECOND independent -1000 cross-batch hard reject mirroring the exact-string lever, plus a within-batch `for (const b of batchSoFar)` parity loop. Empty fingerprint (`""`) treated as "no contribution" so cold-start / malformed hooks don't poison the Set with a sentinel that would silently match every other empty-content hook. **Fix #2 — Hook ↔ scene anchor HARD invariant on legacy `patternIdeator.ts assembleCandidate` (~L10058-10094):** strips article from `scenario.topicNoun` (`/^(?:the|a|an|my|your)\s+/`) and requires the bare noun to appear in `idea.hook` lc OR `idea.whatToShow` lc. Mismatch returns `null` — `assembleCandidate`'s callers already treat null as a soft skip (no whole-batch failure), so the slot re-rolls into the next valid (template, scenario, language) combination from the Cartesian iter. Cohesive author already enforces this at L441 — D1 adds parity to the legacy path so both code paths now refuse to ship hook-scene mismatches. **Fix #3 — Soften Y9 `TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER` pin in `lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts resolveVoiceCluster` (L286-317):** removed the priority-1 hard `return TONE_TO_VOICE_CLUSTER[tone]`. Tone is now folded into the same biased-table mechanism as `familyDefault` — preferred-tone cluster gets +5 slots so it dominates without monopolising. Resulting distribution: tone == family default → preferred ~57% / others ~14%; tone != family default → preferred ~50% / family ~21% / others ~14%; no tone → 9 slots, family ~33% / others ~22% (unchanged from pre-D1). Y10 histogram-LRU walk below still runs unchanged and pushes underused clusters to the front. **Fix #4 — AI-cliché demote band in `lib/hookQuality.ts` (~L541-581):** new pure deterministic `aiClicheScore(hookLower) → -15..0` plus `AI_CLICHE_PATTERNS` regex list (12 patterns: `my body quit`, `my brain (?:hates|filed|kept screaming)`, `is unwell`, `emotional bankruptcy`, `filed for (?:emotional|divorce|bankruptcy)`, `(?:totally|completely) fine (?:about|with)`, `knows i'm lying`, `ruined my villain (?:arc|origin)`, `villain (?:arc|origin) (?:ruined|cancelled|over)`, `my own personal (?:hell|apocalypse|villain)`, `someone please (?:help|stop|tell)`, `not a phase mom`). Each match = -8, capped at -15. Soft demote (NOT a reject) — a hook with genuinely-strong other axes still ships. Wired as new `aiCliche: number` field on `HookQualityBreakdown` and as a negative addend to `total`. List deliberately excludes user-blessed seed-exemplar shapes ("i specialize in"); inline comment forbids future additions of blessed shapes. **Fix #5 — De-template directorial tails:** `lib/patternIdeator.ts buildWhatToShow` (~L7437-7486) replaced 2-option ternary with 4 contrast tails + 4 hold tails rotated by inlined `djb2HashLocal` over `(scenario.family, scenario.topicNoun, template.id, hasContrast)`. Each phrasing preserves the original directorial intent (cut-on-contradiction or hold-the-beat). `lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` (~L338-424) replaced single-shape `whatToShow` / `howToFilm` / `caption` / `whyItWorks` with 4 shapes each rotated by `djb2(`${core.id}|${anchor}|<axis>`)`. Anchor preserved verbatim in every shape so the construction precondition (`hookLcContainsAnchor` validator at L441 + `filmContainsAnchor`) holds. Deterministic per-(core, anchor) so QA harness stays reproducible, but two ideas with different recipes draw different shapes. **Test update (`lib/__tests__/y10VoiceClusterRotation.test.ts`):** rewrote the "taste-pinned preferredTone STILL wins" test to reflect Fix #3's spec — now asserts dry_deadpan dominance ≥40% AND ≤75% over 200 deterministic salts (was: 100% over 16 salts), plus ≥2 other clusters appearing at all. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; full vitest suite 117/117 passing (no test-count delta — Fix #4 added a field to a type that has no consumers asserting field-by-field shape, Fix #1's wire-up is covered by the existing `selectionPenalty` skipping when set is empty). **Architect code review (via `explore` subagent with full diff context):** ZERO CRITICAL or HIGH issues. Two MEDIUM concerns flagged, both accepted as ship-acceptable: (1) O(N²) fingerprint recompute in within-batch loop — `canonicalizeHookForFingerprint(b.idea.hook)` called for each candidate × each existing batchSoFar member; for batch_size=10-15 this is ~112 regex+sort+djb2 invocations per generation, well below latency budget (verified flat vs Y8 baseline). Pre-cache lift deferred to a follow-up if telemetry shows it. (2) `topicNoun` stripping regex covers `the/a/an/my/your` only — if the SCENARIOS catalog ever introduces a topicNoun prefixed with `this/that/these/those` the invariant would over-strip via the bare noun never appearing. Audit of current `scenario.topicNoun` values in `lib/patternIdeator.ts` shows all entries match `the X` shape (verified inline at L260/276/292/308/324/...) so no current-catalog miss. **Honest gaps for follow-up:** (a) the hook-template pool the cohesive author samples from (~10 templates per cluster × 4 clusters = 40 total) may need to expand by sampling from `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS[*].executions` filtered by voice cluster — D1's softening (Fix #3) + freshness axis (Fix #1) + cliché demote (Fix #4) widen taste expression on the existing pool but if the user reports the same monoculture next batch the pool itself is the bottleneck. (b) Fix #5's 4-shape rotators are deterministic — across N batches with the same (core, anchor) repeats they DO repeat the same shape; if N>4 batches before the (core, anchor) rotates, telemetry will surface tail-repeat counts and a follow-up could mix `regenerateSalt` into the rotator key. (c) `recentHookFingerprints` is sourced from the same FULL visible cache as `recentHookStrings` — if the cache window is too narrow (`MAX_VISIBLE_BATCHES_FOR_DEDUP` upstream) some far-historical near-dupes will still slip through, but this is a parameter on the hybridIdeator side not the scoring side. **Cleanup:** no temporary routes added, no temporary scripts, no env vars added; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; vitest 117/117 green. - **PHASE D15-alt — Self-recipe exemption for the unigram fallback (resolves D5-flagged template/seed circularity; additive overlay on D4 telemetry; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; pure validator behavior tweak that LOOSENS one false-positive corner without touching any other gate).** D5 surfaced a circularity in the anti-copy gate: short (≤4-token) `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS` execution examples like `"the dishes won again"` are BOTH (a) the seed substitution table the deterministic recipe loop draws from in `cohesiveIdeaAuthor` AND (b) folded into the seed-bigram pool that `validateAntiCopy`'s short-hook unigram fallback scores against. With the unigram-fallback threshold at 0.6 Jaccard on hooks ≤4 tokens, ANY single-word substitution of a 4-token seed against itself lands at 3/5 = 0.6 — guaranteed to trip the gate, so the recipe loop was rejecting its own legitimate output as "near-copy" of the very seed it was substituted FROM. Pure circularity, not plagiarism. **Fix design (per T003 plan, narrowest possible):** thread a per-candidate `originatingSeedHash` through the validator meta and exempt the match ONLY when (1) the matched seed's source pool is `style_defs`, (2) the seed's hash equals `meta.originatingSeedHash`, AND (3) the unigram fallback fired (NOT the long-hook 0.85 bigram gate — bigram-Jaccard ≥ 0.85 against any seed including the originator IS a true near-verbatim and ships unchanged so cross-template plagiarism still rejects via the normal path). Corpus matches are unaffected because the corpus pool never appears in the cohesive author's substitution table — `originatingSeedHash` is only ever set to a `style_defs` example's hash. **`lib/comedyValidation.ts`:** exported `computeSeedHash(s)` as a public alias of the internal `djb2Hex8` (same byte output) so the cohesive author can compute the SAME hash on its originating example string without duplicating the algorithm; widened `AntiCopySeedSource` from `'corpus' | 'style_defs'` to `'corpus' | 'style_defs' | 'style_defs_self'` (telemetry-only — never appears as a rejection reason); extended `ValidateComedyMeta` with optional `originatingSeedHash?: string`; in the unigram-fallback branch (~L709-746), inserted the self-exempt check BEFORE the existing reject — when `seed.source === "style_defs" && meta.originatingSeedHash === seed.hash`, return `{ reason: null, antiCopyMatch: { source: "style_defs_self", hash, jaccard, gate: "unigram" } }` instead of the rejection. **`lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts`:** added `computeSeedHash` to the comedyValidation import; widened the success arm of `CohesiveAuthorResult` with optional `antiCopyMatch?: AntiCopyMatch` (only populated on a self-exempt event, undefined for genuine clean passes); after the executions[0] resolution (~L488-494), compute `originatingSeedHash = executions[0].example ? computeSeedHash(executions[0].example) : undefined` (matches the SAME string `loadSeedHookBigrams` hashes when it folds PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS into the seed pool); pass `{ ...originatingSeedHash ? { originatingSeedHash } : {} }` into the `validateAntiCopyDetailed` meta arg; on the ok:true return, surface `copyResult.antiCopyMatch` if present so the recipe loop can roll up the telemetry. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts`:** widened `bySource` initializer from `{ corpus: 0, style_defs: 0 }` to `{ corpus: 0, style_defs: 0, style_defs_self: 0 }` (TS Record over the widened union forces this); on the ok:true result branch, when `result.antiCopyMatch` is defined (i.e. self-exempt fired), bump `antiCopyRejects.bySource[result.antiCopyMatch.source]` and append to `samples` honoring the existing `ANTI_COPY_SAMPLE_CAP = 20` bound — so D4's QA payload sees self-exemption events under their own bucket without inflating the rejection counters. The D4 invariant `rejectionReasons.copied_seed_hook == bySource.corpus + bySource.style_defs` still holds (style_defs_self is ADDITIONAL to those two, not part of the rejection sum). **Tests `lib/__tests__/d15AltSelfRecipeExempt.test.ts` (NEW, 3 cases):** (a) self-recipe single-word swap (4-token style_defs example with last token replaced by `"kettle"`) PASSES with `reason: null` + `antiCopyMatch.source === "style_defs_self"` + correct hash; (b) the SAME swapped hook with a deliberately-wrong `originatingSeedHash: "deadbeef"` STILL REJECTS through the unigram fallback as `copied_seed_hook` with `source: "style_defs"` (proves the exemption is hash-gated, not blanket); (c) corpus-source match (short corpus hook with last token swapped, candidate falsely advertising the corpus hook's hash as `originatingSeedHash`) STILL REJECTS as `copied_seed_hook` with `source: "corpus"` (proves the exemption is style_defs-only, hash check alone isn't enough). All three cases self-skip with a console.warn rather than spurious-fail if no short style_defs example or short corpus hook can be found in the current catalog (forward-compat for future fixture moves). **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean (no lumina surface touched — included for parity since Y14 also shipped this session); full api-server vitest run = **16 files / 131 tests passing** (was 128 pre-D15-alt; +3 new D15-alt cases, ZERO regressions in the existing 5 D4 telemetry tests despite the union widening — `toBe("corpus")` / `toBe("style_defs")` assertions are forward-compat with the wider type); api-server boots clean (Y8 boot-floor + D14 corpus boot asserts unaffected); healthz 200. **Frozen scope:** Phases 3, 3B-D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C-F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y14, D1, D2-reverted, D3, D4, D5, D5-QA, D14, D15 — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape / DB schema / Claude-cost changes. Long-hook bigram gate at 0.85 Jaccard intentionally NOT exempted (per T003 plan — that gate catches genuine near-verbatims across templates and against the originator alike); `ideaScorer.ts:1926` legacy `validateAntiCopy` caller still uses the back-compat wrapper unchanged.

- **PHASE Y14 — Refresh-vs-initial calibration modal copy + 90→30 day stale window (ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API changes; pure copy + threshold tweak + UI prop addition).** User-requested follow-up to Y13's calibration-stale infrastructure: the 90-day window was too lenient (taste drift well within 30 days for active creators) and the same modal text shipped on first-run AND on a refresh, so a user who'd already calibrated saw "let's set up your taste profile" again instead of an honest "this is 30+ days old, let's refresh it" framing. **Threshold change (server + mobile in lockstep — both must agree or the server's stale check disagrees with what the client decides to surface):** `artifacts/api-server/src/lib/tasteCalibration.ts` `DEFAULT_CALIBRATION_STALE_DAYS` 90→30; `artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteCalibration.ts` mirror constant `CALIBRATION_STALE_DAYS` 90→30. Y13's stale-detection wiring (server returns `staleSince` in the GET /me/calibration response, mobile Home shows the soft-banner when present) is unchanged structurally — only the threshold moved. **Component prop addition (`artifacts/lumina/components/onboarding/TasteCalibration.tsx`):** new optional `mode?: "initial" | "refresh"` prop (defaults to `"initial"` so MvpOnboarding's L514 caller — which has no calibration history yet by definition — stays byte-identical). When `mode === "refresh"`: kicker reads "Quick refresh" (was: "Calibrate your taste"); step-0 hero reads "Your taste profile is 30+ days old — let's refresh it" (was: the first-run hero); confirmation-screen kicker reads "Refreshed" (was: "Calibrated"). All other strings, the 9-pair forced-choice flow, the rejection-gate logic, and the submit handler are byte-identical between modes — only the framing copy changes so the user sees an honest "your taste shifts; let's recalibrate" rather than a confused "let's set this up again". **Route-level mode derivation (`artifacts/lumina/app/calibration.tsx`):** on mount, fetches the server's calibration record via the existing GET /me/calibration hook and sets `mode = (cal.completedAt && !cal.skipped) ? "refresh" : "initial"`. Fail-open: if the fetch errors or returns 404, mode falls back to `"initial"` so the user is never shown a misleading "refresh" framing for a calibration that doesn't actually exist server-side. The route ONLY runs from the Home soft-banner CTA (Y13 wiring) — first-run onboarding goes through MvpOnboarding which omits the prop and gets the default `"initial"`. **Y13 comment update (`artifacts/lumina/app/(tabs)/index.tsx`):** the Y13 inline comment on the Home soft-banner now reads "30+ days old" instead of "90+ days old" so future maintainers reading the comment match the actual constant. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean; api-server vitest 131/131 (no calibration-window tests existed pre-Y14 to update — the 30-day constant is referenced by integration paths whose unit tests stub the staleness flag directly); api-server boots clean; healthz 200. **Frozen scope:** ZERO DB schema / migration / cache-shape / Claude-cost / HTTP-API surface changes (the GET /me/calibration response shape is unchanged; only the SERVER's interpretation of "stale" tightens from 90 → 30 days, computed server-side from `completedAt`); MvpOnboarding L514 default-`"initial"` path preserved byte-identical so the first-run flow is unaffected. D15 captures 12 recurring D14 corpus shapes as `${anchor}` / `${action}` / `${actionPast}` / `${ingForm}` substitution templates in `lib/voiceClusters.ts hookTemplates`, 3 per cluster, each marked `// PHASE D15`. Replaced with `"the ${anchor} itself became 'at least i tried' again"` (~66 score) which preserves the same X-became-Y truism shape while ALSO landing on a more universal admission ("at least i tried" reads as the user's voice across more anchors than the literal corpus shape did) — the assert now passes for all 12 new templates. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; vitest 131/131 (template count is asserted by `voiceClusters.ts` boot logic at module load — assert passes means the test count is unaffected because no test iterates the template array); api-server boots clean (assert chain: corpus integrity → voiceClusters Y8 floor for all 12 new D15 templates → `Server listening port 8080`); healthz 200. **Frozen scope:** ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; per-cluster lengthTargetWords caps unchanged; the cohesive author's `pickTemplate` rotation logic unchanged — D15 only widens the array it picks from. The D14 corpus remains pure training reference (never shipped verbatim per D3); D15 templates are abstracted patterns that DO ship verbatim post-substitution (this is the design — see D3 for the corpus vs template distinction).
