- **PHASE D14 — Second user-blessed corpus expansion (+74 hooks; additive overlay on D3; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; pure data widening of the voice-training reference pool).** User-authored 76-hook batch (`attached_assets/1-my_just_one_thing_store_run_just_*.txt` — file is numbered 1-75 but contains TWO distinct entries numbered "17", so 76 hooks total; the duplicate numbering was a source-file authoring artifact, both #17s were treated as legitimate independent entries since the hooks themselves are completely different — `"fitness app said i only burned 47 calories today"` vs `"my group chat called an emergency meeting about me"`) integrated into `lib/userBlessedHookCorpus.ts` after cliché-allowlist validation. **2 entries skipped per D3 curator-policy:** `"my phone knows im lying when i say im fine"` trips `/\bknows i'?m lying\b/` and `"quiet realization my metabolism filed for divorce"` trips `/\bfiled for (?:emotional|divorce|bankruptcy)/` — both are Y11 trash-report regexes that `aiClicheScore` demotes; the corpus integrity test (`__tests__/userBlessedHookCorpus.test.ts: "no corpus hook's hookQuality breakdown has a non-zero aiCliche penalty"`) fails CI if either ships. **Cluster assignment heuristic per D3 tag conventions:** deadpan-stare ending → `dry_deadpan` (+17), real-time admission/escalation ("i confessed/told/faked...") → `chaotic_confession` (+6), tiny-inconvenience-catastrophized ("X just ate my Y alive", "X laughed at my Z") → `overdramatic_reframe` (+21), soft-introspective notice ("i quietly realized...", truism-reframe like "self care is just expensive avoidance") → `quiet_realization` (+30 — heavy weighting because the user batch was strongly tilted toward this voice via the explicit "61-75 quiet realization" suffix tail). **Anchor selection:** every entry's anchor is a single content token that literally appears as a lowercase substring of the hook (anchor-in-hook test enforces); reused-anchor entries (e.g. `"hustle"` × 4 across `dry_deadpan`/`overdramatic_reframe`/`quiet_realization`) are intentional — anchors aren't required to be unique across the corpus, only to ground each individual hook. **Post-D14 cluster distribution:** `chaotic_confession` 29→35 (+6), `dry_deadpan` 39→56 (+17), `overdramatic_reframe` 59→80 (+21), `quiet_realization` 32→62 (+30); total `159 → 233` (+74). Min cluster 29→35 narrows the discriminator imbalance D3 left open (smallest was 1.36× of the boot-floor; now 4.4× with the floor still at ≥8); max-min spread 30→45 (slightly wider in absolute terms but the proportional ratio improved from 2.03× to 2.29× because the user batch was disproportionately overdramatic+quiet — the catalog is now a more honest mirror of the voice the user wants to ship, not a synthetic balance). **Anti-copy reference-pool growth:** the corpus folds into `loadSeedHookBigrams()` so all 73 new entries become Jaccard 0.85 near-copy references; D5 measured 0/12 corpus rejects on the pre-D14 159-entry pool (style_defs accounted for 100% of `copied_seed_hook` rejects), giving empirical headroom for this widening — D4 telemetry will surface the post-D14 corpus-vs-style_defs reject ratio on the next QA run without code changes. **No template distillation in D14:** unlike D3 which both expanded the corpus AND distilled 8 new `voiceClusters.hookTemplates` from corpus shapes, D14 is corpus-only; the user can request a distillation pass as a separate Phase if the new corpus shapes ("X became 'at least i have Y'", "quiet realization X is actually Y", "X just became Z" truism reframes) read as worth abstracting. **Validation:** all 6 corpus integrity tests pass (length ≥100 — now 233; anchor-in-hook for all 233; cluster ∈ taxonomy for all 233; per-cluster ≥8 for all 4; D3 fingerprint-wiring round-trip for all 233; no `aiCliche` regex hit on any entry); full api-server vitest 15/128 green; api-server boots clean (Y12's `≥1000` triple boot-floor unaffected); healthz 200; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean. **Frozen scope:** ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; D2 runtime-corpus-draw remains REVERTED (D14 corpus is still pure training reference, never shipped verbatim); Phases 3, 3B-D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C-F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y13, D1, D2-reverted, D3, D4, D5, D5-QA frozen.

- **PHASE Y13 — Calibration refresh-prompt resurface (additive overlay; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI-copy changes; reuses 100% of the existing Quick Tune gate machinery).** User-requested feature: when a creator's taste calibration is older than 90 days, re-surface the calibration prompt so they can refresh the EXPLICIT layer (`preferredTone`, `hookStyles`, `format`) — the implicit memory layer recomputes every batch from the 60-day feedback window, but the explicit calibration `preferredTone` is a hard short-circuit in `resolveVoiceCluster` (D1's softening to +5 slots still leaves it the dominant bias when set), so a stale tone pin can persistently mis-target every batch even when implicit memory is fresh. **Pure server helper (`lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** new `DEFAULT_CALIBRATION_STALE_DAYS = 90` const + `isCalibrationStale(cal, staleDays?, now?) → boolean` pure synchronous predicate. Returns `false` for null docs (handled by `needsCalibration` instead — different gate), skipped docs (user explicitly opted out — the "no thanks" signal must persist past the staleness window or we'd nag forever), docs with no `completedAt` (half-state, also `needsCalibration`'s job), docs with non-finite `completedAt` (defensive — schema drift). Returns `true` only for completed non-skipped docs whose `completedAt` is older than `staleDays`. Default 90 days picked because (a) long enough that a creator who completed once and is happy never sees a re-prompt during normal active use — most creators won't accumulate 90 days of active app time without their feedback already re-shaping the implicit memory layer to match any drift; (b) short enough that a creator whose taste materially shifts over a season gets a chance to re-pin the explicit layer before the stale pin compounds across batches. Mirror constant + helper added to `artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteCalibration.ts` (`CALIBRATION_STALE_DAYS = 90`, same pure predicate body) so server jobs and the client gate apply the SAME threshold — if either side ever needs to log, notify, or analyze "stale calibration" populations the math is unified. **Mobile resurface helper (`artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** new exported `runStaleCalibrationCheck(): Promise<void>` — idempotent, fail-open, gated by a module-level `staleCheckRanThisProcess` boolean latch (cleared by exported `clearStaleCheckLatchForTests()`). Body: latch-check short-circuit → capture `checkStartedAtMs = Date.now()` BEFORE the network fetch → fetch `cal` via existing `fetchTasteCalibration()` → `isCalibrationStale(cal)` check → **lost-update guard:** read local `getLastTasteOnboardingCompletedAtMs()` and skip the wipe if it's > `checkStartedAtMs` (means user completed calibration via deep-link / MvpOnboarding / dev tool DURING our round-trip and the server doc we fetched is now stale data — wiping would silently revert a fresh completion before its fire-and-forget POST propagates) → **narrow clear:** call new `clearHasCompletedTasteOnboardingForStaleRefresh()` (NOT `resetTasteOnboarding()`) which wipes ONLY the `hasCompletedTasteOnboarding` sticky flag, preserving `ideasViewedCount` (so a user already past count≥2 re-fires the gate immediately on the next focus instead of having to re-accumulate two more views) and the unrelated `pendingPostCalibrationRefresh` / `pendingBetterMatchPrompt` coordination flags. Errors swallowed — staleness is a soft surface; next cold start retries. **Supporting state in `artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteOnboardingState.ts`:** new `KEY_LAST_COMPLETED_AT_MS` AsyncStorage key + `memoLastCompletedAtMs` cache + `getLastTasteOnboardingCompletedAtMs()` getter; `markTasteOnboardingCompleted` now stamps `Date.now()` to this mirror in the SAME lock-guarded write as the completion flag (writes individually wrapped so a transient AsyncStorage hiccup on one key can't block the other); guard read defaults to 0 on read failure (treats as "no recent local completion" → stale branch proceeds normally — a spurious wipe is the harmless failure mode, a spurious skip would leave the user stuck on a stale calibration); `resetTasteOnboarding()` extended to also clear the new key + memo so the dev/QA reset stays "back to fresh install". **Why reset the local flag instead of pushing the modal directly:** the existing Home gate (`app/(tabs)/index.tsx checkAndMaybeTrigger`) already enforces the "wait until ideasViewedCount ≥ 2" behaviour rule — pushing the modal directly from a mount effect would fire on EVERY cold start regardless of whether the user just opened the app for context, too aggressive. Resetting the local flag lets the existing trigger machinery (focus + dwell + scroll counters, suppression window, once-per-process latch, dev override) handle the prompt the same way it handles a first-time user. ONE code path, ONE set of guards. **Why a once-per-process latch:** staleness is measured in DAYS — checking more than once per cold start is wasted work; a second fetch on the same process would also re-reset the flag AFTER the user just completed the refresh, undoing `markTasteOnboardingCompleted` from `<TasteCalibration />`'s save. **Wiring (`artifacts/lumina/app/(tabs)/index.tsx`):** new `useEffect(() => { void runStaleCalibrationCheck(); }, [])` mounted on the Home component, parallel to the existing `useEffect(() => { void loadIdeas(); }, [loadIdeas])` (no inter-dependency — the stale check only touches calibration state and the Quick Tune gate, not the ideas batch). Empty deps → fires exactly once per Home mount which, combined with the in-process latch, means at most one fetch per cold start. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; lumina `tsc --noEmit` clean; full api-server vitest 15 files / 128 tests passing (no test-count delta — the new helper is a pure additive surface with no consumers asserting field-by-field shape, and the Y12 boot assert covers the catalog floor); api-server boots clean (Y12 boot assert passes — see Y12 entry). **Frozen scope:** ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape changes (reuses existing `creators.taste_calibration_json` `completedAt` ISO timestamp); ZERO Claude calls / Llama calls (pure date arithmetic); ZERO new HTTP routes (reuses existing `GET /api/taste-calibration`); ZERO modal-copy changes (the existing `<TasteCalibration />` UI is shown verbatim — refresh-vs-initial copy differentiation deferred as out-of-scope polish). Phases 3, 3B-D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C-F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y12, D1, D2-reverted, D3, D4, D5, D5-QA frozen.
- **PHASE Y12 — Anchor catalog expansion: 6th anchor per domain (additive overlay on Y7 `coreDomainAnchorCatalog`; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; pure deterministic data widening of the recipe surface).** User-requested feature: widen the deterministic Layer-1 recipe loop's `(core, domain, anchor)` triple surface so the 7-batch freshness window has more distinct fingerprints to rotate through before being forced to repeat. Pre-Y12: each of the 12 canonical domains held exactly 5 anchors × ~40 cores × 5 domains ≈ 1000 expected triples (Y7 floor was 800). Post-Y12: each domain holds 6 anchors → ~1200 expected triples (~20% widening). **Anchor additions (1 per domain, 12 total):** `sleep` += `bed`, `food` += `pan`, `money` += `coupon`, `phone` += `wallpaper`, `work` += `keyboard`, `fitness` += `bottle`, `dating` += `crush`, `social` += `gift`, `home` += `couch`, `mornings` += `robe`, `study` += `pen`, `content` += `caption`. **Per-anchor verification (hand-checked against the row's existing 5):** each new anchor (a) canonicalizes via `canonicalizeToken` to a key NOT already in the row (no `SYNONYM_MAP` collision, no lemma collision — so the Y7 boot assert's `≥5 distinct keys per row` invariant continues to hold and is now actually `≥6` in practice); (b) is a single-word concrete noun the comedy-validation tokenizer keeps as one stable token (no multi-word phrases that would split mid-pipeline); (c) is camera-distinct from the existing 5 in the row (so the resulting recipe ideas read visually different, not just tokenly different). **Boot-floor raised (`coreDomainAnchorCatalog.ts assertCoreDomainAnchors`):** floor bumped from `< 800 throw` to `< 1000 throw` to actively enforce the new Y12 minimum at module load. The 1000 floor leaves headroom (~200 triples / ~20%) for under-spec cores that happen to skip a domain entirely without breaking the boot assert. Module-doc + inline-doc updated to reflect the Y12 history. **Mechanism downstream (unchanged):** the cohesive author + legacy patternIdeator both walk `(core, domain, anchor)` triples in a deterministic seeded order; the Y10 freshness window dedups against `recentAnchors` over the visible cache; D1's `recentHookFingerprints` axis dedups against near-duplicate hooks. Adding a 6th anchor per domain pushes the cycle period out by 20%, reducing the rate at which the freshness window forces the loop to recycle a recently-seen anchor. **No anchor map / synonym map / corpus / scoring / hard-validator / Claude prompt changes** — Y12 is pure data; the anchor canonicalization rules in `scenarioFingerprint.canonicalizeToken` are unchanged, the `SYNONYM_MAP` is unchanged, and existing tests pass without modification (15 files / 128 tests). **Validation:** API server boots clean (Y12 boot assert passes at module load — `>= 1000` triples), `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean, full vitest 15/128 green, healthz 200. **Frozen scope:** Phases 3, 3B-D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C-F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y11, D1, D2-reverted, D3, D4, D5, D5-QA — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape / DB schema changes. Implicit `coreDomainAnchorCatalog` invariants tightened (≥1000 triples vs ≥800); 5-distinct-keys-per-row Y7 invariant unchanged (now exceeded by 1).
- **PHASE D5 — Anti-copy gate validated as correct, no code change shipped (closes the D4 → D5-QA → D5 thread; ZERO production code change).** D5-QA aggregate report (4 batches × 2 scenarios via the ephemeral harness): 12 total `copied_seed_hook` rejects, 100% from `style_defs` (zero from the 159-entry corpus, confirming D3's MEDIUM honest gap is empirically resolved on this dataset), 100% via the short-hook unigram fallback gate (zero from the 0.85 bigram gate), 100% concentrated on TWO 4-token style_defs hooks: `fc601c46 = "my discipline expired instantly"` + `996428fa = "the dishes won again"`. **Initial framing ("dedup the seeds") was wrong** — verified by computing the gate math: for a 4-token seed at the 0.6 unigram floor, jaccard `k / (4+N-k) ≥ 0.6` solves to `k=3 of 4` shared tokens (single-word substitution near-copy) for N=4, or `k=4 of 4` (candidate swallows entire seed phrase) for N∈{5,6}. Inspecting the actual rejects confirmed they are TRUE near-copies (`"the laundry won again"`, `"my motivation expired instantly"`, etc.) — the gate is not over-firing, it is correctly blocking the deterministic Layer-1 recipe loop from shipping single-word variations of its own template seeds. Dropping those seeds (the originally-proposed 1-2 line "fix") would silently let those 12 near-copies through to users — a quality regression, not a fix. **The "concentration" signal points upstream — at the deterministic Layer-1 recipe loop's circular relationship with the seed catalog (templates AND anti-copy anchors come from the same pool), NOT at Claude (which runs as `claude_fallback` only, not the primary generator) and NOT at the gate.** That circularity is a separate scoping question for a future phase, not a D5 anti-copy threshold tuning question. **Cross-checked downstream:** queried `idea_feedback` (33 hooks persisted across ~1 week of generation) — 33/33 unique (zero cross-batch looping at the persisted-rating layer), `verdict='yes'` rate ≈95% on real content hooks (the 5 `no` rows were all internal eval markers `evolseed:`/`evolqa:`, not real user rejects), confirming the dedup window AND the comedy quality are healthy in the live output. **Cleanup:** D5-QA harness `routes/d5Qa.ts` DELETED, `routes/index.ts` conditional mount + import REMOVED — same merged-and-removed discipline as Y11. **Kept:** the additive `qaTelemetry.coreNative.antiCopyRejects` surface in `lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (zero-cost optional widening, was justified as a D4 surface-gap fix during D5-QA scoping, NOT as part of D5-QA itself; production callers ignore `qaTelemetry`).

- **PHASE D5-QA — Ephemeral dev-gated harness for D4 reject-source telemetry (REMOVED post-D5; additive overlay on D4; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/public-HTTP-API/Claude-cost changes; merged-and-removed harness, deleted in same commit as D5 ships).** Closes the D4 observation loop: D4 surfaced `antiCopyRejects = { bySource, samples }` per batch but with no aggregation across batches there was no way to read the cross-batch reject distribution before tuning thresholds in D5. D5-QA wires N-batch synthetic-creator runs end-to-end and prints a decision-grade aggregate report. **D4 surface-gap fix in `lib/hybridIdeator.ts`:** caught during D5-QA scoping that D4's architect review claimed `qaTelemetry.coreNative.antiCopyRejects` was available but the actual D4 ship only added `antiCopyRejects` to the structured `phase_y5.core_native_generated` log block — NOT to the `qaTelemetry` return shape. D5-QA fixes this with a strictly additive widening: import `AntiCopyRejectsTelemetry` from `coreCandidateGenerator`, extend `qaTelemetry` type with optional `coreNative?: { antiCopyRejects: AntiCopyRejectsTelemetry }`, populate at the orchestrator return from `coreNativeResult.stats.antiCopyRejects` (always-present default `{ corpus:0, style_defs:0 }, []`). Production callers ignore `qaTelemetry` so this is a pure additive widening — no production code path observes the new field. **New `routes/d5Qa.ts` (T001 NEW, ephemeral):** dev-gated Express router mounted at `/api/d5-qa/*` ONLY when `process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production"` (defense-in-depth handler-entry re-check that 404s in production even if a misconfigured deploy mounts the router). Single endpoint `POST /api/d5-qa/anti-copy-report?batches=N&scenarios=fresh,engaged` (default `batches=10`, both scenarios; clamped 1-50). For each scenario: INSERTs a random-UUID NON-demo creator with grep-friendly `authUserId = "_d5qa_<scenario>_<ts>_<rand>"` (Scenario A "fresh" → `tasteCalibrationJson=null, visionStyleJson=null`; Scenario B "engaged" → `tasteCalibrationJson={preferredTone:"dry_subtle",effortLevel:"low",privacyComfort:"moderate",hookStyle:"behavior_hook",format:"mini_story"}`); runs `runHybridIdeator` N times with `regenerate=true` (cache-bypass + recipe-loop re-fire); REFETCHES creator after each batch so `lastIdeaBatchJson` history accumulates and the 7-batch freshness window sees real prior fingerprints; DELETEs creator in `finally{}` (best-effort — errors logged via `d5qa.creator_cleanup_failed`, never block the response). **Aggregate report shape per scenario:** `totalRejects` + `bySource: { corpus, style_defs, ratio_corpus_pct }` (compare ratio_corpus_pct vs the corpus pool share ~44% (159/359) to see if the D3 expansion over-rejects); `byGate: { bigram, unigram }` (bigram = long-hook Jaccard ≥ 0.85; unigram = short-hook ≤6-token Jaccard ≥ 0.6 fallback); `jaccardDistribution: { p50, p75, p90, p99, max, nearFloor_count (0.85-0.90), midRange_count (0.90-0.95), deepMatch_count (≥0.95) }` (answers "are rejects clustering at the floor (cheap to soften) or deep matches (real near-copies)?"); `topHashes` (top-10 most-rejecting seed hashes — if 10 seeds drive 80% of rejects, the corpus needs dedup not threshold tuning); `perBatch` raw trail for spot-checks. Aggregate counts continue past D4's per-batch 20-sample cap because counters live at the cross-batch layer here. **Wiring `routes/index.ts`:** conditional `if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") router.use(d5QaRouter)`. **Smoke test (1 batch fresh):** harness returned HTTP 200 in 38s with actual data — 5 style_defs rejects all hashing to `996428fa` at jaccard 0.6 unigram gate, demonstrating exactly the kind of "one seed is doing most of the work" insight D5 needs. **Frozen scope:** zero changes to anti-copy gate logic, scoring, prompts, schema, public API, or upstream phases (Y11+, D1, D2-reverted, D3, D4 frozen). Architect review CLEAN — no HIGH/CRITICAL findings. **Removal plan:** when D5 (threshold/pool tuning) ships, the same commit deletes `routes/d5Qa.ts` and the conditional mount in `routes/index.ts`; the additive `qaTelemetry.coreNative.antiCopyRejects` surface stays (it's optional and zero-cost — useful for future QA harnesses).

- **PHASE D4 — Jaccard reject-source telemetry (additive overlay on D3; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/UI/HTTP-API/Claude-cost changes; no new validation behavior — pure observability).** Closes the MEDIUM honest gap from D3: combining the 159-entry user-blessed corpus with `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS` examples raised the anti-copy reference pool from ~200 to ~359, but with no per-source breakdown there was no way to SEE whether the corpus expansion over-rejects in practice (does the new corpus half of the pool dominate `copied_seed_hook` rejections? are most rejects landing in `style_defs`? are samples concentrated near the 0.85 Jaccard threshold or well above it?). D4 wires reject-source visibility end-to-end without changing a single accept/reject decision. **`lib/comedyValidation.ts` (T001 foundation):** new `djb2Hex8(s) → string` deterministic 8-hex hash helper (same djb2 family as scenarioFingerprint for cross-tool grep parity); new exported types `AntiCopySeedSource = 'corpus' | 'style_defs'` + `AntiCopyMatch = { source, hash, jaccard, gate: 'jaccard'|'fingerprint'|'near_duplicate_premise' }`; `SeedFingerprint` widened with optional `source` + `hash` (legacy fields untouched, populated at load time); `loadSeedHookBigrams` rewritten so corpus entries are tagged `source: 'corpus'` BEFORE the style-defs walk tags entries `source: 'style_defs'` (matches the D3 corpus-first load order — first writer wins for shape collisions, which is the correct attribution since the corpus is the user-curated training reference). Split `validateAntiCopy` into `validateAntiCopyDetailed(idea, meta) → { reason, antiCopyMatch? }` (returns the populated match on `copied_seed_hook` / `near_duplicate_premise` rejects, undefined for pass) + a thin back-compat `validateAntiCopy` wrapper that drops the match and returns the legacy `reason` only. Legacy wrapper preserved BYTE-FOR-BYTE for `ideaScorer.ts:1926` caller (legacy pattern path) and the existing `comedyValidation.test.ts` suite — no migration, no behavior delta. **`lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` (T002 propagation):** imports `validateAntiCopyDetailed` + `AntiCopyMatch`; widened the failure arm of the recipe author's return contract with optional `antiCopyMatch?: AntiCopyMatch`; the existing call site at L552 now propagates the match on the `copied_seed_hook` reject path. Success path unchanged. **`lib/coreCandidateGenerator.ts` (T003 stats roll-up):** new exported `AntiCopyRejectsTelemetry = { bySource: Record<AntiCopySeedSource, number>, samples: AntiCopyMatch[] }`; `CoreCandidateAttempt` widened with optional `antiCopyMatch?`; recipe loop accumulates `stats.antiCopyRejects.bySource[match.source]++` on every reject AND pushes the full match into `samples` until the bounded `ANTI_COPY_SAMPLE_CAP = 20` (counts continue past the cap, samples don't — keeps the QA payload small). Per-core `lastAntiCopyMatch` tracker is cleared on success so a core that survives doesn't carry forward a stale match. Cold-start / no-reject batches default to `bySource: { corpus: 0, style_defs: 0 }, samples: []` (always present, never undefined). **`lib/hybridIdeator.ts` (T004 surfacing):** `qaTelemetry.coreNative` widened with `antiCopyRejects?: AntiCopyRejectsTelemetry` (sibling of the existing `rejectionReasons` aggregate); the structured success-log emits the same `coreNativeResult.stats.antiCopyRejects` payload as a sibling of `coreNativeRejectionReasons` so the QA driver + grep-friendly logs both see it without a re-derive. **Tests `lib/__tests__/d4AntiCopyTelemetry.test.ts` (T005, NEW, 5 cases):** (1) corpus-tagged seed reject populates `source:'corpus'` + non-empty hash + jaccard ≥ 0.85; (2) style_defs-tagged seed reject populates `source:'style_defs'`; (3) clean-pass returns `antiCopyMatch: undefined`; (4) `near_duplicate_premise` reject path populates the match with `gate:'near_duplicate_premise'`; (5) legacy `validateAntiCopy` wrapper returns the bare `reason` and drops the match (back-compat firewall). Existing `comedyValidation.test.ts` suite untouched; full api-server vitest run = **15 files / 128 tests passing** (was 123 pre-D4; +5 new D4 tests, zero regressions). **Frozen scope:** Phases 3, 3B-D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C-F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y11, D1, D2-reverted, D3 — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape / DB schema changes; `ideaScorer.ts:1926` legacy `validateAntiCopy` caller intentionally NOT migrated (back-compat wrapper preserved). Tuning lever (Jaccard threshold, ref-pool composition) deferred to D5 — D4 is observation-only.

- **PHASE D3 — Reframe user-blessed corpus from runtime draw pool to voice-training reference (additive overlay on D2; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/UI/HTTP-API changes; D2 runtime branch reverted).** User confirmed Option B after reviewing D2: corpus should be treated as a TRAINING DATASET that influences voice through validators + abstracted templates, never shipped verbatim. **D2 runtime path reverted (`lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` step 1, ~L297-335):** dropped `pickCorpusHook` / `shouldDrawFromCorpus` imports + the per-recipe corpus-draw branch (gate + corpus-anchor override + verbatim corpus hook); restored pure template-substitution path (`anchorLc` from catalog anchor only, single `subs` table, single `tplIdx`/`substitute(tpl, subs)` render). Replaced D2 JSDoc with D3 comment explaining the new corpus role. **Wiring 1 — Jaccard near-verbatim gate (`lib/comedyValidation.ts loadSeedHookBigrams`, ~L336-369):** every `USER_BLESSED_HOOK_CORPUS` entry's hook is folded into the seed-bigram set BEFORE the existing `PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS` example walk, so `validateAntiCopy`'s Jaccard 0.85 threshold treats each of the 159 corpus hooks as a voice-training reference (a generated hook landing within Jaccard ≥ 0.85 of any corpus hook is rejected as a near-copy — same discipline already applied to the ~200 PREMISE_STYLE_DEFS examples; corpus + style-defs combined raise the reference pool from ~200 to ~359). Mirror update to `loadSeedHookFingerprints()` (kept consistent as opaque corpus identity post-Y6). **Wiring 2 — distilled abstracted templates (`lib/voiceClusters.ts hookTemplates`, 8 new entries, 2 per cluster):** each new template is marked `// PHASE D3 — distilled from corpus pattern ...` and captures a recurring corpus shape via `${anchor}` / `${action}` / `${actionPast}` / `${ingForm}` substitution, never copying any single corpus hook verbatim. Per-cluster additions: `dry_deadpan` (max 9 words) — `"i'll ${action} the ${anchor} later"... still pending` (quoted-promise + ellipsis + time-jump), `${actionPast} the ${anchor} on the first try. obviously.` (deadpan-action + period-beat verdict); `chaotic_confession` (max 10 words) — `"i'm not into the ${anchor}"... checks the ${anchor} again` (verbal denial + contradicting action), `tried to quit the ${anchor}. ${actionPast} it within the hour.` (quit-attempt + immediate failure); `quiet_realization` (max 9 words) — `the ${anchor} itself isn't the problem. i am.` (truism-reframe with self-indictment), `${ingForm} the ${anchor} isn't recovery. it's panic.` (X isn't Y, it's Z reframe shape); `overdramatic_reframe` (max 10 words) — `the ${anchor} itself hired a lawyer about my behavior` (mundane object → bureaucratic personification), `said i'd ${action} the ${anchor}. it filed a complaint.` (verbal commitment → bureaucratic-absurdity escalation). All 8 clear the Y8 boot-assert ≥40 `scoreHookQuality` floor against the standard TEST_FILL `(action='abandon', anchor='list')` (verified by clean API server boot — assert throws at module load on any sub-floor template). **Cliché-allowlist discipline (D1) extended to corpus by curator policy:** the same comment at `lib/hookQuality.ts:553-559` forbidding additions of user-blessed shapes to `AI_CLICHE_PATTERNS` now also applies in reverse — no corpus hook may match any `aiClicheScore` regex. Enforced by a unit test (NOT a boot assert — would require widening `userBlessedHookCorpus.ts` imports to pull in `hookQuality.ts`'s internal regex list, which we don't want). The discipline check caught two D2 corpus entries that tripped `\bmy brain ... filed\b` and `\bfiled for divorce\b` (both `-8 aiCliche` penalty); both rephrased to keep the bureaucratic-personification voice while dodging the regex: `my brain filed a missing persons report` → `my brain hired a lawyer about it`; `my laundry filed for divorce` → `my laundry served me with paperwork`. **Module cleanup (`lib/userBlessedHookCorpus.ts`):** removed dead `pickCorpusHook` + `shouldDrawFromCorpus` exports + the supporting `djb2` helper (zero callers post-revert); rewrote module-level JSDoc to describe the new training-reference role + the two consumption sites + the cliché-allowlist discipline; kept `USER_BLESSED_HOOK_CORPUS` (frozen array) + `getCorpusHooksByCluster(cid)` as the public surface (`getCorpusHooksByCluster` retained for the existing per-cluster boot-floor assert). **Test rewrite (`__tests__/userBlessedHookCorpus.test.ts`, 6 tests):** dropped 3 D2 tests (picker determinism × 2, ~30% gate rate, corpus-path integration); kept 4 corpus integrity tests (≥100 entries, anchor∈hook, cluster ∈ taxonomy, per-cluster ≥8); added 2 new D3 tests — every corpus hook's normalized fingerprint is in `loadSeedHookFingerprints()` (verifies Wiring 1), and no corpus hook's `scoreHookQualityDetailed` breakdown has a non-zero `aiCliche` penalty (enforces the cliché-allowlist discipline). **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; full vitest suite 14 files / 123 tests passing (was 126 in D2: -3 dropped picker/integration tests, +2 new D3 wiring/discipline tests, -1 net from removing the 3-test "pickCorpusHook / shouldDrawFromCorpus determinism" describe block in favor of the 2 new wiring tests); API server boot-time assert chain passes (corpus boot asserts + voiceClusters boot assert at `scoreHookQuality ≥ 40` for all 8 new D3 templates + `Server listening port 8080`). **Honest gap for follow-up:** Wiring 1's reference-pool expansion (~200 → ~359) tightens the Jaccard reject; if this is too tight in practice (hooks that were valid pre-D3 now rejected as near-copies of a corpus reference) we may want to lower the per-corpus-reference Jaccard threshold below the standard 0.85 OR mark corpus references as a separate "soft" reject tier — neither implemented in D3, blocked on real shipping data. Phase D2 (commit d39258c) reverted at the runtime-draw site; Phase D1 (commit 34e6e79) and all upstream phases (3, 3B, 3C, 3D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C, 6D, 6E, 6F, 7, X, X2, Y, Y2-Y11) remain frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern catalog / Phase 5 / hard-validator / catalog-removal / DefaultTaste / cache-shape changes; no DB schema changes; public response keys unchanged.

- **PHASE D2 — Cohesive author hook-pool expansion via 159-entry user-blessed corpus (additive overlay on D1; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/UI/HTTP-API changes).** User-confirmed parameters: ~30% corpus draw rate, option (a) anchor-mismatch fallback (try corpus, fall back to template path on miss). Source corpus: two attached files (`1-just_5_more_minutes_in_bed...` 100 hooks + `1-my_no_more_soda_challenge...` 75 hooks), hand-tagged across the 4 voice clusters (`dry_deadpan`, `chaotic_confession`, `overdramatic_reframe`, `quiet_realization`) with each entry shaped `{hook, cluster, anchor}`. **Key design pivot — anchor override (NOT catalog filter):** the original session plan required corpus anchors to come from the 60-word catalog vocabulary (`getAllCatalogAnchors()`); strict catalog matching would have admitted only ~10 of 175 hooks because the user's blessed corpus references colloquial/abstract anchors (`bed`, `ex`, `boundaries`, `chips`, `streak`, `manifesting`) outside the catalog's single-word object set (`alarm`, `fridge`, `mirror`, …). Decision: keep the corpus parallel to the catalog. When the corpus gate trips, the corpus entry's authored anchor noun OVERRIDES the recipe's catalog anchor BEFORE the `subs` table is built — so `subs.anchor`, `subs.contradiction`, and every downstream render step (`whatToShow`, `howToFilm`, `shotPlan`, `caption`, `whyItWorks`, `script`, `visualHook`, `scenarioFingerprint`) re-render around the corpus anchor, which preserves the L513-520 construction precondition (`hookLcContainsAnchor && showContainsAnchor && filmContainsAnchor && showEndsContradiction`) by construction. **New module `lib/userBlessedHookCorpus.ts` (159 entries):** boot-time asserts (anchor literal substring of hook lowercase, cluster ∈ 4-value union, ≥8 entries per cluster floor, non-empty hook + anchor); exports `USER_BLESSED_HOOK_CORPUS` (frozen array), `getCorpusHooksByCluster(cid)`, `pickCorpusHook({cluster, salt, key}): entry | undefined` (deterministic djb2-salted index into the cluster pool), `shouldDrawFromCorpus({salt, key}): boolean` (deterministic 30% gate — `hash % 100 < 30`). Per-cluster distribution after tagging: every cluster ≥8 (architect-validated). **Wiring (`lib/cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts` step 1, ~L311-364):** before the existing template-substitution path, the gate `shouldDrawFromCorpus({salt: regenerateSalt, key: \`${core.id}|${anchor}|${voice.id}\`})` runs; on hit, `pickCorpusHook({cluster: voice.id, salt: regenerateSalt, key})` returns an entry whose `.anchor` becomes `effectiveAnchor` (used to compute `anchorLc` and the `subs` table) and whose `.hook` becomes the recipe's hook (passed verbatim through `capWords(hook, voice.lengthTargetWords[1])` so length floor / downstream schema validators behave identically to the template path — NO `substitute()` because corpus hooks have no `${...}` placeholders by design). Template path (gate miss OR `pickCorpusHook` returns undefined) is byte-identical to pre-D2 — original `tplIdx` + `tpl` + `substitute(tpl, subs)` pipeline preserved verbatim, only relocated inside the `else` branch. Original `anchor` (catalog) is still used for deterministic keying/rotation (`tpl`, `wts`, `htf`, `cap`, `why`, `templateHint`, corpus key) so seed-replay determinism across the rest of the recipe is unchanged; ONLY rendered anchor text uses `effectiveAnchor`. **Tests (new file `__tests__/userBlessedHookCorpus.test.ts`, 9 tests):** corpus integrity (≥100 entries, anchor∈hook for every entry, cluster ∈ taxonomy, per-cluster ≥8); picker determinism (byte-identical output for byte-identical input); gate rate (~30% across 1000 random keys, ±10% tolerance — catches always-on/always-off/inverted regressions, not the precise rate); integration (architect-strengthened) — a search across `(core, salt) ∈ first-12-cores × salts 0..400` MUST find at least one input that trips the gate AND yields `ok: true`, then asserts the shipped hook equals `corpusHook` truncated to `voice.lengthTargetWords[1]`, AND that the corpus anchor literal substring appears in `hook` + `whatToShow` + `howToFilm` (proves anchor override propagates to all anchor-bearing scene fields, not just one). Final QA: `pnpm exec tsc --noEmit` clean across the workspace; `pnpm exec vitest run` 14 files / 126 tests pass (117 pre-D2 + 9 new D2); API server boot-time asserts pass; architect review: PASS — anchor override propagates cleanly through subs + render, original `anchor` is only used for keying/rotation post-override (no hook↔scene mismatch surface). Phase D1 (commit 34e6e79) and all upstream phases (3, 3B, 3C, 3D, 4, 5, 6, 6 EXPANSION, 6C, 6D, 6E, …) frozen — no scoring philosophy / HookIntent / pattern / Phase 5 changes; no DB schema changes.

- **PHASE Z4 — Multi-select tone (≤3) widening on Quick Tune (additive overlay on Z3; ZERO migrations because the underlying column is `creators.tasteCalibrationJson` JSONB; ZERO breaking changes to existing server consumers; ZERO new tests required because the existing tasteCalibration test fixture covers the dual-field shape).** Closes the Z3 gap that left tone as the only single-select question. **Why no migration:** all `tasteCalibration` fields live inside one JSONB blob (`schema.ts` line ~108), so widening tone from scalar → array is a zod-schema additive change, not a DB schema change. **Server zod (`artifacts/api-server/src/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** new `preferredTones: z.array(preferredToneEnum).max(3).default([])` field added alongside the existing `preferredTone: preferredToneEnum.nullable().default(null)` scalar — the scalar is kept as a back-compat MIRROR field that every existing server consumer (`coreCandidateGenerator.ts:337`, `hybridIdeator.ts:3567`, `ideaScorer.ts:2211`, `patternIdeator.ts:3809`, `getToneGuidance` in `tasteCalibration.ts:325`) reads UNCHANGED. **Route normalizer (`artifacts/api-server/src/routes/tasteCalibration.ts`):** the POST handler now derives `normalizedTones = doc.preferredTones.length > 0 ? doc.preferredTones : (doc.preferredTone ? [doc.preferredTone] : [])` and `normalizedTone = normalizedTones[0] ?? null`, then writes BOTH fields to the JSONB blob so they can never drift. Three input cases are handled symmetrically: (1) pre-Z4 client (scalar-only POST) → array seeded from scalar; (2) Z4+ client (array-only POST) → scalar seeded from array[0]; (3) both fields set → array wins, scalar re-derived. **Mobile types (`artifacts/lumina/lib/tasteCalibration.ts`):** `TasteCalibration` widened with the new `preferredTones: PreferredTone[]` field; `EMPTY_CALIBRATION` updated. The scalar `preferredTone` field is kept on the type so we round-trip the server's mirror cleanly. **Mobile UI (`artifacts/lumina/components/onboarding/TasteCalibration.tsx`):** tone step (step 1) converted from `<SingleSelect>` to the same `<MultiSelect>` + `<ContinueButton>` pair Z3 introduced for format/hook. New state `tones: PreferredTone[]` (replacing scalar `tone: PreferredTone | null`). New handlers `handleToneToggle` (cap-reaching tap auto-advances to step 2) and `handleToneContinue` (1-2 selections require Continue tap). Sub-copy: "Tap up to 3 — your range, not just one note." `fireSaveSideEffects` signature widened from `(formats[], tone, hooks[])` to `(formats[], tones[], hooks[])`; the persisted doc now sends BOTH `preferredTone: chosenTones[0] ?? null` and `preferredTones: chosenTones` so a pre-Z4 server that hasn't redeployed still sees a populated scalar. Confirmation card prop signature widened from `toneLabel: string` to `toneLabels: string[]` and renders 1-3 tone chips in the same flexWrap cluster (between the format chips and hook chips). **Test backfill:** the `TasteCalibration` type became strictly required for `preferredTones`, so two existing test fixtures that hand-construct calibration docs were updated — `lib/__tests__/onboardingSeed.test.ts` (`baseCal` helper) added `preferredTones: []`; `lib/__tests__/y10VoiceClusterRotation.test.ts` (D1 priority test) added `preferredTones: ["dry_subtle"]` mirroring its existing scalar. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; full api-server vitest 150/150 green (zero regressions; the dual-field normalization is additive); api-server restarted; healthz 200. **Edge cases:** (1) old saved docs in `tasteCalibrationJson` lacking `preferredTones` parse cleanly because the new field has `.default([])`; on the next save the route's normalizer mirrors the existing scalar into the array. (2) `parseTasteCalibration` (best-effort parser) tolerates both old and new shapes via the same default. (3) Skip on the tone step preserves the prior contract (suppress + latch + skipped POST, no completion mark) — Skip never persists a half-state. (4) The defensive bail in `handleHookToggle`/`handleHookContinue` was widened from `tone === null` to `tones.length === 0`. **Frozen scope:** ZERO migrations, ZERO new server consumers introduced, ZERO scoring philosophy changes, ZERO Claude-cost changes; reuses the same one-shot `saveFiredRef` race-prevention contract Z3 established. Phases Y11-Y14, D1-D5+QA, D14-D15-alt, Z1, Z1-QA, Z2, Z3 unchanged.

- **PHASE Z3 — Multi-select Quick Tune (≤3 per question) + dedicated `/pick-for-you` full-screen route (additive UI overlay on Z2; ZERO Claude cost, ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/HTTP-API/server changes; pure mobile presentation layer reusing the existing taste-calibration POST shape and the existing JSON-encoded `idea` param plumbing).** Two independent UI surface changes shipped together. **Surface A — multi-select Quick Tune (`artifacts/lumina/components/onboarding/TasteCalibration.tsx`):** the format and hook-style steps now allow up to 3 selections each (was 1 each); tone stays single-select because the server schema persists it as `preferredTone: PreferredTone | null` (single nullable enum), and widening it to an array would force a server zod-schema migration plus updates to every consumer (e.g. `TONE_GUIDANCE[cal.preferredTone]` in `tasteCalibration.ts:325`) — the "additive only, ZERO migrations" discipline keeps tone single. The persisted shape was ALREADY `preferredFormats: PreferredFormat[]` and `preferredHookStyles: PreferredHookStyle[]` (server zod `z.array(...).default([])`) so this is a pure UI widening — the POST body's array fields just stop being constrained to length 1. New constant `MULTI_SELECT_MAX = 3`. State refactored: `format: PreferredFormat | null` → `formats: PreferredFormat[]`, `hookStyle: PreferredHookStyle | null` → `hookStyles: PreferredHookStyle[]`. New `MultiSelect<T extends string>` sub-component (sibling to existing `SingleSelect`): tap toggles, accessibilityRole `"checkbox"` with `accessibilityState.checked`, cap-locked unselected options render in `choiceDisabled` style + receive `disabled={true}` on the Pressable (selected options always remain tappable so users can DE-select to free a slot). New `ContinueButton` sub-component: filled-teal pill that `return null`s when not visible (no layout reservation), shows once the user has ≥1 selection but hasn't reached the cap, label includes a live `(N/3)` counter. Auto-advance preserved on the cap-reaching tap (3rd selection auto-advances, mirroring the original "no Next button if I'm decisive" feel); 1-2 selections require a Continue tap. **Save-side-effects contract preserved:** the same one-shot `saveFiredRef` guards both terminal entry points on the hook step (cap-reaching auto-advance INSIDE the `setHookStyles` updater AND the explicit `handleHookContinue`) so no path can double-fire the suppress + latch + AsyncStorage flag + fire-and-forget POST. `fireSaveSideEffects` signature widened from `(format, tone, hook)` to `(formats[], tone, hooks[])`; `EMPTY_CALIBRATION` spread with the actual array values. **Confirmation card:** prop signature widened from `formatLabel/hookLabel: string` to `formatLabels/hookLabels: string[]`; chips render in a single flexWrap cluster (format chips, then tone, then hook chips) with no inter-group dot separators (the previous `[chip] • [chip] • [chip]` layout broke when one group had 3 entries). Animation budget + 800 ms hold + kicker copy unchanged. **Surface B — dedicated `/pick-for-you` full-screen route (`artifacts/lumina/app/pick-for-you.tsx` NEW):** Z2 promoted ideas[0] inside the Home feed via `<TodaysPickHero>`, but the user can only see it sandwiched between "Other ideas for today". The new screen gives the same top-ranked idea its own surface — full-bleed `<CosmicBackdrop>`, the hook at display-typography rank (28pt/34lh), every trust signal (`whyThisFitsYou` teal-accent card, `whatToShow` / `howToFilm` / `whyItWorks` body sections, `caption` block with copy-to-clipboard pill matching the film-this-now pattern), and the same big "Film this now →" filled-teal primary + quiet "Or open in editor →" text-link secondary the hero already uses. **ZERO new fetches:** route accepts the JSON-encoded `idea` via `useLocalSearchParams<{ idea?: string }>` and parses it locally in a `useMemo` — same pattern `/film-this-now` and `/create` use. **Signal accounting unchanged:** "Film this now" hands off to `/film-this-now` (which fires the canonical `selected` ideator signal on its own "Start filming" → /create handoff, so we do NOT fire here — visiting this screen is read-only); "Open in editor" mirrors Home's `openCreate` and `film-this-now`'s `handleStartFilming` and DOES fire `selected` before navigating. Defensive `!idea` recovery state with "Back to Home" CTA. Close affordance: `router.back()` if `canGoBack()`, otherwise `router.replace("/(tabs)")` to handle the deep-linked-with-empty-stack edge case. **Wiring (`artifacts/lumina/components/TodaysPickHero.tsx`):** the kicker row (the "● Today's pick" label) became a `<Pressable>` with comfortable padding for a ~44pt tap target + a small "→" affordance. Tapping pushes `/pick-for-you` with the same JSON-encoded payload. Handler stays internal to the hero (not threaded as a prop) because navigation here is presentation-side; Home's signal accounting is byte-identical to the Z2 baseline. **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; full api-server vitest 150/150 green (Z3 is mobile-only, no server tests touched, ZERO regressions); healthz 200; expo workflow restarted to regenerate `.expo/types/router.d.ts` for the new `/pick-for-you` route. **Edge cases:** (1) Skip on multi-select steps preserves the prior contract (suppress + latch + skipped POST, no completion mark, no post-cal refresh) — Skip never persists a half-state even if the user had partial selections; (2) cap-reaching tap on the format step transitions to step 1 INSIDE the updater function (avoids a stale-closure read of `formats.length`); (3) defensive bail in `handleHookToggle` and `handleHookContinue` when `formats.length === 0 || tone === null` so a developer tool that skipped earlier steps can't persist an empty doc; (4) confirmation card render gate widened from `format && tone && hookStyle` to `formats.length > 0 && tone && hookStyles.length > 0`; (5) `step0Sub` const removed (sub-copy now rendered inline on step 0 because the multi-select wording differs from the single-select original). **Frozen scope:** ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/HTTP-API-shape/server changes; reuses `tasteCalibrationSchema`'s existing `z.array(...)` discipline for format/hook; reuses Z2's `<TodaysPickHero>` plumbing untouched aside from the kicker tap. Phases Y11-Y14, D1-D5+QA, D14-D15-alt, Z1, Z1-QA, Z2 unchanged.

- **PHASE Z2 — "Today's pick" hero treatment on Home (additive UI overlay on Z1; ZERO Claude cost, ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/HTTP-API/server changes; pure mobile presentation layer that consumes the existing Z1 sort).** Closes the Z1 visual-hierarchy gap: Z1 reordered the surfaced 3-card feed by `(pickerEligible desc, willingnessScore desc)` so `ideas[0]` is the willingness ranker's top pick, but the user just saw three same-sized cards in a flat list — the ranker did its job at the API layer but the UI never said "start with this one." Z2 promotes that first card into a dedicated hero block above an "Other ideas for today" section so the ranker's signal becomes legible. **`artifacts/lumina/components/TodaysPickHero.tsx` (NEW):** purely-presentational component accepting `{idea, onFilmNow, onOpenCreate, fitsYourStyle?}`. Renders a "Today's pick" kicker (firefly-teal bold uppercase + small solid-teal dot) above the canonical `<IdeaCard idea={idea} highlight />` (reuses the pre-existing `cardHighlight` teal-border affordance — no new card chrome), then BELOW the card a large filled-teal `Film this now →` primary button (promoted from the small outline chip the non-hero cards use because for the top-ranked idea filming should feel like the obvious next move) and a quiet `Or open in editor →` text-link secondary CTA so power users keep one-tap access to the full /create flow at a clearly subordinate visual rank. The hero NEVER wraps `<IdeaFeedback>` — that component stays mounted by Home as a sibling so verdict-pill behaviour + accessibility tree are byte-identical between hero and non-hero rendering paths. Hero passes a new `suppressKicker` prop to `IdeaCard` (NOT `index` — passing `index` would render "idea 1", which conflicts with the hero kicker just as badly as the no-index "first idea" fallback). **`IdeaCard` (MODIFIED, additive):** new optional `suppressKicker?: boolean` prop. When true, the cardKicker `<Text>` is hidden; when ALL of `suppressKicker` + no patternLabel + no `fitsYourStyle` pill are true, the entire kickerRow `<View>` is also omitted so the hook sits flush below the hero's "Today's pick" kicker (avoids an empty 10-px row + bottom margin). When patternBadge or fitsBadge still need to render, the kickerRow stays mounted to anchor them. Default false → all 76 existing IdeaCard call sites unchanged. **Hero index is NOT downgraded to "Top pick" when all three cards are `pickerEligible: false`** — the willingness ranker still chose this as the best of the batch, so it's still today's pick by construction. **`artifacts/lumina/app/(tabs)/index.tsx` (MODIFIED):** existing `ideas.map((idea, i) => …)` body refactored to special-case `i === 0` (renders `<TodaysPickHero>` + sibling `<IdeaFeedback>` + conditional `"Other ideas for today"` section header when `ideas.length > 1`) vs `i > 0` (renders the EXACT pre-Z2 layout — `Pressable → IdeaCard → IdeaFeedback → film-this-now Pressable` chip — UNCHANGED structurally so cards 2/3 keep the same tap targets and verdict pills). The hero's `onFilmNow` reuses the same `router.push("/film-this-now", …)` payload the non-hero chip uses; `onOpenCreate` reuses `openCreate(idea)` so the canonical `selected` ideator signal still fires from the same call site (signal accounting unchanged from Z1 baseline — no double-fire, no missing fire). New `otherIdeasHeading` style: quiet uppercase 11pt firefly-dim kicker matching the existing `cardLabel` rhythm so the section divider reads as visual hierarchy, not a competing headline. **Edge cases:** (1) empty/error → existing empty-state block fires unchanged (the `hasIdeas` gate above the map short-circuits before either branch runs); (2) single idea → hero renders alone with no "Other ideas" header (`ideas.length > 1` gate); (3) pre-Z1 cached batches lacking `whyThisFitsYou` → IdeaCard already hides the line conditionally, hero treatment still applies; (4) all-ineligible batch → hero treatment still applies (see above). **Validation:** `pnpm --filter @workspace/lumina exec tsc --noEmit` clean; `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; full api-server vitest 150/150 green (Z1-QA suite + everything prior; ZERO regressions — Z2 is mobile-only, no server tests touched); healthz 200; Expo workflow running. Web-preview screenshot reaches the onboarding region-picker (Home gates behind onboarding completion); the hero rendering is reached via the same `!loading && !regenerating && ideas` conditional Z1 already exercised, so the existing card-list test path covers entry into the modified branch.

- **PHASE Z1-QA — Ephemeral dev-gated willingness ranker effectiveness report (additive overlay on Z1; ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/Claude-cost/HTTP-API/UI changes; merged-and-removed harness, intended for deletion in the same cycle the Z1 measurement window closes — same discipline as D5-QA).** Closes the Z1 observation loop: Z1 reorders the surfaced 3-card feed by `(pickerEligible desc, willingnessScore desc)` but until we can see whether picker-eligible cards actually convert at higher rates and whether high-willingness cards drive more `exported` signals than low-willingness ones, there's no way to validate the ranker's design or tune the floor. **`routes/z1Qa.ts` (NEW, ephemeral):** dev-gated Express router exporting `GET /api/z1-qa/willingness-report?days=N&creatorId=<uuid>` (default `days=7`, clamped 1-90; `creatorId` optional single-creator filter). Mounted in `routes/index.ts` ONLY when `process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production"` with a defense-in-depth handler-entry re-check that 404s in production even if a misconfigured deploy mounts the router (mirrors D5-QA discipline). **ZERO-migration JOIN strategy:** `ideator_signal` is a flat table with no JSONB column, so willingnessScore/pickerEligible can't be stashed there without a schema change. Instead the route exploits the fact that `annotateAndSortByWillingness` mutates `c.idea` BEFORE `persistCache` writes the envelope at `hybridIdeator.ts:4388`, so the Z1 fields are already persisted inside `creators.lastIdeaBatchJson` (envelope `{version:2, current:CachedBatchEntry[], history:CachedBatchEntry[][]}`). Pulls all signals in window + all cache envelopes for those creators, walks each envelope to build a hook → `{willingnessScore, pickerEligible}` lookup map (history first, then current — current overwrites so most-recent-batch annotation wins), classifies every signal into one of three eligibility tiers (`eligible` / `ineligible` / `unknown`), and returns aggregate counts by `(signalType × tier)` plus median willingness per signalType for matched hooks. **Tolerant cache parser:** uses a local Zod `envelopeSchema` with `passthrough()` + `safeParse` rather than importing the strict `tryParseCachedEnvelope` from `hybridIdeator` — at the orchestrator a malformed envelope means the cache is broken and gets re-seeded, but at report time we want to extract whatever's parseable; a creator with a malformed envelope just contributes zero hooks to the lookup and their signals classify as `unknown`. Pre-Z1 cached entries (no `willingnessScore`/`pickerEligible` fields) also classify as `unknown` since the cached `idea` object lacks the optional Z1 fields. **Aggregator (`buildWillingnessReport`):** pure function over `(windowDays, signals, hookLookupByCreator)` returning `{windowDays, totalSignals, totalCreators, totalHooksMatched, totalHooksUnmatched, bySignalType: Record<string, {total, byTier, medianWillingness}>, totalsByTier}`. Median is computed from matched hooks only (unmatched hooks contribute nothing to the willingness sample). **Tests `lib/__tests__/z1QaReport.test.ts` (NEW, 8 cases):** `buildHookLookup` covers Z1 field extraction from both current+history, current-batch precedence on collisions, pre-Z1 entries surfacing as null records, and malformed-input safety; `buildWillingnessReport` covers tier classification, per-signalType median willingness from matched hooks only, multi-creator lookup isolation, and empty-input shape. **Smoke test:** harness returned HTTP 200 with real aggregate (50 signals over 7 days from one creator, all classified as `unknown` — the existing signals predate Z1's ship at commit 423d5be so their hooks have rotated past the 7-batch cache window; future signals fired against still-cached Z1-annotated batches will populate the eligible/ineligible buckets since `selected`/`exported` typically fire while the card is still in `current`). Validation: full api-server vitest 19/150 green (was 19/142 pre-Z1-QA; +8 new cases, ZERO regressions); `pnpm --filter @workspace/api-server exec tsc --noEmit` clean; healthz 200; route returns 200 on valid input, 400 on out-of-range `days`, 400 on invalid UUID, 404 in production via the handler-entry gate. **Frozen scope:** ZERO schema/migration/cache-shape/HTTP-API-shape/UI changes; reuses Z1's annotated cache as the source-of-truth for "was this idea eligible when shipped"; Phases Y11-Y14, D1-D5+QA, D14-D15-alt, Z1 unchanged. **Removal plan:** when the Z1 measurement window closes (sufficient post-Z1 signals fired against still-cached batches to read a real eligible-vs-ineligible conversion ratio), the same commit deletes `routes/z1Qa.ts`, `lib/__tests__/z1QaReport.test.ts`, and the conditional mount + import in `routes/index.ts`.

- **PHASE Z1 — Willingness ranker + "Why this fits you" trust line + Film-This-Now flow (additive presentation/ranking layer on the existing 16-candidate batch; ZERO Claude cost, ZERO schema migrations, ZERO new tables, ZERO cache-shape changes; reuses the existing `ideator_signal` table for the new `exported` action signal).** Reframes the ideator output from "best by score" to "most likely to film today" without touching any of the upstream filters that protect edge. **Server foundation (`lib/willingnessScorer.ts` NEW + `lib/whyThisFitsYou.ts` NEW):** `scoreWillingness({ idea, score, meta }) → { total: 0-100, breakdown, pickerEligible }` blends filmability (from `IdeaScore.filmability` + scene tag + shotPlan complexity), tasteFit (`IdeaScore.personalFit`), freshness (`IdeaScore.freshness`), and hookStrength (`meta.hookQualityScore`) into an additive base, then applies a MULTIPLICATIVE `edgeFactor` derived from `aiClicheScore` + contradiction signals so a high-filmability/low-edge candidate can never eclipse a sharp one with the same baseline metrics — the ranker explicitly cannot surface "safe and boring" winners. `pickerEligible = hookQualityScore >= 50 && aiClicheScore === 0` is a HARD floor: ineligible candidates STILL ship in the batch (so the user can see them) but sort behind eligible ones. `composeWhyThisFitsYou({ voiceClusterId, ideaCoreFamily?, scenarioFingerprint, hook }) → string` picks one of 4 templates × 4 voice clusters (16 shapes total) deterministically rotated by `djb2(scenarioFingerprint)` — pure deterministic, no Claude. **Schema widening (`lib/ideaGen.ts ideaSchema`):** three OPTIONAL additive fields appended (`willingnessScore` 0-100, `pickerEligible` boolean, `whyThisFitsYou` 1-280 chars). Optional so cached pre-Z1 batches still pass the orchestrator's `ideaSchema.safeParse` gate AND so the route layer doesn't need a separate response shape. **Orchestrator wiring (`lib/hybridIdeator.ts`):** new generic helper `annotateAndSortByWillingness<T extends { idea, score, meta }>(candidates)` mutates each `c.idea` with the three Z1 fields then returns a sort by `(pickerEligible desc, willingnessScore desc)`. Wired AFTER `enforceTrendCap` on the main ship path (preserves trend semantics — cap operates on `score.total`, ranker on the separate `willingnessScore` axis) so cache writes + downstream consumers (`final.map(c => c.idea)`, source-label counters) carry the annotated idea forward with zero additional plumbing. Rescue path intentionally does NOT carry willingness annotation (rescue candidates are `PatternCandidate[]` — they bypass `filterAndRescore` so they have no `IdeaScore` to feed the scorer; rescue ships are rare and mobile renders cards fine without the optional fields). New imports: `scoreWillingness` from `./willingnessScorer`, `composeWhyThisFitsYou` from `./whyThisFitsYou`, `IdeaScore` type added to existing `./ideaScorer` import. **Mobile presentation (`artifacts/lumina/components/IdeaCard.tsx`):** `IdeaCardData` widened with the three optional Z1 fields. New `whyThisFitsYou` italic line renders directly under the hook (dimmer + smaller than the hook so it reads as a quiet aside, not another headline); hidden when absent so pre-Z1 cached cards are unchanged. Server has already SORTED the array so Home renders ideas in array order — no client-side resort needed. **Mobile "Film this now" CTA (`artifacts/lumina/app/(tabs)/index.tsx`):** new secondary Pressable per card, sibling to `IdeaFeedback` (NOT inside the card pressable, so the tap target never fights the primary card → /create navigation). Routes to a new `/film-this-now` screen with the idea JSON-encoded into params (mirrors the existing /create handoff). **Film-This-Now timeline screen (`artifacts/lumina/app/film-this-now.tsx` NEW):** lightweight 0-8s shotlist view of a single idea — hook beat, "what to show" beat (falls back to `trigger`), payoff beat (`reaction` then `whyItWorks`), shotPlan bullets, caption with copy-to-clipboard button (same `expo-clipboard` pattern review.tsx uses). Beat timestamps derived from `idea.hookSeconds` + `idea.videoLengthSec` — never invented. "Start filming" CTA hands off to `/create` with the same payload so the canonical `selected` ideator signal still fires from the existing openCreate path; this screen does NOT fire its own signal (avoids double-counting). Defensive recovery state when params.idea fails to parse. **`exported` ideator signal wiring (`artifacts/lumina/app/review.tsx handleSave`):** the `exported` signal type was defined in `lib/ideatorSignal.ts` since Evolution Engine but never fired. Z1 fires it fire-and-forget on the FIRST successful gallery save per /review mount, deduped via a new `exportedSignalFiredRef = useRef<boolean>(false)` (separate from `savedUrisRef` because savedUrisRef is per-uri and a multi-clip save would otherwise fire the signal twice for the same idea). Fires from BOTH the web-QA short-circuit AND the real `MediaLibrary.saveToLibraryAsync` success branch, threading `idea.pattern / emotionalSpike / payoffType / structure / hookStyle` through so the server-side `viralPatternMemory` aggregator can credit the export to the right structure/hookStyle/spike/format buckets. Server already weights `exported` heavier than verdict taps (see `api-server/src/lib/viralPatternMemory.ts`) — this is the strongest intent signal short of `posted`. **Tests:** new vitest suites at `lib/__tests__/willingnessScorer.test.ts` (6 cases: high-edge wins over high-filmability-low-edge, pickerEligible floor enforcement, deterministic across runs, edgeFactor monotonicity, score-range guards, breakdown completeness) + `lib/__tests__/whyThisFitsYou.test.ts` (5 cases: deterministic from same fingerprint, all 4 voice clusters covered, fingerprint rotation produces variety, missing optional ideaCoreFamily handled, output within schema length bounds). Full api-server suite: 142 tests passing (was 131 pre-Z1, +11 net), tsc clean both sides, healthz 200. **Edge protection guarantees:** (1) `pickerEligible` is a hard floor — ineligible candidates can never sort first; (2) `edgeFactor` is multiplicative not additive — a sharp hook with mediocre filmability beats a polished hook with low edge by construction; (3) all upstream filters (`filterAndRescore`, `enforceTrendCap`, `validateAntiCopy`, hookQuality gates) run BEFORE willingness annotation so Z1 cannot rescue an idea those filters would have killed.

- **Phase UX2 — Low-Cringe Filming Modes (mobile-only, additive overlay on UX1; ZERO migrations, ZERO API breaking changes, ZERO validator loosening, ZERO server touch — opt-in comfort modes the user toggles inside Film-This-Now to get filming instructions adapted to face/voice/setting anxieties).** Layered on top of the UX1 `actionConversion.ts` derivation library to address the "I have a great idea but I'd feel awkward filming this" failure mode. Surface decision: comfort chips ship ONLY on Film-This-Now (NOT Home) — the spec allowed either, and Film-This-Now is where the creator is actually about to film, so the chips have the highest impact there without fighting the existing willingness ranker on the Home feed. **`artifacts/lumina/lib/actionConversion.ts` (extended, additions only — no edits to existing UX1 functions):** new exported `ComfortMode = "no_face" | "no_voice" | "text_overlay" | "bedroom_easy"` union (curated to 4 — optional "Car only" / "Hands only" intentionally NOT included because they overlap with `bedroom_easy`/`no_face` without adding new actionable instructions). New `COMFORT_MODES` iterable order const + `COMFORT_MODE_LABELS` display map. New `matchesComfortMode(idea, mode): boolean` — STRICT confidence check, returns `true` ONLY when the idea provably works in that mode. **Per-mode gates (conservative-by-default per the UX2 hard rule):** `no_face` requires `pattern !== "reaction"` AND `hasVisualAction === true` (so the no-face version isn't empty frames); `no_voice` requires `scriptLen < 50` AND `payoffType !== "punchline"|"reaction"` AND `(pattern === "contrast"|"mini_story")` AND `(payoffType === "reveal"|"transformation")` AND `caption` present AND `hasVisualAction === true`; `text_overlay` requires `caption` present AND `payoffType !== "punchline"|"reaction"` AND `pattern === "contrast"|"mini_story"`; `bedroom_easy` requires `setting === "bed"` AND `scriptLen < 100`. Each mode rationally only consults the fields that matter for THAT mode (e.g. `bedroom_easy` is literally a setting check; padding it with unrelated gates would produce false negatives). New `getComfortAdaptation(idea, mode): { mode, fits: "match"|"mismatch", tips: string[], safetyNote: string|null }` — always returns tips because the user opted in by tapping the chip; `fits` lets the UI render a teal "match" tone vs a dim "mismatch" tone. **Curated tip pools** (3 hardcoded English tips per mode — no LLM, deterministic) covering the spec's adaptation guidance verbatim: no_face → tilt phone down / over-the-shoulder / crop below chin; no_voice → bold overlay text on first frame / caption carries the punchline / ambient or trending audio; text_overlay → 1-2 sec full-screen text card / short label per beat / caption is the closing line; bedroom_easy → phone propped on pillow/nightstand / soft lamp light / one quiet take. **Safety regex (`SCREEN_CONTENT_RX`):** internal `/\b(screen|phone screen|inbox|email|message|notification|dm|text message|chat window|wallet|balance|account|bank|paystub|salary|medical|prescription|passport|driver|license|password|work email|slack|teams|zoom|gmail|whatsapp|messenger)\b/i` applied to `whatToShow + howToFilm + script + shotPlan` blob; when it matches AND the active mode has a registered `SAFETY_NOTE_BY_MODE` entry (no_face / no_voice / text_overlay — bedroom_easy has no safety note by design since the framing isn't a digital surface), the adaptation block surfaces a single-sentence safety reminder ("If you film a screen, use a demo or crop tightly. Don't show real messages, balances, IDs, work email, or anything personal you wouldn't post."). Acknowledged residual risk: regex may false-positive on benign instructional uses ("don't show your password") and false-negative on paraphrases ("log-in", "two-factor code", "SSN") — accepted for v1 since over-warning is safer than under-warning and the regex is easy to extend post-beta. **`artifacts/lumina/app/film-this-now.tsx` (extended):** new screen-local `comfortMode: ComfortMode | null` state (single-select, tap-to-toggle, tap-to-deselect, no AsyncStorage persistence — intentionally deferred until beta interviews show creators want it carried across sessions; resets naturally when navigating to a new idea since `params.idea` re-mounts the screen). New chip toggle row inserted BETWEEN `whyThisFitsYou` and the first beat so creators with face/voice anxiety see the modes BEFORE deciding "this isn't for me today." Each chip is a `Pressable` with `accessibilityRole="button"` + `accessibilityState.selected` (the conventional RN toggle-chip pattern — NOT `radio`/`radiogroup` because tap-to-deselect is not radio semantics, and `radiogroup` isn't even a documented RN accessibility role). New "ADAPTED — {MODE}" block renders right below the chip row when a mode is active: teal-tinted (`adaptBlockMatch`) when `matchesComfortMode` is true, dim-neutral (`adaptBlockMismatch` with " · less ideal fit" suffix on the kicker) when false. Body shows the curated tips list + amber-tinted safety note when present. New StyleSheet entries: `comfortRow` (flexWrap so 4 chips wrap cleanly on small iPhone viewports), `comfortChip`/`comfortChipActive`/`comfortChipPressed`/`comfortChipText`/`comfortChipTextActive` for the toggle row, `adaptBlock`/`adaptBlockMatch`/`adaptBlockMismatch`/`adaptKicker`/`adaptTip`/`adaptSafety` for the adaptation block. **Acceptance:** lumina TypeScript clean both before and after architect-review fixes; api-server untouched (no test re-run needed; backend code identical to UX1 ship); lumina app boots cleanly (1750 modules bundled, no errors). Architect review surfaced two issues — (1) `matchesComfortMode` not strict enough on `no_voice`/`text_overlay`/`bedroom_easy` (fixed in same pass: added `hasVisualAction` gate to no_voice, payoffType reject to text_overlay, scriptLen gate to bedroom_easy), (2) `accessibilityRole="radiogroup"` with `button` children was incorrect (fixed in same pass: dropped the radiogroup role, kept conventional button-with-selected-state pattern). Non-blocking nits (regex paraphrase coverage, AsyncStorage persistence) deliberately left for post-beta data.

- **Phase UX1 — Action Conversion Layer (mobile-only, additive overlay; ZERO migrations, ZERO API breaking changes, ZERO validator loosening, ZERO server touch — every signal derived purely client-side from fields the server already ships).** Shifts the product framing on Home + Film-This-Now from "Lumina gives ideas" to "Lumina helps me film this right now." All derivation lives in **`artifacts/lumina/lib/actionConversion.ts` (NEW)**, exporting `deriveActionConversion(idea) → ActionConversion` (estimatedShootSec / filmingTimeMin / difficultyLabel / embarrassmentRisk / faceRequired / voiceRequired / publicFilmingRequired / canFilmAlone / wouldFilmToday) and `deriveConfidenceLabels(idea, maxChips=3) → string[]`. **Conservative-by-default contract:** every chip is HIDDEN unless the helper is confident from the inputs — `deriveEmbarrassmentRisk` requires BOTH a private setting AND a present `emotionalSpike` to land at "low" or "medium" (private-setting-alone falls to `"unknown"` so downstream chips like "No public filming" / "Can film alone" don't render on legacy cached batches that lack `emotionalSpike`); `deriveVoiceRequired` only returns `false` for `(no script + visual payoff + contrast/mini_story pattern)` and `true` for `(meaningful script + punchline/reaction payoff)`, otherwise `"unknown"`; `deriveFaceRequired` only commits to `true` for the `reaction` pattern; `deriveCanFilmAlone` defaults `true` but flips `false` on a strict second-person regex (my friend / partner / sister / etc.). Chip priority order curated for filming relevance: difficulty ("Bedroom easy" / "Desk easy" / "Car easy" / etc. via `DIFFICULTY_LABEL_BY_SETTING`) → "No talking required" → "No face needed" → "{N}s shoot" or "~2 min to film" → "No public filming" → "Can film alone" → "Low cringe" → "Text overlay works", capped at the call-site's `maxChips`. **`IdeaCardData` widening (`components/IdeaCard.tsx`):** added optional `setting` (8-value enum mirroring server), `script`, `shotPlan`, `trigger`, `reaction`, `hasContrast`, `hasVisualAction`, `triggerCategory`, `contentType` — all already shipped by the server today (route only strips `premise` + `premiseCoreId` per `routes/ideator.ts:298-309`), so this is pure type-system disclosure of fields the wire already carries. Cached pre-UX1 batches lacking the fields no-op gracefully. **Chip strip rendering (`IdeaCard.tsx`):** new `chipRow` / `chip` / `chipText` styles (flexWrap, low-opacity background, dim border, capped at 3 chips) sit between the Caption block and the meta row; renders nothing when `deriveConfidenceLabels` returns 0. **Home non-hero CTA promotion (`app/(tabs)/index.tsx`):** the per-card "Film this now" button was a quiet outline chip in Z1 — UX1 lifts it to a filled-teal primary CTA matching `TodaysPickHero.primaryBtn` style (`filmNowPrimaryBtn` / `filmNowPrimaryBtnText` styles). The legacy `filmNowBtn` / `filmNowBtnText` styles remain in the StyleSheet for reference but have no active call sites. The card-body tap → `/create` navigation is unchanged (becomes the secondary path); IdeaFeedback verdict row stays a sibling so voting never accidentally navigates. **Film-This-Now PLAN footer (`app/film-this-now.tsx`):** new section before the "Start filming →" CTA showing two-column Time + Difficulty rows + a chip strip of up to 4 confidence labels; whole block is suppressed when no signals are derivable. **Acceptance:** lumina TypeScript clean; api-server 331/331 tests still passing (zero backend touch); lumina app boots cleanly (1755 modules bundled). Architect review surfaced one severe-conservatism violation (medium-risk firing without `emotionalSpike` evidence) — fixed in the same pass before commit.

- **Phase Z5.5 — Template Output Polish (additive overlay on Z5; ZERO migrations, ZERO API breaking changes, ZERO validator loosening; pure TS data + scoring changes in 3 files).** Fixes 6 pre-existing output-quality issues found in Z5 Post-Expansion QA. **T001 — "Shop chef eat student" fix (`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts`):** replaced `humanize(core.mechanism)` with `core.tension` in script LINE 3, premise, and whyItWorks fields — the mechanism field (`shop_chef_eat_student`) humanized to nonsense; `core.tension` contains the human-readable description. The `subs.mechanism` substitution at line 329 is INTENTIONALLY kept as `humanize(core.mechanism)` because it feeds hook template `{mechanism}` tokens where the humanized form works as an inline noun phrase. **T002 — Reaction/trigger/shotPlan diversification (`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts`):** replaced single-template reaction ("deadpan stare at {anchor}") with 10-pool rotating reactions, 6-pool rotating triggers, and 6-pool rotating shotPlan beat 3 — all use `djb2(anchorLc) % pool.length` for deterministic hash selection. **T003 — Caption tail variation (`cohesiveIdeaAuthor.ts`):** expanded caption shapes from 4 to 10 with diverse tail patterns so no single tail pattern dominates. **T004 — Cold-start skeleton similarity guard (`ideaScorer.ts`):** new `hookWordBigrams(hook)` extracts word-level bigrams, `hookBigramJaccard(a, b)` computes Jaccard similarity; `selectionPenalty` applies -5 when any already-selected hook has Jaccard >= 0.45 with the candidate — prevents near-identical hook skeletons within same batch at cold-start (no cross-batch history). Both functions exported for testing. **T005 — howToFilm desk template variation (`patternIdeator.ts`):** expanded `desk_avoidance` howToFilm from 1 template to 4 variants with djb2 hash selection. **T006 — Fallback investigation:** `regenerate: true` ALWAYS forces Claude fallback by design (`const layer1CoreAwareTriggered = regenerate` at line 3778) — 5/5 fallback in QA batches is expected behavior, not a bug. **Test coverage:** 16 new tests in `z55TemplateOutputPolish.test.ts` (210 total = 194 existing + 16 new). QA report: `.local/z55_template_output_polish_qa_report.md`.

# External Dependencies

- **Expo (React Native):** Mobile application framework.
- **Express:** Web application framework.
- **Replit Postgres:** Database hosting.
- **Drizzle ORM:** Object-Relational Mapper.
- **Clerk:** Authentication service.
- **Claude Haiku 4.5 (via Replit AI Integrations):** Large Language Model.
- **Zod:** Schema declaration and validation.
- **Orval:** OpenAPI client code generator.
- **esbuild:** JavaScript bundler.
- **pino:** Structured logging library.
